**Heavenly Penetrator Salvation Method**
The Heavenly Penetrator is a general under the Northern Emperor. The scripture states: The Heavenly Penetrator’s original form is the ninth star of the Northern Dipper, the transformed body of the Golden-Browed Lord, who subdues demons and rescues living beings without distinction of sex. All may venerate him. Always on the fifth and twenty-fifth days of the month—days when the Heavenly Penetrator Great Sage descends—prepare a bowl of pure water, a sword, an incense burner, and a table. Burn incense according to the method. White glue or a decoction of cypress may also be used. Offer cakes, fruits, and flowers as one wishes. On the Three Primordial Days, light the Seven Stars Lamp and present an altar array of flowers and fruits. When performing prohibitions, first clench the fists, close the eyes to visualize the spirit, knock the teeth together, and sound the Heavenly Drum three times. While visualizing with eyes closed, transform the five viscera and five qi into the Five Spirits: Green Dragon on the left, White Tiger on the right, Vermilion Bird in front, Dark Warrior behind, the Seven Stars within the head, and the Qilin beneath the feet. The Three Terraces take form, the Celestial Rigidity faces forward, the three demonic paths are traversed, the Subduing Demon Mudra is formed, and evil ghosts are vanquished. When invoking, first visualize the sun on the left and the moon on the right, the Northern Ultimate Great Emperor in a dark crown and feathered robes, and the Seven Stars True Sovereigns in vermilion garments with crimson sashes. Next, visualize within the Northern Dipper the Perfected Ones and Jade Maidens, the Three Primordial Generals and officers, descending from the void in response to their corporeal forms. Then visualize the Heavenly Penetrator, Great Sage of the Golden Head, eight-faced and eight-armed, fifty *zhang* in height, clad in golden armor, wielding a sword, halberd, imperial bell, and spirit seal, leading thirty thousand cavalry. Thunder Masters and Lightning Masters, immortal youths and jade maidens, their feathered banners resplendent, each brandishing a golden sword, descend from the void to stand before and behind. Only then burn incense and make the invocation. To recite the Heavenly Penetrator’s divine spell, first knock the teeth together thirty-six times, then press the Heavenly Penetrator’s Ghost-Subduing Eye, located on the second joint of the left middle finger. Having pressed it, recite the incantation:

Heavenly Penetrator, Heavenly Penetrator,
Nine Primes’ Slaying Youth.
Five Ding Commanders, Tall Blade Northern Elder.
Seven Governances, Eight Numinous Ones,
Supreme Lord’s Vast Ferocity.
Long-Fanged Giant Beast,
Grasping the Imperial Bell.
White Owl of the Three Vehicles,
Mounting the Mighty Kui Dragon.
Mighty Sword Spirit King,
Slaying evil, eradicating traces.
Purple qi rides the sky,
Cinnabar radiance blazes forth.
Devouring demons, consuming ghosts,
Body transverse, drinking the wind.
Blue tongue, green teeth,
Four-eyed Elder Nie.
Heavenly Ding Force-Soldiers,
Might of the South repelling ferocity.
Heavenly Couriers, fierce and wrathful,
Might of the North bearing blades.
Thirty thousand troops,
Guard my ninefold layers.
Expel corpses a thousand *li*,
Dispel misfortune and avert calamity.
Should any petty ghost
Dare approach to witness this,
Heavenly Great Axe,
Severing the five forms of ghosts.
Fiery Emperor’s scorching blood,
Northern Dipper’s burning bones.
Four Luminaries shatter the skeleton,
Heavenly Strategy annihilates the kind.
One stroke of the divine blade—
Ten thousand ghosts scatter in rout.

When uttering the word “slay,” recite it habitually. If one fears harming ghosts and spirits, omit the word “slay.” After ten thousand recitations, merit is accomplished. Whenever reciting this incantation, tap the teeth once for every four words as a regular rhythm—this is the discipline of cultivating the true. If reciting day and night, one need not tap the teeth for every four words. In cases of ghostly affliction, sit upright according to the method, tap the teeth once for every four words, or first tap seven times, recite three times, then tap seven more times, and earnestly state one’s heartfelt vow. The haunting ghost will then suffer darkened, rotting eyes and perish. This incantation is the Northern Emperor’s secret. If a person of this world obtains this incantation and method and practices it regularly, they may control all evils, augment spirit and qi, prolong life, avert misfortune, cross tribulations, exorcise calamities, rescue and protect living beings, and prevent unjust harm. Men and women, young and old, may all practice it. Those who cultivate and recite must wholeheartedly focus, without mixing in other methods or heterodox defenses, nor sharing the same chamber—these are all the malign spirits of the Six Heavens. To profane the numinous and upright, or to mock and deride the divine spells as mere common text, will incur the Heavenly Penetrator’s resentment, causing one to go mad, throw oneself into water or fire, suffer prolonged torment in the grave, or bring cascading misfortune upon one’s family, extending calamity to seven generations. One cannot be too cautious—do not treat true secrets lightly.

**Heavenly Penetrator’s Ghost-Pursuing Method and Talisman**
When someone comes to request a ritual master, first draw three breaths of the person’s qi, step the Dipper, and ascend to the Dipper’s mouth. Then point to the *chou* earthly branch of the Dipper, and from *wei* dispatch the command. Visualize the Dipper’s mouth covering the head, the Dipper’s handle pointing forward. Upon exiting the door, visualize a Heavenly Official! Issue the command to go forth first, then from *chen* dispatch the Heavenly Troops, and from *wu* dispatch the Earthly Troops.

Proceed thirty-six steps, then dispatch one Dipper, and summon the troops and generals of the Five Marchmounts and the Three Luminaries. Concurrently, dispatch the city gods, earth gods, bridge gods, and the deities of the five roads. Upon reaching the afflicted household’s gate, employ one Small Functionary Bureau, then use the Standing Tusk and Venom-Sealing Seal to mark the *zi-wu* Dipper.

If the ghost or spirit remains unresponsive, silently visualize the Black Sea, use the Iron Drum Seal, and envision the Terrace Press as a divine dragon. First visualize the Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water, then the city gods and earth gods, and afterward dispatch the troops and generals of the Five Marchmount Lords to search and reinforce.

When inscribing the talisman, first draw the Heavenly Rigorous *qi* and hold it over the heart, transforming the body into the majestic presence of the Heavenly Penetrator Marshal, with the *kuilong* on the left and the Six *Jia* and Six *Ding* spirits on the right, accompanied by the six great duty-attending talisman messengers. Envision the brush as a sword, the paper as an iron tablet, grind the ink, and recite the Heavenly Penetrator Mantra five times. After each recitation, draw one breath of Heavenly Rigorous *qi* and blow it into the ink. Only when the brush is exhausted is the talisman complete.

**Dispersed Form:**
Upper Prime: General Tang
Middle Prime: General Ge
Lower Prime: General Zhou
Majestic Presence: *Kuilong*
Penetrator Marshal: Iron Pillar Lock
Heavenly Penetrator Marshal: Glare of Wrath at Ghosts
Heavenly Penetrator Marshal: Long Nail Piercing Ghost Eyes
Marshal of Heavenly Troops and Horses
Thousand-Foot Venomous Dragon
Thousand-Foot Venomous Serpent
Marshal’s Crossed Sword Severing Ghost Feet
*Qian, Kan, Zhen, Gen, Xun, Li, Kun, Dui*—if you are a ghost or spirit causing misfortune and do not depart swiftly, you shall be delivered beneath my *Kuigang* to die by decree.

**Assembled Form:**
Heavenly Penetrator’s Thirty-Six Generals Talisman, Oral Formula, and Preface

During the Great Tang, on Mount Magu—so named because the immortal Magu attained Dao there—there lived a man surnamed Zheng, styled Ziyang, who burned incense and studied the Daoist canon. On this mountain, he practiced the arts of Fengdu, dwelling in its grottoes for five years. Day and night he cultivated without the slightest slackening, reciting the Heavenly Penetrator’s divine incantations without pause. One night of the Upper Prime, the sky was serene, the moon bright as day. Ziyang burned incense and made his petition, praying for the descent of true numina. As he recited as before, suddenly a book descended from heaven—white silk inscribed in black characters, radiant with several beams of light—flying into his chamber before vanishing in an instant. Ziyang sighed in wonder, unable to fathom its depths. Resolving his intent, he sat upon a flat stone, closed his eyes, and as if in slumber, beheld a divine figure clad in armor, bearing a sword, who addressed him: “I am the Messenger of the Six *Ding* of the Northern Heaven. By the Celestial Emperor’s decree, I bestow upon you thirty-six talismans of the Black Script, two characters within them forbidden for use, all recorded herein.”

The Heavenly Penetrator’s Thirty-Six Talismans are now rarely practiced. Though the texts exist in the world, most appear as thirty-six isolated characters, lacking the secret art of their assembled forms. I once received these texts along with their composite forms, distinct from those in common circulation. When applied, they manifest extraordinary efficacy, and I have thus recorded them with care.

**Heavenly Canopy**
This is the true talisman of the Heavenly Penetrator, Great Marshal of the Primordial. Envision the Five Stars descending azure *qi* to infuse the brush. Conjure the first star of the Northern Dipper to inscribe the talisman, shattering demonic shrines and restraining all fierce and violent ghosts and spirits. It subdues lingering corpse-qi, malevolent essences, and the ailments of yin-yang perversion. If inscribed with utmost sincerity, swallowed, or worn, a thousand ghosts and ten thousand specters shall be obliterated upon sight.

**Ninefold Prime Slays the Youth**
This is the talisman of the Great General of Heavenly Slaughter. Envision the sixth star of the Northern Dipper descending black *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It dispels demonic afflictions, illnesses, madness, and wandering winds. When inscribed, swallowed, or worn, it banishes evil ghosts and *wangliang*, driving them far away.

**Five *Ding* Commander**
This is the talisman of the Great Divine General of the Six *Ding*. Envision the fifth star of the Northern Dipper descending purple-black *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It can subdue malaria ghosts and the five types of epilepsy. Simply inscribe, swallow, or wear the talisman, and the ailment shall vanish at once.

**Tall Blade, Northern Elder**
This is the talisman of the Seven Primes of the Northern Dipper. Envision the seventh star of the Northern Dipper descending yellow *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. To meet with nobles or esteemed officials, inscribe and wear it; all who see you shall hold you in reverence.

**Seven Governances, Eight Numinas**
This is the talisman of the Great General of the Three Slaughters. Envision the fourth star of the Northern Dipper descending azure *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It halts the five pestilences, miasmas, and afflictions such as red eyes and headaches. Simply inscribe, swallow, or affix the talisman, and great efficacy shall be attained.

**Supreme August Expels the Malevolent**
This is the talisman of the Divine General of Supreme August Expulsion. Envision the Northern Dipper descending vermilion *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. In military formations or battles, inscribe and wear it to gain the strength of mighty soldiers and ensure victory. It commands and dispatches evil ghosts and spirits, capturing mountain essences and demonic entities.

**Long-Skulled Giant Beast**
This is the talisman of the Sea Dragon King, who captures and restrains the three essence-spirits. Envision the fourth star of the Northern Dipper descending vermilion *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It subdues tigers, wolves, snakes, insects, wasps, scorpions, and all venomous creatures that sting or bite, causing pain, pus, or blood. Simply inscribe and affix it to the afflicted area, or swallow it, and healing shall be immediate.

**Grasping the Emperor’s Bell**
This is the talisman of the Great Divine General of the Five Marchmounts. Envision the second star of the Northern Dipper descending yellow *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. Regardless of official or private matters, wearing it brings great fortune.

**White Owl, Three Vehicles**
This is the talisman of the Eight Radiant Divine Generals of the Three Thousand Great Demons. Envision the third star of the Northern Dipper descending yellow *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. The wearer shall not be harassed by evil demons; those with malicious intent shall all submit and be unable to cause harm. Instead, they shall incur misfortune, grievances shall be forever dispelled, and no trials shall befall.

**Majestic Presence: *Kuilong***
This spirit constantly serves in the presence of the Jade Emperor; it cannot be commanded in the mortal realm. If used improperly, it shall bring calamity and harm.

**Mighty Sword Divine King**
This is the talisman of the Mighty Southern Divine General. Envision the fifth star of the Northern Dipper descending azure *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It can restrain ghosts of those who died away from home and revenants. If such spirits afflict a person, simply inscribe this talisman, swallow it, or affix it, and the malevolent ghost shall flee ten *li* and conceal its form.

**Severing Evil, Erasing Traces**
This spirit constantly serves before the Jade Emperor of the Supreme August; it cannot be commanded in the mortal realm. Improper use shall invite calamity and misfortune.

**Purple *Qi* Rides the Heavens**
This is the talisman of the Divine King of the Northern Emperor’s Register. Envision the fifth star of the Northern Dipper descending white *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. To seek official rank or emolument, all matters shall be answered. If worn, it prevents nightmares, stabilizes one’s form and spirit, anchors the primordial *qi* within the body, repels evil, and ensures long-lasting good fortune.

**Cinnabar Radiance, Surging Impulse**
This is the talisman of the Great Divine General of the Dark Capital. Envision the seventh star of the Northern Dipper descending purple *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. Simply inscribe and wear it to disperse thieves, bandits, and those with malicious intent, turning them toward goodness.

**Devouring Demons, Consuming Ghosts**
This is the talisman of the Great Divine General of Black Slaughter. Envision the seventh star of the Northern Dipper descending black *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It can bind thieves, restrain ships, avert shipwrecking demons, and expel ghosts of the dead lingering in old graves, as well as malevolent spirits causing male and female omens. Inscribe and wear it to drive them far away.

**Body Transverse, Drinking the Wind**
This is the talisman of the Twenty-Four Great Divine Generals.

Envision the fifth star of the Northern Dipper descending white *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It can disperse tree spirits, stone demons, and malevolent ghosts; simply inscribe the talisman and affix it to suppress them, ensuring they dare not cause harm and all retreat in defeat.

**Green Tongue, Green Teeth**
This is the Great Divine King of the Sun and Moon. Envision the second star of the Northern Dipper descending purple *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It can avert official and private slander, all manner of calamities, and dissolve them entirely.

**Four-Eyed Old Man**
This is the Great Divine King of the Four-Eyed Old Man, commanding a million hosts. Envision the sixth star of the Northern Dipper descending red *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It can heal all manner of perverse *qi*, ghostly fetuses, abdominal masses, and *qi* of swelling, pus, and pain. Inscribe it to swallow or affix, and it will take effect immediately.

**Celestial Guardians, Mighty Warriors**
This is the Great Divine General of the Celestial Guards. Envision the sixth star of the Northern Dipper descending *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It can subdue fierce demons, perverse *qi* throughout the body, pain, and dizziness. Inscribe it to swallow or affix, and its divine efficacy will manifest at once.

**Mighty South, Subduing Evil**
This is the Great Divine General of the Mighty South of Supreme Clarity. Envision the seventh star of the Northern Dipper descending yellow *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It can subdue a hundred ghosts and inspire filial piety in men and women.

**Celestial Heralds, Fierce and Stern**
Envision the Great Divine Heralds of Heaven, their eyes blazing with wrathful glare.

**Purple Radiance of the Third Star**
Envision the third star of the Northern Dipper descending purple *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It can summon the spirits of the Five Marchmounts, capture wayward ghosts, and dispel malevolent vapors.

**Mighty North, Bearing the Blade**
This is the Mighty Northern Deity. Envision the descent from the Northern Dipper, then the *qi* of the eighth star’s Fire Chariot infusing the brush to form the talisman. It cures ailments of perverse *qi* in children; swallow or wear it to protect the body and ensure great fortune.

**Three Hundred Thousand Warriors**
These are the three hundred thousand divine generals and soldiers, all attending the Great Marshal Tianpeng. They can subdue ten thousand demons and all manner of malevolent intent. Simply inscribe and wear it to remain free from harm.

**Guardian of My Ninefold Gates**
This is the Lord of the Northern Culmen. Envision the seventh star of the Northern Dipper descending yellow *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. All spirits of temples who behold one wearing this talisman will flee. When traversing perilous voids and dangers, it is essential to wear it.

**Expelling Pestilence for a Thousand Li**
This is the Great Divine General of Supreme Mystery’s Slaying Might. Envision the red *qi* within the Northern Dipper infusing the brush to form the talisman. It can eradicate epidemics and pestilential vapors. When traveling at night, wear it to dispel terror and guard body and soul.

**Dispelling Inauspiciousness**
This is the Great Divine General of the Celestial Guards’ Officers. Envision the sixth star of the Northern Dipper descending yellow *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It can break and expel inauspicious ghosts afflicting men and women, as well as the spirits of stoves, wells, and dwellings causing misfortune. Wear or affix it, and relief will be immediate.

**Dare Any Lesser Ghost**
These are the soldiers of the Five Emperors. Envision the luminous *qi* of the moon directly infusing the brush to form the talisman, inscribing it as the *qi* flows. It can heal wounds from the bites of a hundred venomous creatures and treat sores and scabies. Simply inscribe it in a bowl of water and wash the afflicted area; the sores and scabies will heal.

**Manifesting the Form to Come**
These are the Perfected Lords of the Three Caverns and Six Palaces.

Envision the sixth star of the Northern Dipper descending yellow *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It dispels abdominal distension and fullness, ghostly *qi* and spectral fetuses, shortness of breath and pain, as well as undigested food from the past.

**The Celestial Great Axe**
These are the soldiers under the command of Marshal Tianpeng, wielding golden axes to slay all malevolent ghosts and spirits. Envision the second star of the Northern Dipper descending blue-green *qi* to infuse the brush and form the talisman. It can relieve pain in the bones and joints.

**Beheading the Ghost King’s Form**
These are the fierce and mighty generals of the Northern Emperor. Envision the luminous *qi* of the moon infusing the brush to form the talisman. It can slay ten thousand specters and a thousand spirits, as well as all malign dreams. Inscribe it, swallow or affix it, and relief will be immediate.

**Yandi’s Fiery Blood**
This is the Four Luminaries’ Lord of Flame, Yandi, arriving from the south in his chariot. Envision the *qi* of sunlight infusing the brush to form the talisman. It can heal chronic swellings and sores, infestations of worms and maggots, venomous harm from wasps and scorpions, epilepsy and demonic afflictions, burns and scalds, as well as fractures and contusions. Swallow or affix it, and relief will be immediate.

**The Northern Dipper’s Burning Bones**

**The Northern Dipper’s Burning Bones**
This is the messenger of the Northern Ultimate Great Emperor, who burns the bones of a hundred ghosts with fire. Envision the black *qi* of the Northern Dipper’s fifth star infusing the brush to form the talisman. If afflicted by curses or harmed by poison, simply inscribe, swallow, or wear the talisman, and the poison will be immediately vomited forth while curses dissipate.

**The Four Luminaries’ Shattered Bones**
This is the messenger of the Four Luminaries’ Merit Officer. Envision the blue *qi* of the Northern Dipper’s second star infusing the brush to form the talisman. It can repel locusts, rats, and other vermin. Should such calamities arise, inscribe the talisman and affix it to a bamboo pole, and the pests will vanish at once.

**Heavenly Strategist’s Annihilation of Species**
This is the mighty general Heavenly Strategist. Envision the blue *qi* of the Northern Dipper’s fifth star infusing the brush to form the talisman. It can pursue and capture spectral entities that traverse the void, as well as birds that manifest as malevolent spirits. Inscribe and deploy the talisman, and they will be instantly eradicated.

**Divine Power Descends**
This is the great general Black Slayer. Envision the red *qi* of the Northern Dipper infusing the brush to form the talisman. It repels the five weapons, ten thousand ghosts, and spirits of ancient temples. Inscribe and deploy it, and they will flee far away. If the temple’s deity submits, there will be a response; otherwise, the myriad ghosts will scatter of their own accord.

**The Myriad Ghosts Rout Themselves**
These are the thirty-six generals, who raise their halberds in unison to conquer a thousand myriad foes. Further envision the true *qi* of the Black Slayer of the Supreme Subtlety infusing the brush to form the talisman. It can subdue and restrain all manner of ghosts and spirits that refuse to submit, as well as demonic entities, causing them to scatter in defeat.

All students of the Dao who encounter this sacred scripture and true method must revere it with utmost sincerity, visualizing the true *qi* as they inscribe each character. Thus, they will attain spiritual communion and manifest profound efficacy. Practice it in secret, and do not treat it with carelessness or disdain. It must not be recklessly shown to those unworthy of the Dao, lest they grow frivolous and invite harm and misfortune.

*Tai Shang’s Secret Essentials for Assisting the State and Rescuing the People, Volume Three, Concludes.*

#1 The character originally written as 佗 (*tuo*) was likely an error for 他 (*ta*); amended according to the context.

*Tai Shang’s Secret Essentials for Assisting the State and Rescuing the People, Volume Four*
Compiled by Master Dongyou of the Yuanmiao School

*The Hidden Writ of the Upper Clarity’s Marrow Spirit*

The *Marrow Spirit Writ* was transmitted by the Tang dynasty Master Leaf of the Dao, and derives from the legacy of the Han dynasty’s Orthodox Celestial Master. Its efficacy and numinous wonders defy estimation. Formerly, nine talismans were customarily employed in transmission, while the remainder remained concealed, unseen and unheard.

In addition to the nine talismans, your servant has since obtained ten more. Reverently appending them to the present text, I have compiled a middle volume to further elucidate the fundamental principles and expand their wondrous applications. As for the regulations and statutes, they remain as in the original, and are recorded below.

**Talisman of the Fiery Bell and Valiant General**
Within this scroll, the *Gathering Form Talismans*—except for the *Yin Talisman* written in black—are all to be inscribed in vermilion.

**Dispersed Form**
The Jade Clarity Lord of the Highest Dao cleaves open the Gate of Heaven.
Square is the earth, round the heavens; follow my brush’s course:
Enter directly into the *Kui Gang* of the left *Yin*, the *Kui* of the right *Yang*, the *Kui* of the left—seven revolutions.
Tang Hong, Ge Yong, Zhou Wu.
Metal, Wood, Water, Fire, Earth—
the Perfected Lords of the Circumpolar Stars and the Constellations of the Celestial Circuit.
The Three-Foot Dragon King of the Thunderbolt, the Swift Thunder of the Great Unity,
the Flying Talisman Envoys—
hurl heaven, cast earth, mount the fiery clouds.
Mount the heavens, wield the sword, swift and fierce—
the winds and thunders above.
Spread the Heavenly Net above, lay the Earthly Snare below.
Today’s Direct Talisman:
The Heavenly Officers of the Great Clarity, the Envoys of the Three Officials,
proceed to [such-and-such] place to seize and capture the demonic ghosts.

**Gathering Form**
The Talisman of the Great Unity’s Rushing Star for Seizing Demons.

**Dispersed Form**
Metal, Wood, Water, Fire, Earth—[...] the numinous, numinous follows my brush’s course.
The Six *Jia*, the Six *Ding*, the Officers of the Three Bureaus, the Four Generals—enter.
Harness the solemn chariot of *Kui* dragons, bind them into iron pillars to stir their traces.
The Green Dragon on the left draws the *hun*-soul’s qi from [so-and-so],
The White Tiger on the right draws the *po*-soul’s qi from [so-and-so].
The Three Terraces bear me—*tsu-tsu!*

**Gathering Form**
For these two talismans to be inscribed, first observe where the Celestial Rigidity resides in the heavens, and use yellow silk. On *yang* days, write in ink; on *yang* days, write in cinnabar. Pace the stars of the heavens to gather the qi of Celestial Rigidity. With the left hand form the Seal of the Purple Tenuity, and with the right hand raise the talisman.

**Incantation:**
Celestial Rigidity of the Seven Stars, divine soldiers of the Three Heavens—
the soldiers that overturn heaven and shake earth.
Great Demon Kings of the Three Heavens, Jade Clarity’s attendants,
Flying Talisman Envoys—descend from heaven,
follow my talisman of the Supreme Perfected,
today, at this hour,
accompany this divine talisman to [so-and-so]’s household for [such-and-such] matter,
to pursue and seize demonic ghosts.
Today’s Duty Officer of the Merit Clerk, the Demon-Slaying Soldiers of the Northern Emperor,
attend me on left and right.
Use one guiding talisman to go together.

Hold the talisman and pace the Dipper from the Gate of Heaven to the Celestial *Kui*, then pace from the Earthly Door to Celestial Rigidity. Turn the body and re-enter [8A40], face [8A41], burn the talisman to ash, and knock the teeth seven times. Recite the previous incantation again. With the left hand grasp the talisman ash, and with the right hand wield the sword. Retreat three steps to stand upon the Net, then shout to the Talisman Envoys and Merit Clerks to proceed to [so-and-so]’s place without delay. Blow qi onto the sword and point it toward the desired direction, then spray water from the mouth.

This method can reach the Gate of Heaven, the Five Peaks, the Four Marshes, the Yangzi, the Yellow, the Huai, and the Ji—nowhere is it not efficacious. It may be inscribed on twelve feet of yellow silk, though this is not necessary for regular use. Whenever employed, it must be done according to the proper method. Its efficacy is great, and no other technique surpasses it—thus these two talismans are foremost.

**Mountain-Shaking Talisman**
**Dispersed Form**

This Heaven is my father,
This Earth is my mother,
Sun, Moon, and the Five Stars are my envoys.
Heavenly Officials, Earthly Officials, Water Officials—
Spring Thunder, Summer Thunder, Autumn Thunder, Winter Thunder,
Flying Winds and Rushing Stones, Great Divine Kings,
Legions of soldiers who overturn heaven and shake earth—
To the left, fire chariots rumble and crack,
To the right, fire chariots fly like swift lightning.
One stroke of the brush and mountains tremble,
Two strokes and poisonous dragons churn the sea.
Mountains quake, trees sway, the hundred valleys boil—
What dares resist or disobey? □□□□□□□

**Concentrated Form**
**Great Dragon-Locking Talisman**
**Dispersed Form**

By the decree of the Heavenly Honored One, the Supreme Emperor,
By the decree of the Jade Emperor, the Supreme Emperor,
By the flying riders of the Five Thunders,
By the Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water,
By the Lord of the Sun and the Lord of the Moon,
By the soldiers of the Three Heavens and the steps of the celestial scribes,
By the Fire Generals of the Five Heavens—
A single iron pillar, a thousand feet long,
Blazing fire, Heavenly Ding spirits guard and protect.
Should any water demon encounter this, it shall perish.
Iron platforms interlock, fierce thunder and fire chariots bind the dragon,
Command the dragon to spew water, then command it again.
Iron riders charge forth, cutting off the sea’s source—
Whoever opposes this talisman shall be rendered formless.
By the decree of the Supreme Emperor, flowing gold and fire bells,
Mighty Heavenly Ding spirits, deliver this to the Water Emperor.
How dare you not comply? Today, I emit nine streams of qi to seal all.

**Concentrated Form**

When inscribing these two talismans, stand upon the Dipper’s Net during the moon’s established phase. Then observe where the celestial yang resides, draw in qi, hold the breath, reverse the qi’s flow, press the tongue against the upper palate, and clasp the middle joint of the left hand’s middle finger without releasing. Inscribe the talisman at the Dipper’s mouth while forming the mudra with the eyes.

The incantation reads:
*Proceeding along the Supreme Clarity’s boundless Great Dao, I, the master of this method, reverently summon the Water Official, the Earth Official, the local Earth God, the Envoys of the Dao, the River Lords, and the Mountain Spirits. For [such-and-such] matter in [such-and-such] place, I solemnly command this talisman to seal the Three Rivers, to flow through the Five Seas and the boundaries of the earthly and watery realms. Should any demonic beings or portents from the water palaces arise untimely to harm the people below, I dispatch the divine generals of Dinghai, Dingchou, Jiaxu, and Jiashen, leading the soldiers who overturn heaven and shake earth, to follow this divine talisman. With a single strike, all shall be pacified, obeying my commands without fail.*

Knock the teeth twenty-four times, then inscribe the **Mountain-Shaking Talisman** with the brush.

On twelve feet of crimson silk, when inscribing this talisman, shout loudly toward the mountain—it shall tremble, and spirits and gods shall flee in haste. To suppress dragon spirits and strange anomalies, inscribe the **Dragon-Locking Talisman** in seal script on an iron plaque twelve inches long and place it upon the riverbank’s wall—nothing shall pass. If cast into a lake or deep pool, any dragon or strange being that charges against the talisman shall die.

**Supreme Clarity’s Flying Storm Seizing Spirit Talisman**
**Dispersed Form**

Invoke the **Three Terraces Mantra** as recorded in the second scroll. On a yin day of the lunar month, first inscribe the right eye; on a yang day, first inscribe the left.

**Taiqing Wangdi Decree:**
Summon the true qi of the Great Sun, the Celestial Pacifier, and the Great Demon King—let their qi enter the true qi. By the command of the Nine Heavens’ Great Marshal, Flying Immortals, Celestial Scribes, Heavenly Ding, and Mighty Warriors, seize them swiftly.

**Left Origin, Great Unity, Sun, Moon, Stars, Three Officials, Lone Guardian General:**
With one qi, tally the sword; with two qi, mark the stars. The Seven Origins of the Northern Dipper—swift as lightning, fierce as gale and thunder—charge into heaven, arraying the battle formation. The Six Jia draw their bows, the myriad stars align, capturing and binding malevolent spirits. **Well**, **Ghost**, and **Willow** follow my brush’s course; those who resist are bound, those who oppose the Dao are beheaded. The Dipper’s Rampart, vast qi, governs my body and speech—swiftly, by command!

**Concentrated Form**

When inscribing this talisman, first trace the Dipper from your own life-star, transforming into an **Upper Clarity** Dharma Master. Then, within the Dipper’s mouth, step backward to the **Gang** position. Use twelve feet of white silk, inscribed in cinnabar. Draw the **Gang qi**, visualize it entering the cinnabar brush, and pinch the first joint of the middle finger. Burn incense with blazing fire and recite the invocation:

*"I humbly invoke the Three Masters at the Three Heavenly Gates, the martial officers and the Nine Heavens’ Great Marshal, the Great Unity True Officials, the Sun and Moon’s True Realm, the Celestial Pacifier and Great Demon King, the Heavenly Ding Warriors, the Six Jia arraying their formations. Command the Five Thunder Lords to dispatch flying talismans from the clouds, swift messengers—hasten, hasten! Descend from the Heavenly Gate, surge forth from the earth, spread the celestial net above, lay the earthly snare below. Chariots of blazing thunder, winds that scour the land—follow this divine talisman to swiftly proceed to [location], to seize and capture the malevolent ghosts or demonic entities causing harm. Present them before me without delay or obstruction. Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by command!"*

Recite the mantra thrice before inscribing the talisman. Recite it once when dispatching the talisman. This talisman is employed in the same manner as the **Fire Bell Flying Swift Talisman**.

**Shangqing Inverted Sea Rain-Inducing Talisman**
*Source Lord’s Corpse traverses the Nine Rivers and Nine Streams*—[these eight characters are inscribed at the talisman’s base].

To inscribe this talisman for inducing rain, first submit a memorial to the Nine Rivers’ Water Emperors and the nearest river sources or spring caves. If the weather is naturally rainy, the yin spirits will respond of their own accord. If the weather is rainless, point toward river pools, deep ponds, or lakes, and separately state the circumstances in a petition to the Ancestral Master, the *Shangqing Great Emperor*, and the *Jade Sovereign of the Vast Heaven*, humbly beseeching a special decree to command the officials of the designated river source to await the talisman’s arrival and immediately provide relief by bestowing rain, dispersing it across the specified area with a fixed depth of [X] *chi*. *"Humbly beseech your assent to this minister’s petition for implementation."*

Additionally, file a report to the Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water; address a writ to the *Thunder, Rain, and Lightning Department*, the *Tianding* warriors, the *Rain-Dragon Kings*, the *Wind Earl*, and the *Rain Masters*. Clearly describe the circumstances in the memorial and attach an official note to the designated area, instructing all water-bearing locations to await the talisman’s arrival for verification and immediate action. Conduct a Daoist ritual for three days, or five days.

After concluding the memorials, when others have withdrawn, take one *liang* of cinnabar, grind it finely according to the day, and prepare a clean brush and an iron plate one *chi* two *cun* long and four *cun* wide. Follow the method of pacing the Dipper’s net to gather *qi*, then reverse the Dipper’s steps and stand facing the lunar station. Write in cinnabar without additions or omissions. Seal the completed talisman in yellow silk and stamp it with the *Dutian Fazu* seal, including the full official title and signature without revealing the name.

Write a separate directive, clench the *Tianding Mudra*, and recite the *Transformation Spirit Mantra*. Then summon the *Tianding* warriors: *"For [location], long deprived of rain, I have submitted a memorial. Now I designate [specific lake or pond; if others, point as needed]. Rain must descend. I hereby dispatch you to accompany this talisman to [location] and urgently coordinate with the Rain-Dragon Department to deliver rain at [specific day and hour], without delay."* After inscribing the talisman, read it aloud, issue the command, and cast it into the water. Without fail, thunder and rain will promptly spread.

No errors are permitted in the dispatch. All documents must be stamped with the *Dutian Fazu* seal.

**Shangqing Great Power Dragon-Binding Talisman**

**Shangqing Great Power Dragon-Binding Talisman**
**Dispersed Form**

The vast sky’s great cauldron seals the iron mountains of earth;
The primal root of these iron mountains submits to my stride.
Left, the *Tianding* warriors wield molten-gold fire bells to suppress and bind,
Striking down the surging chaos as the *Taiyi Yuanjun*’s sun-clarifying fire and iron chains reinforce my power.
Left, the *Wuhe Jun* of *Yuyu Heaven*; the *Laojun* strides with the *Tianding*;
Right, the *Qi Shi* rides forth.
*Qian, Kan, Gen, Zhen, Xun, Li, Kun, Dui*—inscribe the character "bind" as you recite:
*"The Celestial Officials are my envoys,
The Terrestrial Officials are my envoys,
The Aquatic Officials are my envoys,
The Nine Rivers and Nine Jiang are my envoys.

**Concentrated Form**
For this talisman, use cypress wood or an iron plaque, one foot and two inches in length. First perform the *Transformation of Spirit*, then summon the talisman’s *Guanjun* and the *Zhifu* of the Three Officials. Clearly state the matter at hand. Prepare cinnabar and a purified brush, stand at the Gate of Heaven, face the Dipper, and perform the *Step of the Net* twice in reverse. Enter the Dipper’s mouth, then begin writing the talisman while holding your breath. Once inscribed, deliver it to the *Tianding* warriors.

Clench the *Tianding Mudra* and state the matter:
*"For [specific task], I dispatch you to [location: river, lake, or pond].
Execute [task: drive away or bind] as commanded."*
After issuing the talisman, memorialize the *Zu Shi Shangqing Great Emperor* and the *Jade Sovereign of the Luminous Heaven*, affirming your actions. Submit a formal petition, clearly stating the details without error, and dispatch it to the officials of rivers and seas, as well as the *Nine Jiang Water Emperors*. Once the matter is fully explained, step the Dipper again, summon the *Tianding*, and have them carry the document to launch the talisman. Flick the mudra with your gaze.

When casting the talisman, swiftly send someone to depart, lest the thunder’s roar or the sea’s waves startle the people.

**Methods for Recognizing the Talisman’s Envoys**

**Swift-Flight Talisman Envoy**
Crowned, riding a dragon, wielding a sword in golden armor, clad in crimson robes.
Used to enter households afflicted by illness, drive away ghostly malevolence, and expel lingering corpses.

**Subduing Malevolence Talisman Envoy**
Disheveled hair, wielding a sword, clad in black armor.
Employed to enter water palaces and springs, dispel misfortune, and banish ghosts.

If affixed to a person’s *benming*, it will rouse their spirit at night.

**Dragon-Shackling Talisman Envoy**
Three-eyed, disheveled hair, silver armor, riding the *qi* of the Golden-Winged Scarlet Phoenix.
Used to shackle and sever water demons and monsters, subdue and restrain flood dragons and fish spirits.
Wherever this talisman is placed, water monsters dare not trespass.

**Mountain-Shaking Talisman Envoy**
Four-eyed, eight-armed, riding a fire dragon, borne on black clouds, accompanied by three thousand officers, generals, and soldiers.
Capable of piercing the earth and shaking mountains; even the Five Peaks may be shattered by wind and rain.
This talisman must not be used recklessly.

**Spirit-Seizing Talisman Envoy**
Disheveled hair, clad in golden armor, eyes blazing with fire, wielding a demon-slaying sword, riding fire clouds, moving swift as thunder.
Used to seize ghosts, spirits, and the essences of stone and bronze mountains, shattering them without fail.

**Yin Talisman Envoy**
Wrapped head, wielding a sword, clad in black embroidered robes.
Riding the talisman’s *po* with accompanying soldiers, it severs and banishes ghosts and monsters, annihilating them completely.

**Yang Talisman Envoy**
Wrapped head, wielding a sword, clad in purple embroidered robes.
Riding the talisman’s *hun* with accompanying soldiers, it severs all terrifying specters and nightmares, dissolving them instantly.

These two talismanic scripts are the celestial decrees, the true pledges of heaven, the numinous texts of the Three Luminaries.

**Dragon-Binding Talisman Envoy**
This talisman is the secret script of the *Taiyi Yuanjun*’s iron chains for shackling monsters.
Refer to the instructions below; this talisman must not be recklessly transmitted.

*Tai Shang Zhuguo Jiumin Zongzhen Miyao, Scroll Four Concludes*
*Tai Shang Zhuguo Jiumin Zongzhen Miyao, Scroll Five*

**Five Prisons Talismans**
From the *Esoteric Writings of the Marrow of the Hidden Book of Supreme Clarity*, compiled by Master Dongyou of the Yuanmiao Tradition

The **Five Prisons Talismans** employ the *qi* of the Five Phases—Metal, Wood, Water, Fire, and Earth—to construct prisons, restraining and seizing evil spirits, malevolent ghosts, and wicked specters. Each talisman is inscribed and the prison established according to the dominant phase of the season, enabling interrogation, expulsion, and verification of responses.

**Earth Prison Talisman**
Inscribe in cinnabar on yellow paper, first affixing it within the prison with a nail, then spreading ash.
When creating the Earth Prison Talisman, first visualize the talisman envoy: his forehead smeared with crimson, head wrapped in a black cloth, clad in vermilion robes, wielding an iron rod, descending from the void. Next, envision the brush as a yellow dragon, its mouth emitting luminous *qi* to form the talisman.
Before setting brush to paper, recite the incantation seven times, then recite the name of the Earth Star seven times.
Upon completing the talisman, recite the Earth Star’s name thrice and the "Three Bindings" seven times.

**Incantation:**
*Om □ ra bō sǒng nà yě yě dà tuó ā niè dì líng tí dì hǔ luō ěr yā tí ōm yī hǎi lóu hǎi shā shā pó hē.* Draw *qi*.

**Earth Star’s Name:** *Junzhali.*
This is the secret name of the Earth Star.

**Three Bindings.**
Recite these two characters when completing the talisman.

**Wood Prison Talisman**
Inscribe in cinnabar on blue-green paper, place within the prison, then spread ash.
When creating the Wood Prison Talisman, visualize the Year Star arriving from the east, descending and transforming into blue-green *qi*, which pours into the crown of the head. Envision yourself wearing a star-crowned headdress, clad in blue-green robes and vermilion shoes, holding a blue-green jade tablet in the left hand while inscribing the talisman with the right. Imagine the brush as a blue-green dragon, its mouth emitting luminous *qi* to form the talisman.
Before setting brush to paper, recite the incantation seven times:
- For the character "太上治书," recite: *"By the decree of the Most High Lord Lao,"* draw *qi* and blow.
- For the character "七统," recite: *"By the decree of the Seven Stars,"* draw *qi* and blow.
- For the character "煞鬼," recite: *"Heavenly Slayer, Earthly Slayer, Year Slayer, Month Slayer, Day Slayer, Hour Slayer."* Draw the *qi* of celestial rigidity and blow, each seven times.
- For "急召," recite: *"Hasten! Summon all lawless ghosts and spirits under heaven. By the blue-green numinous *qi* of the East, seize them!"* Draw *qi* and blow.

**Fire Prison Talisman**
Inscribe in ink on red paper, place within the prison, then spread ash.
When creating the Fire Prison Talisman, first visualize the true *qi* of fire from the south arriving like a silk ribbon, entering the eyes and suffusing the body, igniting flames of radiant light. Next, envision yourself as a three-headed, four-armed figure. Then, imagine the brush as a fire dragon, its mouth emitting luminous *qi* to form the talisman.
Before setting brush to paper, recite the incantation seven times, then inscribe the talisman.

**Incantation:**
*Om dīng luó tán nǎng dá luó yě yě wěi bō zhà hōng pó hē.* Draw *qi*.
Upon completing the talisman, recite: *"By the cinnabar numinous *qi* of the South, seize them!"* Seven times, draw *qi*.

**Water Prison Talisman**
Inscribe in cinnabar on black paper, place within the prison, and proceed according to the method.
When creating the Water Prison Talisman, first visualize the dark true *qi* of the north arriving like a silk ribbon, entering the ears and suffusing the body. The *qi* of mysterious light, misty and vast, suddenly transforms you into a Heavenly Soldier: left hand wielding a sword, right hand inscribing the talisman. Envision the brush as a black dragon, its mouth emitting luminous *qi* to form the talisman.
Before setting brush to paper, recite the incantation:

**Incantation:**
*"When the Morning Star appears, all ghosts hide in fear.
The Heavenly Thearch summons you—who dares conceal?
All malevolent specters, hasten to the prison and manifest!"*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by law!*

Upon completing the talisman, recite: *"By the mysterious numinous *qi* of the North, seize them!"* Seven times, draw *qi*.

**Metal Prison Talisman**
Inscribe in cinnabar on white silk, place within the prison, then proceed.
When creating the Metal Prison Talisman, first visualize the *qi* of white light arriving from the west like a silk ribbon, entering the nose and suffusing the body, radiant as moonlight. Suddenly, your form transforms into the Great White Star, crowned and clad in white. Left hand forms the "Pursuing Ghost" mudra, right hand inscribes the talisman. Envision the brush as a white dragon, its mouth emitting luminous *qi* to form the talisman.
Before setting brush to paper, recite the incantation seven times.

**Incantation:**
*"Great White, luminous and pure, captures and seizes the iniquitous.
Ghosts of improper alignment—heaven and earth reject them.
The Metal Tiger displays its might, crushing the demonic vanguard.
All hidden evils—divine officers pursue them to the end!"*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by law!*

Upon completing the talisman, recite: *"By the white numinous *qi* of the West, seize them!"* Seven times, draw *qi*.

To establish these five prisons, first place the talisman at the center, then pace the Twenty-Eight Constellations in reverse, following the *Ding* guideline as you encircle it. When raising such a prison, also inscribe this talisman, burn it, and have the afflicted person ingest it, adhering to the Five Phases’ numerical sequence: one for Water, two for Fire.

**Method for Establishing the Five Prisons**
When constructing the Five Prisons, submit memorials and documents in accordance with the *Celestial Heart* method and the *Celestial Prison* protocol, employing the same directional alignments as before.
Each prison should be circular, thirty-six inches in diameter. Place the talisman at the prison’s center, then spread fine ash atop it to a depth of two *fen*.
For the **Water Prison**, use a new, unblemished basin of three *dou* capacity, free from leaks, filled seven-tenths with pure water. Place a bright mirror above it. Inscribe a talisman for mountain spirits and wild specters in cinnabar, positioning it behind the basin’s mouth at the center. Light a long-burning lamp and float it upon the water’s surface.

The oil exhausted, replenish it. Place a ritual sword horizontally atop the basin, using a bolt of black silk—black silk gauze will also suffice. Prepare one bundle of paper money for the Five Directions, and five paper horses, suspended in midair forty-nine inches above the basin’s surface.

For the **Wood, Metal, Earth, and Fire Prisons**, simply position the mirror upon the ash, place a lamp beside it, and suspend the mirror above. Set the sword upright beside the lamp, with colored silks matching the directional hues; the rest follows the same protocol.

**Proclamation Format for Establishing the Five Prisons**
**Notice from the Northern Dipper Bureau for Expelling Evil:**
To all marshaled divine generals, chief magistrates, and attending officers:
This bureau, on the [day] of [month] at [hour], has submitted a memorial to the Celestial Court and petitioned the Eastern Peak, filing a writ with the Metropolitan City God, requesting the dispatch of divine generals, magistrates, officers, and soldiers to apprehend the malevolent spirits, ghosts, and demonic thieves plaguing the household of [name], bringing them to this prison to manifest their traces and render clear retribution. All relevant divine officers are hereby notified and charged with this duty, to facilitate their subsequent transfer.

This notice is hereby issued to all marshaled divine generals, chief magistrates, officers, and soldiers for their information and compliance.
In the year of [Tai Sui], [month], [day], [hour]
Proclamation.
Sealed by the Ritual Master [half of the name withheld].

**Diagram of the Prison Layout**
After constructing the prison, burn the talisman for summoning ghosts (as per the *Celestial Prison* protocol).

**Invocation upon Completing the Prison**
Once the prison is established, burn incense, transform into the divine form, and pace the Seven Stars of the Dipper, as previously instructed. State the purpose of the prison’s construction, execute the *Duhjian* mudra, silently summon the City God, and entreat the household’s Controller of Destiny, the Five Paths Earth Deities, and the neighboring altar and temple spirits. Clearly command the divine generals, officers, and soldiers to enforce the deadline, ensuring the malevolent ghosts are apprehended within the allotted time, brought to the prison to manifest their traces, and render clear retribution. This will facilitate their transfer; any negligence or disobedience will result in all relevant deities being reported to Mount Tai for investigation, with those complicit subjected to judgment. This decree is hereby issued for implementation.

The prison’s invocation is identical to the *Celestial Prison* incantation. The method for verifying ghostly traces within the prison follows the same protocol. If no retribution is observed after two days, resubmit the writ and urge compliance.

**Talisman for Summoning Mountain Spirits and Wild Specters**
Inscribe this talisman in cinnabar. Execute the *Xuanwu* mudra, visualizing oneself as the True Warrior, hair unbound, wielding a fire bell of samādhi and a divine sword, treading upon the tortoise and serpent. Execute the *Tianding* mudra, summoning the Celestial Ding Warriors, the Four Duty Gods, and the divine generals, visualizing them at one’s side.

First, execute the mudra, cast the Dipper, and with the Dipper’s handle pointing ahead, direct it toward the location of the spirits. Then approach the altar and recite the incantation:
*"I bear the seal of the Most High; hasten to this place. Deploy the divine qi, sever ghosts, and expel demons. Four Duty Messengers, Six Ding and Six Jia, I urgently summon you—speed to this altar. Here I stand, sword planted, awaiting you. Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by law!"*

Upon completing the incantation, visualize the Six Jia, Six Ding, Four Duty Gods, talismanic envoys, and divine soldiers fanning out to search and drive the spirits beneath the altar.

Inscribe the talisman in cinnabar.
*Disperse the forms.*

**Gold, Fire, Earth, Water, Wood—**
**Yin Dipper, the Twenty-Eight Constellations,**
**Devour demons, consume ghosts, seize all perverse ways.**
**Gather the forms.**
This talisman pursues and summons mountain spirits and wild specters.
To establish the Five Prisons, inscribe it as shown above.

**Wind-Pursuit Method**
When one encounters an ill wind on the road—an act of malevolent spirits—if it brings harm to people, execute the Dipper mudra, visualize oneself as a Heavenly Ding Warrior, and form the *Heavenly Steel Ghost-Slaying Seal*. Envision the Four Duty Gods driving and restraining the pernicious specters. Cast the Yin Dipper to ensnare them, then strike with the *Golden Blade Mudra Seal*. The wind will split in two. Cast the Yin Dipper again to cover it, and strike once more with the *Golden Blade Seal*—the wind will plummet or scatter downward, leaving traces of blood.

**Rain-Summoning Method and Talisman**
In times of drought, first perform the Offering Rite on a *ren-gui, zi-chou* day. Pace fifty-six steps with the Dipper’s handle, wielding the sword, and visualize oneself as a Heavenly Ding Warrior clad in crimson robes and vermilion shoes. Facing the current celestial stem-branch, summon the *Gongcao* spirits, then cast this talisman into a nearby river or stream—the rain will arise of itself.
Inscribe this talisman in cinnabar on an iron plaque.

**Memorial-Presentation Method**
When employing talismans to treat illness or dispel violent afflictions, one must first purify body and mind, don solemn and immaculate robes, set up the altar, and present the memorial.
Begin by swallowing the *Purification Talisman*:
When inscribing the talisman, calm the mind, face the *wang* direction, hold the breath, and tap the teeth three times. With cinnabar, draw two talismanic scripts. After completing one talisman, burn it and cast it into the bathing water to cleanse the body. Then dissolve cinnabar in a vessel of pure water, swallow it, and wash the five viscera, purging both inner and outer perverse *qi*.

Next, execute the *Three Terraces Mudra* and recite the incantation. Inscribe the *Master Builder Talisman*, following the mudra while intoning the names of the Three Terraces: *Xujing, Liuchun, Qusheng*. Then recite the incantation:
*"Heaven and Earth in motion, essence of sun and moon,
Radiance piercing the Four Seas, slaying perverse spirits.
Severing demons, dispelling illness, the body shines with light.
The divine water now made, ten thousand calamities vanish in form.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by law!"*

Upon completing the incantation, take up the brush and inscribe the talisman.
**Two *Master Builder Talismans* for Yin and Yang Days**
Inscribe in cinnabar on *gang* days.

On *rou* days, inscribe with ink.

**For the Two Talismans:**
On *yang* days, inscribe the *yang*-day talisman with cinnabar.
On *yin* days, inscribe the *yin*-day talisman with ink.
For each inscription, prepare two talismans of the corresponding day: burn one to ash, mix with pure water, and swallow; place the other on the altar for the memorial petition.
When inscribing, ensure no unauthorized persons witness the process.

**Method for Prostrating the Memorial Petition**
When presenting a memorial to Heaven, the ritual master dons the proper vestments and steps within the *Dipper’s Net* upon the altar, positioning himself at the *Dipper’s Mouth* with the memorial case before him.
First, visualize himself as the Envoy of the Demon-Quelling Court, prostrating in profound stillness. He envisions two youths wielding swords and holding seals, with the Azure Dragon, White Tiger, Vermilion Bird, and Dark Warrior stationed before, behind, left, and right. The radiance of the sun and moon illumines his eyes, the Five Stars crown his head, and the *qi* of blue, yellow, and white swirls about his body. A nine-colored halo emanates from behind his neck, penetrating both within and without, until he beholds the Supreme Lord Tang of the Upper Primordial standing before him, holding a talisman. To his left, Lord Ge of the Middle Primordial stands with a halberd; to his right, Lord Zhou of the Lower Primordial holds a staff. At the center, the Directing Attendant and Merit Clerk, with messengers to left and right, and Golden Lads and Jade Maidens attend. The officials, divine generals, and spirit marshals of the memorial’s retinue, the deities and officers of the register and ritual, and the Vajra-Powered Warriors array themselves in encircling ranks.

Next, he visualizes himself ascending in a cinnabar-jade chariot, borne upon crimson clouds from the northwest. First, he enters the realm of the *Gang* Wind, where sun and moon intertwine in brilliance, the Yellow Path stretches smooth and straight, and he passes through five-colored clouds to reach the Heavenly Gate. Traversing the Desire Realm and the Formless Realm, he crosses the Heaven of the Seed People, where seven-jeweled jade groves line the path, their branches stirred by numinous winds to produce celestial harmonies. Beyond the Yellow Path, a purple cloud forms a canopy, and in the distance, the gates of the Golden Palace appear, inscribed with *Taiqing* and *Taiji*. One hundred paces from the gates, he dismounts, leaving his guardian officers and generals behind. Only the Jade Maiden of the Decade and the Jade Lad bearing the memorial, carrying the memorial case, accompany him as he hastens forward into the palace gates.

He enters the second enclosure of the Golden Palace, inscribed *Gate of the Three Heavens of the Supreme Lord*, but does not proceed through this gate. Instead, he turns west and descends to the *Taiyuan* Capital Gate. North of the gate lies the Heavenly Pivot Court, where he beholds the Great Hall. There, he pays homage to Celestial Master Zhang of the Orthodox Unity and prostrates to present the cause of his memorial. The Celestial Master approves, then exits the hall’s eastern gate, turns north, and proceeds to the Phoenix Tower. After a brief interval, a Jade Lad in vermilion robes and black cap emerges from the gate, takes the memorial case from the hands of the memorial-bearing Jade Lad, and enters to present it before the Supreme Lord.

Next, a Leading Immortal Attendant guides the audience. The Supreme Lord wears a crown of Nine Virtues and a robe of nine-colored cloud and mist, seated upon the central dais. Two Perfected Ones stand in attendance to his left and right, with hosts of immortals in escort. The Grand Unity, clad in vermilion, stands before the Supreme Lord to review the memorial’s text, then privately conveys its intent. The Supreme Lord commands the Grand Unity to inscribe the response beneath the Jade Stairs of the *Taiqing* Palace. Upon the right steps of the Jade Hall, the memorial is entrusted to the duty officers of the day, and the ritual concludes with obeisance.

The Supreme Lord then dismisses the Celestial Master, who rejoins the officials and officers at the gate, exulting as they return to the chariot. Retracing the path of their initial procession, they arrive before the altar. The master announces the completion, rises, and bows twice.

*Tai Shang’s Secret Essentials for Assisting the State and Rescuing the People, Volume Five* concludes.
*Tai Shang’s Secret Essentials for Assisting the State and Rescuing the People, Volume Six* begins.

**Master of the Cavernous Mysteries Yuan Miaozong’s Compilation**
*Ritual Forms and Jade Regulations of the Hidden Writ’s Marrow and Numinous Texts on Ghostly Statutes, Volume Three*
**Comprising Ten Sections, Totaling One Hundred Fifteen Articles**

**Daoist Methods Section: Twenty-Seven Articles**

All ritual officers of the various practices shall conduct yang actions with yin reciprocation, their merits and demerits assessed annually in accordance with these forms. Those who suppress evil, restrain wrongdoing, relieve distress, rescue the imperiled, deliver the dead to transcendence, or grant boons to sentient beings—resolving enmities and grievances—shall be promoted in rank according to the rites. Should any collude in private bias, indulging malice and fostering villainy, the Three Officials shall be permitted to impeach them, and upon report, severe demotion or punishment shall be meted out.

All dispatches and urgent missives must be delivered immediately—such as cases of grave illness, consultations with the Courts of Hell or Celestial Bureaus, or matters concerning the extension or curtailment of fate. Next in urgency are petitions to the City Gods, with a limit of one day. Following these are appeals to the Eastern Peak to establish prisons and summon spirits, with a limit of two days. Routine documents shall not exceed three days in transmission. Any delay of half a day shall incur one hundred strokes of the rod. Delays due to private bias shall result in one year of penal servitude, with heavier offenses punished by one degree more. Those who obstruct the Dao through obstruction shall be punished according to their crime.

All divine generals, officers, and soldiers assigned by the Eastern Peak shall serve three-year terms, though one-year terms may also be permitted. Their merits, demerits, and transgressions shall be reported to their native peak for evaluation and reward or punishment. One month prior to the end of their term, replacement troops shall be dispatched in advance. Those wishing to remain in service shall petition their native peak. Failure to replace when due, or replacing when not due, shall incur one hundred strokes. Exceptions shall be made for those with just cause.

Divine generals who, upon receiving commands, delay in reporting shall incur one hundred strokes. Those who harm others for personal gain or accept bribes shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude. Celestial soldiers, generals, and officers shall have their offenses and circumstances reported for imperial review.

In all ritual matters, no changes shall be made arbitrarily to inconvenient procedures. Immediate memorials shall be submitted to await responses—such as cases where dispatched ghosts refuse to depart or talismanic envoys prove ineffectual. Violators shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude. Those not authorized as ritual officers who interfere shall be sentenced to three years.

Should dispatched spirits prove unfit for their duties, mistakenly seize the souls of the living, or cause madness or illness, they shall be exiled two thousand *li*. If such actions result in death, the punishment shall be increased by two degrees. Those who defy the law and refuse compliance shall be put to death.

All ritual officers, wherever they travel, are permitted to carry talismans and seals. In all places of their sojourn, they shall be addressed as "Acting Bureau." Should any summoned generals, officers, or soldiers disobey, they shall be sentenced to one year of penal servitude. Those who encroach upon the ranks of immortals shall have their circumstances reported for imperial review.

Should any documents be lost in transmission, the bearer shall immediately report to the Bureau of Exorcism, where the matter shall be investigated and new orders issued. A deadline shall be set for recovery; failure to comply shall incur one hundred strokes. Recovery within the deadline shall exempt the bearer from punishment.

Spirits who, upon being dispatched, disobey and fail to proceed to their assigned posts shall be exiled three thousand *li*. Repeat offenders shall be put to death.

Divine generals, officers, and soldiers who, in the course of pursuing and capturing malevolent spirits, inflict harm or accept bribes shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude. Those who conceal, shield, or allow such spirits to escape shall be punished according to the crime of the offender. Should a criminal, after being exposed and verified at the altar, suddenly die due to unrelated causes, the circumstances of the officers’ conduct shall be reported for review.

All divine generals of famous mountains and great rivers, City Gods, Earth Gods, and spirits of the third rank and above shall, upon receiving documents from the Bureau of Exorcism, verify the seals and marks, strictly safeguard the texts, and promptly report compliance. Those who treat the matter lightly shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude.

Spirits who, upon receiving dispatches from the Bureau of Exorcism, fail to depart their current location by the next day shall be sentenced to one year of penal servitude for each day of delay, with the punishment increasing by one degree for every ten days, up to a maximum of three years.

Should the Six Jia Earth Spirits or other deities conceal and fail to expel malevolent spirits after their dispatch, they shall be sentenced to three years of penal servitude. If such concealment results in death, they shall be exiled three thousand *li*. Exceptions shall be made for those detained by decree of the Celestial Bureaus.

When commoners bring matters to ritual officers, they shall not refuse to receive them, nor shall they act negligently or falsely accuse spirits of crimes. Violators shall incur one hundred strokes. Officers who, without awaiting a complaint, arbitrarily dispatch spirits for unrelated matters shall be deemed in error.

Spirits in office who engage in illicit relations with the wives of commoners shall be exiled three thousand *li*. Those whose circumstances are particularly egregious shall have their cases reported for imperial judgment. Local earth spirits who commit such offenses shall be punished by one degree more.

Spirits who, without cause, take lives or steal property from the mortal realm, refusing entreaties and resisting capture, shall be put to death. City Gods, Earth Gods, and other local deities who knowingly allow such offenses shall be punished equally. Those who fail to detect such crimes shall incur one hundred strokes.

Spirits who, upon being dispatched, fail to act immediately shall incur one hundred strokes. In urgent matters involving human life, the punishment shall be two years of penal servitude. If such delay results in death, they shall be exiled three thousand *li*. Those who, upon receiving imperial talismans, disobey and refuse to depart shall be put to death.

When locusts, droughts, floods, frost, snow, hail, or other calamities harm the people’s crops, and the local spirits fail to provide relief, the Bureau of Exorcism shall dispatch generals and officers to eradicate the affliction. Violators shall incur one hundred strokes. For disasters decreed by the Celestial Bureaus or seasonal calamities, memorials may be submitted for imperial review.

Divine generals, officers, and soldiers who are summoned but refuse, or who are not summoned but act without authorization, shall incur one hundred strokes for each offense, with the punishment increasing by one degree for every ten offenses, up to a maximum of three years of penal servitude.

When aiding the people’s suffering, should any necessary spirits prove obstructive and fail to respond to summons, they shall be exiled three thousand *li*. Those who respond but fail to cooperate in pursuit or capture shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude. Exceptions shall be made for those dispatched by the Celestial Courts on other matters.

During epidemics that cause sores, swellings, or wandering pains, the spirits governed by the Twelve-Year Cycle and the Kings’ Administrations, upon receiving dispatches from the Bureau of Exorcism, shall comply with Celestial Bureau decrees to restrain and collect the afflicting spirits, promptly reporting their actions to the upper realms. Violators shall incur one hundred strokes.

Here follows the translation:

---

All mountain, river, earth, and land spirits overseeing life and destiny, as well as city gods, upon receiving orders to search for and capture malevolent spirits, shall not delay, obstruct, or willfully release them. Should such spirits cause harm to people within their jurisdictions, they shall be sent directly to the Eastern Peak for judgment. Those in charge who fail to detect such negligence shall receive one hundred strokes.

For any city gods or local deities found to have transgressed, a full report shall be submitted to the Northern Culmen, whereupon the Three Officials shall be ordered to investigate. The Bureau of Exorcism shall then carry out the decrees.

In any region afflicted by famine or severe epidemics that harm people, livestock, or beasts, the local deities shall, upon notification, command the Year-King spirits to withdraw the poison. They shall also report the matter to the upper realms. Violators shall incur one hundred strokes.

For prisoners languishing in confinement who are innocent of their alleged crimes and truly suffer wrongful grievances, if local authorities fail to clarify the matter, the city gods and mountain spirits of the respective jurisdictions shall manifest and investigate. Once officials recognize the truth, they shall immediately render judgment. Violators shall be sentenced to one year of penal servitude. If the prisoner is indeed subject to karmic retribution, no action shall be taken.

All divine generals, celestial soldiers, and spirit officials who abandon their assigned exorcism officers shall receive one hundred strokes. In cases of urgent need, they may be temporarily borrowed from nearby spirit shrines, but the total number shall not exceed five hundred. Upon completion of their duties, they shall be rewarded and commended, and their merits shall be reported to their superiors for recognition.

Any spirits or deities who receive celestial decrees but delay execution shall, after five days, receive one hundred strokes. For every ten days of delay, the penalty shall increase by one degree, up to a maximum of three years of penal servitude. Those with justifiable reasons shall submit a report to the Celestial Courts.

**Tai Jia Gate, Two Articles**
All malevolent anomalies in forests and valleys that repeatedly harm people shall be put to death. Their subordinate spirits, if not directly involved in the offenses, shall be sent to the Eastern Peak for disposition. Those responsible for the jurisdictions where such events occur who fail to detect them shall receive one hundred strokes. Those who collude in the offenses shall be punished likewise.

All forests or trees of great size that are revered by people and enshrined but fail to bring blessings in response to prayers shall be removed. If such shrines cause no harm and are capable of bestowing blessings upon people, their merits or lack thereof shall be reported for consideration. Violators shall receive one hundred strokes.

**Tai Wu Gate, Ten Articles**
All creatures nurtured by the earth’s *qi* shall, in times of famine, be allowed to live freely upon the land. If spirits or deities, without cause, traverse the area, stir winds and rains, and thereby damage crops or endanger lives, they shall be exiled two thousand *li*. Immortal officials shall apprehend those who violate the six earthly domains and report them to the Celestial Courts.

Any spirits or deities who steal human property shall, if the amount reaches one thousand coins, be exiled two thousand *li*. For amounts less than one thousand coins, they shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude. If the stolen items are offerings dedicated to sacred sites, regardless of quantity, the offenders shall be annihilated.

Local deities who willfully allow malevolent spirits to cause harm within their jurisdictions shall be reported by the Day-Patrolling Spirit Officials. Violators shall receive one hundred strokes.

All officials responsible for documents and the suppression of demons who dispatch the Day-Functioning Spirit Officers to receive decrees shall ensure prompt delivery. Delays, damage, or defacement of documents shall incur one hundred strokes. Those who privately open or inspect sealed documents shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude. Leaks or losses of memorials shall result in exile of three thousand *li*.

Any spirits or deities who wrongfully seize human souls shall be exiled three thousand *li*. If such actions result in death, the offenders shall be put to death.

Spirits or deities who fail to respond to summons or act with disrespect and irreverence shall be sentenced to three years of penal servitude.

Spirits or deities not assigned to interact with the mortal world shall not mingle with living beings. Violators shall receive one hundred strokes. Exiled immortals of the Celestial Courts are exempt. Those who falsely assume titles to extort sacrifices shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude. If they cause serious harm, they shall be sent to the Eastern Peak for disposition. Those who resist arrest shall be put to death.

Any spirits or deities who, without cause, lurk in human dwellings, stir up malevolence, and cause harm, and do not depart after one night, shall receive one hundred strokes. For every five days of delay, the penalty shall increase by one degree, up to a maximum of two years of penal servitude. Those who defy divine commands to depart shall be put to death.

When people suffer prolonged illnesses that do not improve after ten days or a month, and dream of communicating with ghosts or demons, the local earth deities shall report the circumstances to the Eastern Peak for execution. Violators shall receive one hundred strokes.

Exorcism officials who, upon receiving celestial decrees to command mountain and river spirits to capture malevolent spirits, fail to act diligently and show disrespect shall be sentenced to one year of penal servitude.

**Zheng Yi Gate, Four Articles**
All bodies of water, regardless of size or depth, that beneficially nourish crops but do not do so in a timely manner shall be evaluated by the Nine Rivers Water Emperor for their merits or faults, with reports submitted accordingly. Violators shall receive one hundred strokes.

Dragon spirits who preside over rivers, lakes, pools, or deep waters shall be enshrined as their rightful lords. If, during great winds or rains, they roam without cause or reason and harm crops, they shall be sentenced to one year of penal servitude. Those who extort sacrifices shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude.

The Water Bureau officials who divert water, causing fields, houses, or crops to be swept away or drowned, shall be exiled three thousand *li* if the harm affects fifty households or more. If fewer than fifty households are harmed, they shall be sentenced to three years of penal servitude. During times of disaster, if anomalies occur within their jurisdiction, they shall not be held accountable but must submit a detailed report.

Dragon spirits or ghosts presiding over rivers, polluted streams, or drainage areas who deliberately obstruct boats or vehicles to extort sacrifices shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude. Those who recklessly summon wind and rain, capsizing fields and houses, and causing loss of life—one person exiled three thousand *li*, ten persons executed, and if more than ten, their forms shall be eradicated. Those who interfere with lakes or deep pools, along with their ringleaders, shall receive the same punishment. Local officials who fail to intervene shall be held equally culpable.

Hidden spirits responsible for summoning rain who, despite sharing the same compassion as the Water Lords, do not urgently relieve drought but instead withhold rain shall all be sentenced to three years of penal servitude.

**Six Articles of the Wandering Spirits Gate**
Wandering spirits with grievances against the living who have petitioned the Underworld but whose cases remain unresolved, and who then haunt households to cause strange phenomena, harm others, or seek merit as retribution—even if no lives are lost but they disturb the peace by instigating disputes against the innocent—shall be reported to the Underworld for eradication.

Wayward and malevolent spirits who manifest visibly or invisibly, set fires, spill blood, or manipulate the deceased’s family to frighten or harm the living shall be exiled three thousand *li*. If they take lives, they shall be executed.

Spirits who set fires in human dwellings or within chests and cabinets, burning property, houses, or affecting ten households shall be executed. If fewer than ten households are harmed, they shall be sentenced to three years of penal servitude and sent to Fengdu for hard labor. Local officials who knowingly allow or fail to intervene shall be exiled three thousand *li*.

Ancestral remains, ghostly apparitions, ancient artifacts, or any unnamed spirits that falsely claim affiliation with unregistered deceased persons and linger in the world shall be sentenced to one year of penal servitude. Those who exploit their perceived authority to extort sacrifices and harm the living shall be exiled two thousand *li*. Local officials who know but fail to intervene shall receive the same punishment.

Spirits who harm the living and evade capture by hiding shall be sentenced to three years of penal servitude. Those who resist arrest and engage in combat with officials or soldiers shall be executed.

Lonely, masterless, and malevolent spirits that take advantage of newly deceased persons to cling to the living and make demands shall be exiled two thousand *li*. If they take lives, their forms shall be eradicated. If the spirits are indeed deceased family members who act due to lapses in timely sacrifices, they shall be appeased with offerings and virtuous deeds, then admonished and sent away. If, after receiving offerings and blessings, they continue to harm the living, they shall be sent to Mount Tai and bound in the register of lower spirits.

**Five Articles of the State Sacrifices Gate**
Spirits of unrecognized shrines not listed in the state sacrificial canon who stir up malevolence, deceive the people, and falsely claim the power to bring fortune or misfortune shall be exiled three thousand *li*. If they cause loss of life, their forms shall be eradicated.

Spirits not listed in the sacrificial canon but who bring blessings to the people shall have their merits examined and reported for possible rewards. If they boast of their deeds, act recklessly, or cause plagues, demanding prayers and refusing to desist, they shall be sentenced to three years of penal servitude. If they cause loss of life, they shall be exiled three thousand *li*; if ten lives are lost, they shall be executed; if more than ten, their forms shall be eradicated.

Local earth gods and shrines along water and land routes, recognized as divine powers within the sacrificial canon, shall not accept improper sacrifices or be used in curses against lives. Violators shall be investigated, reported to the Three Officials for deliberation, and severely reprimanded.

Blessed spirits in the sacrificial canon who harm the people shall have their offenses reported for imperial review.

Shrines dedicated to meritorious officials or virtuous worthies that later harm the people shall be immediately dismantled. If they refuse to depart, they shall be reported to Mount Tai, along with a full account of their offenses.

**Two Articles of the Flying Memorials Gate**
Urgent flying memorials shall receive a response within two reports. Those addressed to Heaven in haste differ from reports sent to Underworld or immortal officials. If the response is delayed or errors occur in transmission, the responsible parties shall receive one hundred strokes and may resubmit, awaiting further instructions.
