If the error originates from the Demon-Quelling Bureau, no punishment shall be imposed.

Memorials of the utmost urgency shall be submitted within one day; those of secondary urgency within three days; and routine matters within seven days. All responses refer to memorials addressed to Heaven. They must be written on official stationery, sealed, and escorted across jurisdictions by local officials. Those who obstruct or delay them shall receive one hundred strokes for a one-day delay, with penalties increasing by one degree per additional day, up to a maximum of three years of penal servitude. If the delay causes significant harm, the circumstances shall be fully reported.

**Sixteen Articles of the Jade Canon**
Officials of this bureau shall wear ritual robes, star crowns, and vermilion shoes only when performing exorcisms against demonic forces. Violators shall be sentenced to one year of penal servitude. Those who, without proper ritual cause, trouble spirits or gods shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude.

Officials of this bureau, registered in the Upper Clarity Jade Records and overseeing the three realms’ malevolent forces, shall receive their orthodox talismans and registers inscribed in red and black ink on yellow silk, properly bound in scrolls. After bestowal, their masters shall instruct them in strict discipline. Secret incantations and sacred texts of the ritual tradition shall be transmitted orally and memorized; omission is forbidden. Violators shall be investigated by the Three Officials.

Ritual officers who skillfully transmit orthodox teachings to Daoist practitioners, aiding and saving the people with efficacious results, may annually submit memorials for consideration and exceptional rewards.

Those who recommend unworthy candidates or fail to recommend worthy ones shall be sentenced to one year of penal servitude. Those who transmit seals or oral instructions without prior memorial shall receive the same punishment.

Within one hundred days, the master shall self-examine. If within the prescribed period one fails to confess and report an offense, the punishment shall be the same. For those whose names have been submitted for approval, if they disobey their master’s instructions or violate ritual propriety, they shall be sentenced to one year of penal servitude. If the circumstances are particularly harmful, the master shall report the facts in full; first, the offender’s life shall be forfeit, and afterward, their nine clans shall be punished.

For Daoist practitioners who report the transmission of orthodox teachings to save the people, if their master obstructs them out of greed for wealth, they shall receive one hundred strokes of the rod. Those who recklessly bestow teachings in exchange for goods shall be sentenced to one year of penal servitude per bolt of silk, with an additional degree of punishment for every ten bolts, up to a maximum of three years; they shall also be demoted by two ranks in the ritual hierarchy. For gifts of less than one bolt, the punishment shall be one hundred strokes. Offerings of wine and food shall be treated the same.

For ritual officers who each year save twenty or more critically ill individuals, their rank shall be promoted by one degree. For those who save more than twenty, their positions shall be advanced according to the immortal ranks, their merit and conduct determining their promotion in the ritual hierarchy, which shall be reported for approval. If, upon receiving human petitions, they fail to act with due diligence or promptly provide salvation, or if they falsely promote or appoint ritual officers without justification, they shall be sentenced to one year of penal servitude.

Those who falsely claim ritual office before their names have been submitted shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude. If their names have been submitted but the response has not yet arrived, and the recommendations or investigations prove improper, a further memorial shall be submitted for reconsideration. Those who presumptuously claim master-disciple relationships before the response arrives shall each be sentenced to two years of penal servitude.

For newly appointed ritual officers of this institute, they shall practice celestial talismans, stellar seals, Big Dipper incantations, and pacing the stars, inscribing them on plates of gold, jade, fragrant wood, or metal. After completing the practice, they shall wash the inscriptions away with fragrant water and cast them into flowing waters; violators shall be sentenced to one year of penal servitude.

Those who recklessly transmit orthodox teachings to unworthy recipients for personal gain, or who accept payment but later regret and refuse to transmit, shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude. The same punishment applies if no payment is received. Those who falsely present other methods as orthodox teachings shall be sentenced to three years of penal servitude.

Those who show orthodox demon statutes to unworthy persons, or who lend or entrust them to others for transcription, thereby treating them with disrespect, or who debate them with unqualified practitioners and reveal their secrets, shall be sentenced to three years of penal servitude. Those who treat the teachings as playthings for ghosts and spirits shall be sentenced to one year. Those who deliberately cause others to use the teachings to entrap ghosts and spirits shall be sentenced to two years; if death results, they shall be exiled three thousand *li*. Those who fail to maintain proper dignity and purity while reading the texts shall be exiled two thousand *li*.

For memorials submitted to the Supreme Clarity, the documents shall be entrusted to the Direct-Day Merit Officers, who shall transmit them to the Eastern Marchmount to capture malevolent spirits. The institute’s divine generals and officers shall be dispatched to report the matter and carry out the appropriate punishments according to severity. Those who submit memorials when they should not, or fail to submit when they should, shall receive one hundred strokes of the rod.

When transmitting orthodox celestial writings, secret records, talismans, and registers to others, copies may be made, but the originals shall be stored in stone caskets within famous mountains, great rivers, grottoes, or cliffs. After ritual officers receive new edicts, talismans, or promotions, all previously bestowed documents shall be burned and cast into rivers or lakes; only the documents of their current office may be retained. If the documents are not burned, they shall be wrapped in old ritual robes and cast into rivers. Used talismans, brushes, ink, cinnabar, paper, inkstones, water, Daoist crowns, ritual robes, and all other replaced items shall be burned and cast into water, or buried in grottoes or stone chambers, with their secrets preserved by incantations; violators shall be sentenced to one year of penal servitude.

For the transmission of orthodox teachings, on the days of *jiazi*, *gengshen*, the Three Origins, the Eight Festivals, the Five Lax Days, or one’s own life-day, the recipient shall kneel to receive the sword, seal, incantations, brushes, ink, cinnabar, and ritual implements, all of which shall be consecrated and offered. Pledges, contracts, and instruments of trust, such as gold and silver, shall be melted down and sold, the proceeds used for offerings and to aid the poor; they shall not be appropriated for personal use, or the offender shall be sentenced to three years of penal servitude.

For ritual officers who pass away suddenly, if they have foretold their departure with extraordinary signs, this is a mandate from heaven, and they shall depart abruptly. If no such signs appear, the authorities shall investigate, and if the circumstances are unclear, the heir to their teachings or their kin shall promptly burn the talismans, edicts, ordination certificates, and ritual robes of their master, as well as the documents and robes of their own rank, casting the ashes into the Yangtze River for the Water Officials to convey to the underworld; violators shall be sentenced to two years of penal servitude.

For ritual officers whose merit and conduct are complete and who are summoned by heaven, their bodies shall move twice upward and thrice downward, like the motion of serpents or insects, accompanied by a sound like the wind. Their eyes shall lack divine radiance, the Celestial Pillar shall not rise, the Heavenly Drum shall not sound, and their Kidney Hall shall ache. Their spirit and *qi* shall surge from the Bubbling Spring point to the Crown Gate. They shall then gather their edicts, registers, talismans, seals, and containers in one place, don fresh ritual robes, sit upright, and leave final instructions to their heirs. Before their transformation, auspicious clouds and immortal retinues shall arrive to escort them directly to their grotto-heaven, where they shall receive immortal office and assume their duties. If their body shows signs of failing but they are unable to sustain themselves, the local earth deity shall assist their heirs in sealing the documents as described above; violators shall be exiled three thousand *li*. For grave offenses, the punishment shall be death.

**Articles 35–39:**
All orthodox demon statutes, talismans, and registers shall be stored in fragrant boxes, embroidered bags, or bamboo containers. When inspecting them, one shall enter stillness with eyes closed, establish a ritual boundary, and only then open the scrolls, reading no more than five lines at a time. They shall be kept secret and never allowed to be stolen or seen by ghosts and spirits.

For virtuous commoners who truly drive away evil and assist the upright, demonstrating merit in aiding others, their names shall be recorded and submitted, and they shall be transmitted orthodox teachings, appointed to office, and granted rank.

All ritual implements of the institute—such as swords, seals, brushes, ink, cinnabar, inkstones, crowns, shoes, and ritual water—shall not be privately used without prior submission and consecration.

For disciples seeking transmission, they shall approach their master with measured steps.

The master ascends the altar to expound the precepts, performs the rites of blood-oath and cinnabar-drinking, divides the ring and breaks the contract, swearing solemn vows. Next, he imparts the esoteric hand seals and talismanic texts, declares the true instructions, and kneeling, the disciple receives the official rank, seals, swords, and the like. The master petitions the Perfected Ones above, expelling the Three Worms from the four limbs, absolving the myriad sins of the Nine Mysteries, and reports the disciple’s conduct to the appropriate authorities, aligning with the celestial will.

All divine generals, officers, and soldiers—those dispatched by the Eastern Peak—shall, upon arriving at the institute, be received with wine, food, spirit money, and paper horses as offerings. They shall remain steadfast in their duties, prepared for summoning and use, and must not be privately employed.

When ritual officers pass by places with spirit shrines, they shall form the *Tian Ding* hand seal, sound the celestial drum, and summon the divine officials and guardian generals within their bodies to accompany them, thus displaying their majesty, so that spirits naturally submit in awe.

Ritual officers shall don their robes at dawn, harnessing the vital *qi* for their work. When submitting memorials or conducting jiao rites, they must not burn sandalwood or frankincense.

All human lifespans are ordained by Heaven, with destiny and longevity fixed. If, after the institute’s efforts to save them, the afflicted still do not recover, it is because their allotted span has ended and their karmic cycle is complete; in such cases, no further talismanic texts may be employed, for it would be in vain.

When aiding the world’s people, the documents dispatched must not be overly elaborate; only sincere and direct matters may be stated. Moreover, one must explicitly declare that the person’s life is under celestial jurisdiction, that their fate and lifespan are being contested, and that the petition does not fall within the scope of the current appeal, thus seeking a clear response.

When receiving complaints about maddened demons or malevolent spirits, the ritual officer transforms into a divine form, accepts the petition, seals it, and dispatches the spirits accordingly.

For jiao rites, memorials to the Three Clarities and the Jade Emperor may be submitted, but these must not be offered frivolously at improper times. When burning memorials, they shall first be consecrated with a pledge token and sent by the dispatched *Gong Cao* and *Zhi Fu* spirits.

When conducting jiao rites before the Three Clarities and the Jade Emperor, a single *Cai Fang* emissary may be positioned beside them; no other deities may approach the imperial seat.

When entering stillness to burn incense, perform rituals, or transcribe texts from the esoteric tradition, one must first cover the Dipper, and must not allow one’s gaze to wander.

For those who have been wronged unto death and return to cry for vengeance, they shall be suppressed with the Dipper’s cover.

When treating cattle, horses, and other livestock afflicted by pestilence, inquire after the number of losses and submit a document to the Year-Star deity to drive away the plague.

When accepting offerings of faith, assess the sincerity of the giver; the monetary value shall be divided into three parts: one for use, one for offerings, and one for alms to the poor, thus sustaining the Dao.

When establishing a prison to treat illnesses or dispatching talismanic texts, those who resist shall be seized and tried as prisoners.

For those possessed or tormented by nightmares, with depleted heart and kidney *qi*, talismans shall be swallowed or worn to suppress the affliction.

When treating children suffering from night terrors or nocturnal crying, entrust the case to the Household Deity, the Eaves Spirit, the Four Heavenly Kings, the Flying Celestials, and the Swift Spirits, using the Three Lights talisman for healing.

Ritual officers who daily save the world’s people shall use the funds for sustaining the Dao, accepting no bribes from the people. Heaven will naturally bestow blessings; if resources are lacking, memorials may be submitted, for sincerity will be met with unseen aid, and no want shall remain. If one accepts bribes, worldly support will not endure.

For households whose hearths or businesses are afflicted by malevolent hexes, employ the Three Lights talisman to dispatch spirits for treatment.

When undertaking construction or repairs, submit a document to the Year-Star deity to pacify the local Earth God and other spirits, preventing them from causing harm.

For strange anomalies residing in ponds, embankments, or dikes that cause frequent damage or untimely destruction, entrust the local Earth God to drive them away, and suppress them with the Three Lights talisman. Those who refuse to leave shall be punished and expelled according to the law.

When epidemics spread and people suffer from illness, in addition to submitting documents to the local Earth God, a petition shall be sent to the Year-Star deity to withdraw the toxic *qi*. If a memorial must be flown to Heaven, the institute’s officer shall perform the *Yu Bu* step, transform into a divine form, and silently recite the oral memorial to make it known.

For childless commoners, whether due to barrenness or poverty, first use ritual methods to repel the Three Punishments and Six Harms stars, then have them wear the register.

For those whose dwellings are inauspicious, with disharmony between yin and yang, mutual clashes, and years of hardship, bestow upon them the Orthodox Register.

When performing rituals, gauge the severity of the matter and act accordingly; do not recklessly mobilize divine generals, officers, or soldiers. When receiving and sealing petitions, dispatch them promptly, and do not implicate the spirits in wrongdoing.

When transmitting orthodox teachings, conduct a jiao rite on an auspicious day within the esoteric tradition, called the Transmission Jiao. Offer 120 portions of spirit money and paper horses as ceremonial gifts. For the Middle Sage’s position, the offerings shall be half the number. The memorialist shall comply, reporting to Heaven and Earth. After the officiating officer submits a letter of guarantee, the esoteric hand seals, talismans, official decrees, and true registers shall be conferred, and a report shall be sent to the Eastern Peak to transfer the name from the underworld’s ledgers to the celestial records. Thus, the nine generations shall be pardoned, liberated from the dark realms, and ascend to the realm of the living. The sequence of rites upon the altar shall follow the prescribed method.

When ritual officers of the Demon-Quelling Institute perform their duties, they shall be titled *Du Da*, overseeing all demonic matters across the Three Realms. The initial appointment is as Right Vice Magistrate, followed by Right Magistrate, then Left Vice Magistrate, then Left Magistrate—all of whom jointly administer the institute’s affairs. Those with exceptional merit shall ascend to the immortal ranks and be appointed as *Du Tian Da Fa Zhu*, jointly administering the institute’s affairs. Next, they may be promoted to *Jiu Tian Jin Que Da Fu* for saving twenty people within a year, or for swiftly answering prayers during famines, droughts, or floods. Further ranks include Minister of the Water Department, Minister of the Wood Department, Minister of the Earth Department, Minister of the Metal Department, and Minister of the Fire Department—each awarded based on the number of people saved annually, exceeding twenty. Those who perform exceptionally in averting great disasters shall be promoted accordingly. Finally, they may be appointed as *Zi Wei Gong Shi Ri Zhi Yuan Jun*.

Those who, by year’s end, assist the state in averting disasters and secure the peace of the realm, dispatching ghostly soldiers to secretly aid the imperial throne in achieving great tranquility, shall be promoted. Further, those who within a year drive away or eradicate locust plagues and monstrous calamities from the designated celestial regions, employing ritual methods to remove them, shall be elevated to *Jiu Tian Jin Que Yu Shi*. In the following year, should they vow to establish altars upon renowned mountains, submit petitions, and present memorials to pray for the sovereign’s longevity—with verifiable efficacy—they shall be advanced to *Jin Que Shang Xian Shi Zhong*. In another year, if they attain self-realization of their nature and essence, transcending the mundane, and guide the deluded masses to escape the Five Sufferings, personally journeying to the Southern Bureau to register their merits—ensuring sagely rulers, virtuous ministers, the salvation of their nine clans, and the benefaction of all beings—they shall be promoted to *Zi Fu Shang Xiang*, followed by *Xuan Du Da Xiang*, *Tai Xuan Shang Xiang*, *Tai Ji Shang Xiang*, and *Jin Que Shang Xiang*. In yet another year, if they fully comprehend the boundless Dao, free from attachment to written words, and through direct instruction achieve tangible results—such as quelling the harm caused by dragons in rivers, lakes, and seas, or averting landslides and floods—demonstrating true merit in benefiting the state and relieving the people while eradicating great malevolence, they shall be elevated to *Wu Ji Shang Xiang*.

From *Ri Zhi Yuan Jun* to *Wu Ji Shang Xiang*, encompassing nine ranks of promotion, one shall be conferred the *Shang Qing Jiu Deng Da Lu* before being permitted to enter this system of advancement. Other positions follow the hierarchy of the immortal officials, with the Three Primes as the foremost. For those of the *Dong Shen* rank and below, progression begins with the *Chu Xia Yuan Yi Pin Xian Guan*. Next is the *Zhi Bei Ji Qu Xie Yuan Shi Zhong Yuan Yi Pin Xian Guan*, who oversees the Northern Pole Exorcism Institute. Following is the *Shang Yuan Yi Pin Xian Guan*, who governs the Fengdu Bureau. Those who fulfill their merit and karmic fruition shall ascend in sequence, attaining the Golden Gates and standing in attendance beside the Three Pure Ones.

All officials tasked with issuing the talismans of the Three Pure Ones, the Jade Emperor, the Northern Dipper, and the Three Luminaries shall transform their spirits and submit memorials, stating their requests and declaring themselves as subjects. In accordance with the prescribed formula, the petition shall be dispatched with the prayer: "May it be as this subject has declared." Upon concluding the invocation, the talisman-bearing messenger shall be immediately dispatched, and upon its arrival, the decree shall be executed.

All ritual officers, when entering or exiting, shall constantly visualize the Six Ding, the Four Straight-Land Deities, and the Guardian Warriors following them. They shall command these spirits by ritual, ensuring no mishaps occur. When ritual officers ascend to the presence of the Supreme Emperor, exorcise pestilential spirits, or sever demonic influences, they must first don the Northern Dipper’s Three Terraces and transform into the Exorcism Institute’s Envoys. When paying homage to the Supreme Emperor, they shall ascend the Golden Hall on the first day of the new year, the Lapis Lazuli Hall in spring, the Precious Pearl Hall in summer, the Silver Hall in autumn, and the Crystal Hall in winter.

After completing their memorials to the Supreme Emperor, they shall proceed to the Celestial Pivot Institute to command the Four Heavenly Kings, the Twelve Great Deities, the Eight Vajras, the Six Ding and Six Jia, the Marshals Tian Peng and Tian You, the Fire Bell Generals, the Five Thunder and Wind-Rain Gods, and exit through the Celestial Gate. When establishing prisons, they must memorialize and report to Mount Tai, detailing the circumstances and stating: "On such-and-such a day of such-and-such a month, a celestial prison was established in such-and-such a direction." They shall memorialize the Supreme Emperor, designating it as the Five Dipper Prison.

**Eight Regulations**

All celestial talismans and registers shall be inscribed with the brush of the Six Jia and Six Ding, using the ink of the Black Emperor, the cinnabar of the Solar Numinosity, and the inkstone of the Five Dragons, strictly adhering to the transmission and empowerment methods before use. When subduing fierce ghosts and spirits, it is essential to deploy the divine generals with meticulous care, employing the left and right exorcism incantations of the Dipper’s canopy. The practitioner shall then proclaim: "I record your transgressions and pardon you, for my heart is set on saving the people."

When conducting rites to beseech blessings and avert disasters for the people, one shall first memorialize the Star Host True Lords, then sit and declare: "Disciple [Name] performs this rite to avert calamity, accumulate blessings, prolong life, and dispel misfortune, ensuring prosperity and longevity. With utmost sincerity, I prepare these offerings, humbly beseeching your divine perception and response to my devotion."

When reciting the *Shang Qing* Dipper-Stepping Incantation, upon reaching the "Celestial Rigidity" step, one shall flick the seal mudra and then point with the Celestial Rigidity Seal. If reciting incantations within talismans, one shall step the Dipper beginning with the Star of Greed and Wolf.

When offering sacrifices to the gods, one shall do so on the seasonal days of the Six Jia and other designated dates. In spring, the Six Jia days; in summer, the Six Bing days; in autumn, the Six Geng days; and in winter, the Six Gui days. Outside the gates, one shall present three portions of vegetarian fruits, dates, and fragrant tea to honor the Three Realms. The Straight Talisman and Four Straight Merit Officers shall first transform the spirit money for the local earth god, then state: "By the decree of the Jade Emperor, I assist in the transformation of heaven, aid the state, and save the people. In all talismanic rituals to sever demonic influences, cure illnesses, rescue the perilous, bestow blessings, and invoke auspiciousness, I rely on you, the messengers, to communicate with the myriad sagely hosts above and below. Today, I have prepared wine, fruits, spirit money, and horses as offerings for this rite. I humbly beseech your benevolence, manifest your majestic radiance, and bestow your divine protection."

Next, one shall pour three libations of wine, burn the spirit money, and recite the incantation.

**Oath to the Merit Officers**

"I have heard that those who cultivate the great Dao in former lives now become supreme spirits, with merit and conduct as their foremost priority and the salvation of the people as their urgent task. Thus, they manifest in the unseen and respond in the netherworld, emerging from water and entering fire, assuming myriad forms with boundless efficacy. Clad in armor, bearing drums and bells, they traverse freely without obstruction. At their presence, evil demons tremble in fear, and the afflicted find peace. I wield the orthodox Dharma to subdue demons, relying on your divine might to assist in capturing and subduing malevolent spirits, severing the roots of calamity, bestowing blessings upon the virtuous, and ensuring merit returns to the path of goodness. Today, with this sacrificial offering, I modestly repay your divine merit, slightly expressing gratitude for your toils, and reciprocating your numinous power. I deeply appreciate your strenuous efforts and humbly invite you all to feast to your fill."

**Oath to the Divine Generals**

"You shall all feast to your fill on wine and food, then compose yourselves with solemn dignity, uphold the celestial precepts, reverently execute the Emperor’s commands, wield the authority of martial prowess, and achieve the merit of pacification. With your illustrious achievements, may your resounding response be clear. I now invoke the divine generals and soldiers dispatched by the Eastern Peak, who possess hidden martial prowess, innate strategic acumen, awe-inspiring reputations, and majestic virtue. Hear my call!"

"Responding to the Eastern Peak’s command to pacify the realm, you wield the exclusive authority of punitive expeditions, striking terror—where malevolent spirits vanish in an instant, the winds and clouds shift hue, and wherever your divine halberd points, no great evil dares stand before you. You aid the state and succor the people, benefiting the times and sustaining all beings. With wholehearted devotion to the Dao, none surpass your merit. Having early received the immortal’s decree and long been sheltered by the Dao’s grace, I have presumptuously assumed the authority of a celestial officer, relying solely on the protection of the supreme deities. Above, I guard my person and preserve my life, cultivating the Dao and serving Heaven, drawing upon my innate truth to aspire to celestial rank. In the middle, I propagate the sagely transformation and manifest hidden merits, extending this numinous power to fulfill my aspirations. Below, I rescue people and benefit beings, curing illnesses and expelling evil, exterminating malevolent spirits and fostering prosperity, striving to accumulate good effects and resonant responses, making subtle virtues manifest. You shall share in these benefits; when merit is achieved, you shall together enjoy its glory. Together, we shall advance the conveniences of this world and collectively uphold the supremacy of the true Dharma. Benefit without harm, awe with just punishment. For all matters that deviate from the mean or violate harmony, harm beings or defy Heaven, execute punitive measures and carry out executions, eradicating evil and aiding the upright, thereby completing merit and overcoming malevolent power, triumphing through divine transformation over treacherous schemes. How could I, a mere mortal, withstand such trials? Who could resist? Only with your divine assistance can I uphold the great Dao. *Hasten, hasten, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances!*

To all divine generals, officers, and soldiers: by this Dharma decree, I entrust and charge you to constantly guard and uphold the true Dharma, as proclaimed in this notice to the Northern Dipper Exorcism Institute.

The divine generals, officers, and soldiers currently under the jurisdiction of the Northern Dipper Exorcism Institute have been dispatched by the Jade Emperor’s edict to this institute to protect the Dharma, propagate transformation, assist the state, succor the people, and guide all beings toward the true Dao. It is feared that you may not be aware: this institute possesses the Heavenly Seal, measuring either one inch and eight fen, two inches and one fen, three inches, or five inches square. It commands hundreds of thousands of billions of celestial soldiers. Every stroke and line of the seal’s script conceals thirty-six myriad beings. The seal’s soldiers and generals turn at my command; evil demons hear of it and their gall shatters, the sick see it and find peace. Bestowed by the Supreme Emperor, borne by mighty warriors, the seal’s soldiers—hundreds of thousands of billions—come and go like the wind, formless and traceless, infinitely transformative, hidden within the seal. Summoned, they arrive; some appear as colossal figures filling the void, heads bearing Mount Sumeru, shoulders supporting the sun and moon, hands grasping the Emperor’s bell, feet treading *kui* dragons. Others manifest as minute forms entering a speck of dust, revealing vast numinous power within a hair’s breadth, upholding the true Dharma, endlessly transforming to rescue sentient beings, never boasting of their merit. Their wondrous power and the Dao’s methods are boundless.

It is feared that the divine generals, officers, and soldiers under your command may, in ignorance of these decrees, willfully disobey and incur punishment. Do not slight this institute. Now, the celestial soldiers and generals, as well as the Eastern Peak’s soldiers and generals, are to be divided into rotating shifts, prepared for urgent summons. Upon hearing this institute’s call, you must hasten to arrive. If not on duty or unsummoned, you are to remain concealed within the Six Directions, hidden and lying low.

**Detailed Roster:**

1. Celestial soldiers, generals, and officers must always be prepared for summons. If unsummoned, they may not leave the celestial realm without authorization.
   - Southern Dipper celestial soldiers: 3,600
   - Black *Sha* divine soldiers: 50,000
   - Soldiers and generals of the Four Wheels, Orthodox First Division
   - Soldiers and generals of the Radiant Light Division
   - Celestial *Ding* deities
   - Mighty warriors
   - *Vajra* deities
   - Radiant deities
   - Flying Dragon cavalry officers: 1,000
   - Dragon-Slaying cavalry officers: 1,000
   - Dragon-Severing cavalry officers: 1,000
   - Generals assisting the Dharma: 2

2. Soldiers and generals dispatched by Mount Tai are to be divided into two shifts, alternating daily. They shall accompany the institute’s ritual officers in their comings and goings; in urgent matters, this does not apply. They may only station at this institute and must not act with negligence. The generals assisting the Dharma are to be constantly supervised.
   - Commanding general: 1
   - General assisting the Dharma: 1
   - Infantry and cavalry: unspecified number
   - Personnel arriving from the Eastern Peak Pass

The above-listed soldiers, generals, and divine officers are hereby notified. You are to carefully follow the preceding directives and comply accordingly. Any violation will not be lightly forgiven. For those who render merit, rewards and commendations shall be given, with petitions submitted to the celestial realm to bestow blessings. This is no empty declaration; let all take heed.

*Dated: [Year] [Month] [Day]*
*Sealed by [Dharma Title]*

*End of Scroll Six of the* Supreme Pervasive Essentials for Assisting the State and Rescuing the People
*Scroll Seven of the* Supreme Pervasive Essentials for Assisting the State and Rescuing the People
*Compiled by Master Dongyou of the Mysterious Dao, Yuan Miaozong*
*Preface to the Methods for Aiding the Upright and Exorcising Evil through Summoning*

The Methods of Aiding the Upright and Exorcising Evil through Summoning originate from the Orthodox Unity Dao, hence there are registers for the Three and Five Summoning Methods. The officers, generals, clerks, and soldiers are all recorded in the original texts. According to the *Golden Lock Flowing Pearls*, those who practice the summoning arts must receive the root scriptures and registers from an enlightened master. These include the Generals of the Three Origins and Five Phases, the Six Jia and Seven Stars, and the Jade Maidens’ scriptures and diagrams.

Summoning, in essence, involves the examination of ghosts and the calling of spirits. One must resolve to assist the state and pacify the realm, healing and delivering the common people. Those who receive the true methods of summoning are akin to celestial officials, comparable to the governors of great commanderies. Their sacred duties are not to be taken lightly: every hundred days, they must perform a thought-patrol, inspecting the world for malevolent spirits, ghosts, and demonic influences, ensuring they do not cause harm. Every ten days, they must engage in thought-application, visualizing the world to guard against wicked essences, demonic spirits, dragons, and ghostly entities that might bring calamity, as well as the toxic qi and turbid chaos that disrupt humanity. They must also prevent untimely winds and rains.

Beyond these duties, they must tend to their own being, ensuring their hun and po souls remain upright, their true qi constantly flowing, and their spirit luminous and vigorous—thus attaining longevity. It is further said that those who perform summoning thought-patrols traverse the ten directions of the world, delivering beings with impartiality. Whether serving the state, governing the household, or aiding individuals, their meritorious deeds resonate between Heaven and Earth, and their virtuous deeds are heard in the Jade Capital above. When their merit is complete, the Celestial Emperor dispatches immortal envoys to welcome them, elevating them to the rank of Great Immortal Perfected. Since the time of the Human Sovereign and extending to the era of Luan Ba, those who attained the Dao and practiced these methods were too numerous to record.

Yet, in this age, scholars lack true masters, and the original essence of the practice is lost. Unable to uphold the grand principles of the authentic and true, they cling to minor, fragmented techniques, often misapplying them under false names. Such superficial and incomplete practices are hardly worthy of the Dao. If one does not trace the roots and distinguish the branches, the profound mysteries of the original mechanism will remain obscured. Trivial details and peripheral knowledge, when mistaken for the core discipline, prevent scholars from delving into the profound and mastering the ultimate truths.

Thus, I have meticulously compiled the essential principles of the ancient summoning methods, placing them at the forefront, while supplementary techniques are arranged thereafter. This is to distinguish their origins and clarify their hierarchy, illuminating the fundamental and the peripheral.

**The Six Meritorious Virtues of Summoning**
The Later Sage Lord addressed the Celestial Master, saying: "These summoning methods, when applied by people, yield six kinds of merit and virtue.

First, they can heal illnesses caused by malevolent influences, capture, execute, and eradicate demonic afflictions.

Second, they can assess the celestial and earthly bureaus to determine the lifespan, wealth, and destiny of individuals.

Third, they can restrain and sever public and private grievances that cause harm.

Fourth, they can resolve life-threatening conflicts between husbands and wives, parents and children, ensuring harmony and averting disasters of metal, wood, water, and fire, allowing all to proceed without obstruction.

Fifth, they can dissolve public and private curses, vengeful ghosts, and harmful spirits, whether from the living or the dead, as well as schemes and slander, ensuring mutual safety.

Sixth, they can eliminate natural disasters—untimely winds and rains, imbalanced four qi, venomous dragons, ferocious spirits, excessive floods and droughts, and pestilential qi. Only those who practice the true celestial methods can eradicate these."

The Celestial Master was further told: "These six methods were established by the Supreme Great Dao Lord, who wove the true qi of Heaven and Earth into talismans. Comprising one thousand three hundred eighty-one ranks, they constitute the Great Summoning Method. This is the most sublime and wondrous of the Dao’s methods for delivering people and aiding beings. Those who practice it must do so without deceit or reckless application.

When a Perfected One completes three thousand merits through this method, they ascend in broad daylight, their entire household—including chickens and dogs—rising to Heaven together."

**Establishing the Altar and Visualizing the Master’s Instructions**
According to the *Orthodox Unity Summoning Ritual*: "The summoning method involves examining ghosts and calling spirits. One must set up an altar, establish the register, construct a prison, and open its gates. A rope is used to encircle the altar and prison, with four gates opened. Prohibited steps and boundary formations are then established. A fragrant offering table and bright lamps are prepared, and during the middle of the night, the Yu step is performed at the center, circling outward in a T-shape to seal the boundary and consecrate the water. Facing west, one visualizes the Three Origins Summoning Orthodox Unity Master, the Venerable Li, and the Grand Preceptor of the Register, the Venerable Li Huiju. At times, their names may be softly invoked. They appear in fluttering purple robes, adorned with crowns and swords, riding nine-colored lions. Purple clouds descend from the northwest, encircling the altar three times. One visualizes bowing three times in reverence, then declares: 'I hereby consecrate this altar.'

The master then commands the yang soldiers to join the celestial and human realms, uniting with the register soldiers within one’s body to act in concert for a specific household—whether to expel malevolent ghosts or address a particular matter. The master further commands the yin soldiers to assist the register soldiers within one’s body, entering hells, waters, or tombs to capture harmful spirits. The malevolent ghosts and thieves of the household are brought to the altar, interrogated, and their cases reported."

**Oral Petition Formula**
"I, your subordinate [Name], humbly follow the celestial statutes to perform this method. May the yang and yin masters—if the yang master is absent, visualize the original master in their stead—assist me. I form the Celestial Master’s mudra, invoking the descent of true qi into my body. Aid me in deploying soldiers and spreading qi, releasing water and igniting fire. Dispatch the Three Origins Great Generals, lions, and fierce beasts to unite with me in heart and strength, crushing the mountain, temple, or lair of the malevolent bandits, demons, or evil ghosts. Let their strongholds be shattered, burned, or washed away. Capture the demonic spirits, execute them by waist severance, and cure the illnesses, ensuring the matter is resolved. Additional details may be appended as needed."

**Summoning and Interrogation Mudra for Officials and Soldiers**

For all summoning and interrogation rites, first visualize the master before you, radiating great luminosity. From this light, soldiers emerge in countless numbers, led by the Three Origins and Three Generals, along with the Five Virtue Generals and their armies of hundreds of thousands. Alternatively, visualize the Six Jia and Twelve Divine Generals, the mighty Heavenly Soldiers, arrayed in formation around the person’s dwelling, while also stationing them to guard and defend your own gates. At each gate, deploy sixteen soldiers—eight on each side—wielding blades and spears, as in a military encampment. Once the strict commands are issued, then visualize the master and yourself leading the troops to patrol the aforementioned gates above and below. Only then seal the boundary, recite the prohibitions, and proceed with talismans and documents to summon and apprehend.

**Visualization Mudra for Healing Illness**

When visualizing the master to heal illness, from the radiant light, soldiers surge forth to encircle the seas, block the earth, traverse the heavens, and scour the prisons. Together with [the patient], they extract the three *hun* and seven *po* (or fourteen *po* for women), freeing them from the demonic realm and restoring them to the original body, so that the illness is instantly cured.

**Mudras of the Three Masters**
- The mudra of the *Third Master* is on the first joint of the left hand’s fifth finger.
- The mudra of the *Original Master* is on the third joint of the second finger.
- The mudra of the *Celestial Master* is on the second joint.

**Visualization for Summoning and Interrogation**

For all summoning and interrogation, visualize the master dispatching soldiers precisely as prescribed. Then imagine the Twenty-Eight Constellations arrayed above you. Next, the Three Generals and their officials and soldiers, along with the Three Origins, are fully prepared—the Three Origins’ soldiers and generals are complete. Then form the mudra of the Three Generals, located on the first joint of the left thumb’s center.

Once done, sit beside the altar, recite the text according to the ritual, summon the spirits and gods, interrogate the malevolent entity’s name, and issue a judgment for its capture and confinement. If the spirit is stubbornly evil, later submit a *Red Memorial* to request heavenly troops to execute the demonic entity. Thus, the illness will swiftly be cured, and the matter promptly resolved. Then express gratitude and repay the favor, offering thanks to the venerated master.

**Summoning, Visualization, Incantation, and Protective Mudra for Healing**

For the summoning ritual master, always enter a quiet chamber at dawn, wear the talismans, clasp the mudras, pace the Dipper’s steps, and exhale *qi* to form a purple cloud, first covering your own body so that ghosts and spirits cannot harm you in return. Next, when treating illness, visualize the cloud covering the patient’s dwelling on all sides, as well as the afflicted person’s body. Surround them with the Five Directions’ military formations, encircling their body and home, ensuring swift efficacy. Then form the *Capital Supervisor’s* mudra, visualize the Northern Dipper’s seven stars above the head, the Three Terraces covering the back, and the [missing character] star pointing in the appropriate direction.

**Incantation:**
*"The Supreme transmits the teachings,
The later sages propagate their flow."*

The Heavenly Master personally transmits this,
With ninety million soldiers in array.
Patrolling the ten directions,
Deploying *qi* across the Three Clarities.
No evil factions among the spirits,
No demonic essences among the ghosts.
Humans and ghosts each dwell in their place,
No strife permitted between them.
Those who bring calamity shall die,
Those who bring blessings shall live.
I know fortune and misfortune,
Discerning them clearly with a gesture.
Point left to extinguish three,
Point right to topple four.
Do not violate my Dao,
For my Dao is most serene.
Those with guilt shall not be pardoned,
Those without guilt shall find peace.
Heaven bestows this method upon me,
Commanding me to enforce its decree.
Do not defy my might,
For my might is the Seven Stars’ ferocity.
I drink your blood,
I consume your essence.
All shall be level and smooth,
My Dao does not punish.
All poisons and harms,
My Dao commands to take effect.
Swiftly, swiftly, as in the statutes and decrees!

The incantation complete, again close the *qi* and pace the Yu Steps. The left hand holds the *Dao Father*—*Father* being yang. Men hold it with the left hand. Suddenly, it rises from the hand, like a human head wearing a lotus crown, clad in purple robes, gradually ascending from the hand to the front of the heart, matching one’s own height. Then visualize the body as nine feet tall, with the Four Symbols’ soldiers and generals arrayed clearly on all sides. The right hand forms the *Ghost Eye* and *Spirit Eye* mudras, marking them with cinnabar. The left and right hands face each other before the heart. Either visualize oneself as the *Examination and Summoning* Ritual Master or as the *Examination and Summoning* Envoy. Then click the teeth thirty-six times and recite the incantation:

*"Heaven shines bright,
Earth spirits stir.
I am the master of Examination and Summoning,
Existing before heaven and earth’s beginning.
I patrol as heaven and earth’s envoy,
I stand as heaven and earth’s soldier.
Calamity and evil meet their end,
Fortune and virtue arise of themselves.
Not only do I restrain tigers and wolves,
I also command the Five Weapons.
Divine dragons dare not act divinely,
Evil ghosts dare not act demonically.
Point at mountains, and they crumble,
Point at waters, and they dry up.
Point at stones, and they roll away,
Point at sun and moon, and they shine.
Wherever I walk or sit,
A hundred thousand soldiers guard me.
Where my hand points,
Wind, fire, lightning, and radiance arise.
Swiftly, swiftly, as in the statutes and decrees!"*

**True Names of the Three Yuan Generals:**
Upper Yuan General Tang, personal name Hong.
Middle Yuan General Ge, personal name Yong.
Lower Yuan General Zhou, personal name Wu.

**True Names of the Five Virtue Generals:**
East: Green Dragon General, personal name Mengzhang.
West: White Tiger General, personal name Jianbing.
South: Vermilion Bird General, personal name Lingguang.
North: Dark Warrior General, personal name Zhiming.
Center: Curved Array General, personal name Huangting.

Whenever performing the Examination and Summoning method to save and heal living beings, purify body and mind, uphold the precepts, and accumulate virtuous deeds. Receive and wear the talismans as previously described.

When treating illnesses, have the afflicted household provide a detailed account, stating the cause of the disease, the reason for the malevolent influence, and even the patient’s age—each detail must be recounted in full. Then proceed with the ritual method to examine, treat, and heal. If the matter is of considerable gravity, construct an altar and recite the Divine Incantation of the Northern Emperor of the Purified Heaven and Earth thirty-seven times. Dispel impurity, expel miasma, and command the spirits. Invoke the Celestial Perfected, presenting the circumstances with reverence. Success hinges on sincerity, and merit is thereby accomplished.

Should ghosts, malevolent spirits, demons, or spectral apparitions be present, first employ the Northern Emperor’s Universal Heaven-Covering Method to restrain and enclose the spirits, preventing their escape. Next, establish the altar and arrange the ritual implements. Then, clasp the mudra, knock the teeth, and summon the divine generals and spirit soldiers to drive and seize the spirits. Next, use incantations to reveal the forms of the malevolent entities. Then, apply talismanic methods to expel and disperse the pernicious *qi*. Next, dispatch spirit officials to investigate the root cause of the affliction. If wicked or rebellious ghosts remain unsubdued, immediately establish a prison to confine them. Then, following the Celestial Heart method, submit memorials and petitions. Next, perform the Dipper-Raising Rite to shield and conceal the afflicted household. Finally, admonish the household deities to encamp and protect.

**Northern Emperor’s Universal Heaven-Covering Method:**
The method is numinous, moving heaven and earth, shifting stars and constellations, unlocking celestial gates, turning the earth’s axis, driving mountains and peaks, and covering spirits. My method is no ordinary method—it is the Orthodox Dao of the Three Clarities, reaching upward to the Eight Extremities and descending into the Nine Springs. To the east, it connects with Fusang; to the west, it extends to Yanni.

To the south, it reaches the Sea Gate; to the north, it extends to Fengdu. The Great Mystery’s killing qi disrupts heaven and throws earth into chaos. Ghosts above cannot descend; ghosts below cannot ascend. Above, I unfurl the Celestial Net; below, I spread the Earthly Web. Heavenly ghosts are forbidden from descending to the mortal realm; earthly ghosts are forbidden from revealing their forms. Patrolling the four worlds, all wicked ghosts lie within my covering. I reverently summon the Three-Five Generals, the Five Lakes Generals, the Three Origins Generals, the Huoluo Generals, the officers and soldiers under the Three Masters, the officers and soldiers within the Northern Dipper’s *Kui*, the river officials’ officers and soldiers, the thunder and lightning officers and soldiers, the Southern Dipper’s Ghost-Slaying Envoys, the Northern Dipper’s Blazing Furnace Envoys, the Celestial Couriers’ armored troops, and the ten-thousand-zhang-high striking might of the awe-inspiring sword. The great drum’s mighty warriors, five-eyed and three-eyed, the six-armed Celestial *Ding*, with bronze fangs and iron claws, lightning eyes and six pupils, nine heads and eight horns, crimson hair and indigo bodies, clad in golden spears and silver armor, fill the empty void. Azure Dragon and White Tiger, Vermilion Bird and Victorious Serpent, fierce and colossal beasts, flying owls and hooked ropes. Heavenly Peng and Huoluo, the mighty Flying Heavenly Demon Kings, the Five Directions’ Vajras, the Five Directions’ Warriors, the Five Directions’ officers and soldiers, the Five Directions’ *yakṣas*, the Five Dippers’ encampments, and the clouds converging from the eight directions. The Five Lakes and Seven Marshes, the Five Peaks and Seven Temples, the twenty-four *zhi*’s pits, hollows, caves, and grottoes—all array their ranks, deploying troops step by step. The mountains, forests, and trees are searched meticulously. What spirit does not submit beneath my covering? What ghost does not lie within my net? Those who comply with me will prosper; those who defy me will perish. The merciful shall live; the malevolent shall die. Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the law of the Great Yin and the Northern Emperor’s decree!

When practicing this method, first visualize the fire of the heart blazing around the body, refining form and spirit. Then imagine oneself as the Summoning Envoy, with awe-inspiring divine majesty, roaring like thunder. Stand facing south, form the Celestial Net and Earthly Web mudra with both hands, and exhale qi like a thunderclap. Immediately recite the preceding incantation, then inhale qi and blow it into the mudra, casting it toward the place where the ritual is performed. Pray thus:
*Qi transforms into iron; the net is like black clouds. Dark mist envelops heaven and earth, covering the direction of the wicked ghosts.*

For the Celestial Net and Earthly Web mudra: with the left hand, join the third, fourth, and fifth fingers; with the right hand, join the third, fourth, and fifth fingers. The right thumb presses into the left thumbnail’s base, while the left and right index fingers extend. After reciting the incantation, interlock the index fingers and cast the mudra toward the afflicted household. Then proceed with all ritual methods and prohibitions.

**Method for Revealing Ghosts’ Forms:**
First, have the afflicted person stand at the threshold, eyes closed for a moment. Then, the ritual master takes a mirror in the right hand and, with the left eye, visualizes inscribing a talisman within it. Once done, place the mirror on the table, form the Lion Seal with both hands, and press it over the talisman on the mirror’s surface. The ritual master then holds the mirror before their heart, aligning it properly. Recite the incantation:
*Heavenly spirits and earthly deities, all numinous beings converge. By the decree of the United Brightness Celestial Emperor, I reverently summon the swift envoys from the eight directions to pursue and capture the malevolent ghost, forcing it to reveal its form.*

Then call the names of the spirits:
*Om, judge the malevolent! Om, judge the malevolent! Judge and seize! Judge and seize! Take and judge! Take and judge! Śrī! Śrī! Hūrū! Hūrū!*
*Seize the ghost! Seize the ghost! Seize swiftly! Seize swiftly! Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the law!*

Reverently summon the local Day-Patrolling Envoy to pursue and capture the ghost. Reverently summon the local Earth God to pursue and capture the ghost. Reverently summon the local Five Paths Envoy to pursue and capture the ghost.

After reciting, face north and shine the mirror once, then recite the incantation again, shining it a second time. Repeat this three times. Once the incantation is complete, have the afflicted person blow qi into the mirror and open their eyes to see within it: whether the affliction is a ghost, spirit, or demon; a deceased family member; or an external ghost—all will be clearly revealed.

**Visualize the talisman and incantation within the mirror:**
*Celestial August, Earthly August, Human August, Celestial-Human August, Earthly-Human August, Human-Human August. Om, Emperor Sovereign, summon the local Earth God and warrior to capture!*
*Heaven is yang; earth is yin—ghosts and spirits have nowhere to hide. The Azure Dragon General on the left slays ghosts; the White Tiger General on the right slays ghosts. The Celestial* Ding *pins ghosts; the Earthly* Ding *pins ghosts. Crowned with a floral canopy, treading upon the* Kui *and Gang. Qian, Kan, Gen, Zhen, Xun, Li, Kun, Dui. Yellow-Headed General, Red-Headed General, Azure-Headed General, Yakṣa General, Candana General, Fire-Wheel General, Fire-Head General, Great Might Celestial* Ding *General, Boundless and Unfathomable Perfected Sovereign, Southern Fire Star Perfected Sovereign, Myriad-Responding Crimson Emperor Perfected Sovereign, Fire-Wheel Emperor, Fire-Chariot Emperor, Fire-Wheel Emperor.*

The talisman within the mirror gathers punishments; inscribe it in cinnabar.

**For this method, purify the body and visualize transforming into the Northern Yin Spirit.**
The Yin Spirit is the Mysterious Woman of the Nine Heavens. Hold the bright mirror in the right hand, press the first joint of the left index finger with the left hand, and visualize the mirror emitting a five-colored radiance, illuminating every direction without exception. Proceed step by step to summon and capture the malevolent ghosts and spirits, allowing none to escape, all appearing before the ritual mirror.

**Water Reflection Method:**
*Water Official slays ghosts; Earth Official slays ghosts; Heaven Official slays ghosts. Encounter water, water subdues; encounter earth, earth subdues; encounter heaven, heaven subdues. All waters cease flowing; slay the lawless ghosts and send them beneath the Southern Mountain’s foothills to receive death. Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the law!*

For this method, write the characters for "mountain" and "water" in the air with the right middle finger, then recite the preceding incantation, transforming the words into a spell. With the right hand, scoop from the air into a basin of pure water. Have the afflicted person blow qi into the water. Recite the incantation:
*By the duty officer, the Day Clerk Envoy, and the Twelve Hour Spirits, swiftly summon the local Earth God and the domain’s proper deities to pursue and capture the malevolent ghost afflicting this person, forcing it to reveal its form swiftly!*

Summon and command.

Upon reciting the incantation, have the afflicted person blow qi into the water once more. Whatever ghost or specter appears must be clearly and truthfully described, with no concealment allowed. I enact the Great Highest’s method, duty-bound to subdue ghosts and save the afflicted. Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the law!

**Method for Revealing Ghosts in Darkness**
Reverently invoke the celestial perfected, the celestial cavern’s Six Jia Yang spirits, the Six Jia Yin spirits, the Four Duty Envoys, and the Soul-Driving Envoys. Urgently compel the vengeful ghost’s qi to manifest its form. Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the law, summon and command.

First, have the afflicted person lower their head and close their eyes. Recite the preceding incantation once and blow onto the crown of their head. Then guide qi to a dark place, blowing three breaths into it. Have the afflicted person gaze into the darkness to identify the possessing spirit. If the spirit attempts to enter the afflicted’s body, recite the incantation again, omitting the phrase "manifest in darkness" and instead saying, "Urgently drive the vengeful ghost to swiftly enter the patient, borrowing their mouth to communicate." The possessing spirit will immediately enter the body and speak.

**Method for Binding Ghosts**
Reverently invoke the Upper Clarity’s Three Heavenly Valiants and the Eight Slayer Generals. Urgently assist me in binding the malevolent ghost to prevent its escape. Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the law.

For this method, face north and center the mind. With the left hand, press the second finger onto the *yin* position of the *dou* diagram. Recite the incantation, inhale qi three times, and blow onto the afflicted’s body—the ghost will be bound of its own accord.

**Method for the Twelve Spirit Generals to Capture, Shackle, and Interrogate Ghosts**
Reverently invoke the Divine Generals Dengming, Hekui, Congkui, Chuansong, Xiaoji, Shengxian, Taiyi, Tiangang, Taichong, Gongcao, Daji, and Houshen.

For this method, transform into the Celestial One, the Noble Spirit, donning the Northern Dipper’s three-tiered crown. Stand facing west, feet aligned with the *ding* trigram. With the left hand, begin at the *hai* position, encircle to *zi* to form the mudra. Summon the spirit generals, commanding: "Urgently pursue and capture the ghost afflicting this person’s body, whether it be a temple spirit, earth god, kitchen deity, household spirit, violently deceased specter, malevolent wraith, or demonic entity—any that have harmed the patient. Gather them all without exception and attach them to the afflicted’s body to receive my true method. Interrogate them to reveal their origins, names, and deeds. Whether distant in the six directions and eight wilds or near at hand within the household, they must be pursued and brought forth without fail." Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the law.

This method is performed on a *liu jia* day at the *hai* hour. Hold a ritual offering beneath the stars, using a bolt of blue cloth sewn into a square purification cloth. Place it atop a clean mat, with offerings of seasonal flowers, pure fruits, jujube broth, clear wine, and thirteen sets of lamps and incense. Present the written petition and make the offering. From the *hai* hour through the *xu* hour—one full day and night—read the petition aloud, praying and expressing the intent to commune with spirits to heal the afflicted. Around the ritual space, sprinkle water boiled with *mao* incense for purification, ensuring no outsiders or animals disturb it. After the ritual, consume the offerings yourself; discard the remainder in flowing water, sharing with no one. In cases of urgent illness or peril, pray to the Noble One and summon the generals—they will respond immediately. Each spirit general commands troops to relieve suffering. Sincerity and adherence to the method are paramount; never attempt this lightly.

**Method for the Mighty Celestial Ding to Pursue and Capture Malevolent Ghosts**
First establish an altar. Choose a day when the Perfected Warrior descends for the ritual offering. Lay out a clean mat, spread purified yellow earth half an inch thick, and level it. Unfurl the mat atop the earth, placing four incense burners at the center. Arrange seasonal fruits, dried venison, and clear wine in four portions at the cardinal directions, then light the lamps and burn incense. The officiant, dressed in proper attire, approaches the altar, plants a sword upon it, and faces north to bow to the Most High Lord Lao, the Northern Culmen Great Emperor, the Four Sage Perfected Lords, and all spirit generals and troops. Next, visualize the Northern Emperor above the officiant’s head, suspended in the void, clad in a dark dragon robe, wearing a level-heaven crown, black shoes, and a sword, his solemn countenance vividly painted, guarded by the Four Sages. Then summon the four Mighty Celestial Ding spirit generals, each leading troops, to descend from heaven to the altar and partake of the offerings. Read the petition aloud, offering detailed prayers, presenting incense and wine three times without bowing. After the ritual, gather the spirit tablets and enshrine them in the spirit generals’ hall. For subsequent summonings, follow the procedures below, observing the proper decorum.

**Eastern Mighty Celestial Ding Pursuing Ghost General Wen Yu**
Clad in a green robe with wide sleeves, wearing a green headscarf, his face red, he wields twin blades.

**Southern Mighty Celestial Ding Capturing Ghost General Li Gongda**
Draped in a red-patterned wide-sleeved robe, wearing a red headscarf, his face reddish-yellow, he brandishes an iron staff.

**Western Mighty Celestial Ding Binding Ghost General Wu Tian’an**
Dressed in golden armor, wearing a plain headscarf, his face yellow-white, he holds an iron chain.

**Northern Mighty Celestial Ding Interrogating Ghost General Liu Wuzhen**
Clad in a black wide-sleeved robe, wearing a black headscarf, his face dark and ashen, he wields a halberd.

After invoking and offering to each according to their direction, if malevolent spirits or ghosts employ sorcery, summon the generals to pursue, capture, and interrogate them—they will respond with immediate efficacy.

**Northern Dipper Qi-Directing Method for Curing All Illnesses**
To treat illness, the officiant faces north with the patient before them. The officiant visualizes the Star Lord Tanlang, ten *zhang* tall, clad in plain silk robes, hair unbound, exhaling blue qi. Upon completing the visualization, inquire about the cause of the illness, then inhale the patient’s qi. Next, recite *Om* to Tanlang, draw in his blue qi, and blow it onto the patient’s afflicted area. With the right hand, gather the qi and recite the incantation:

"Subtly profound, profoundly obscure,
First Celestial Stem, Second Celestial Stem, Third Celestial Stem, Fourth Celestial Stem—
born of Heaven and Earth.
Spirits fail to return to nurture, ghosts fail to return to life.
Swiftly respond to my mouth, swiftly respond to my voice.
Hasten as the law commands!"

Upon completing the recitation, form the mudra again to gather the qi, and the illness will be cured immediately.

**Method of the Northern Thearch for Splitting Ghostly Fetuses, Ghostly Masses, and Malevolent Qi**

First face north and visualize oneself as the Six Ding spirits. Hold an iron axe in the right hand while the left hand forms the Six Ding mudra at the second joint of the third finger—do not move carelessly, for movement will render it inefficacious.

Next, visualize the earth as the Black Prison of Fengdu and burn incense to the left and right.

Then, bend the left leg and kneel on the right, placing a purified axe before the face.

Next, have the patient stand or sit facing south before the officiant. With the right hand, trace the character "田" (field) on the ground.

**Pattern of the "田" Character**
Open the Gate of Heaven,
Close the Door of Earth,
Leave the Gate of Man,
Block the Path of Ghosts,
Pierce the Heart of Ghosts,
Rupture the Belly of Ghosts.

Then recite the incantation again while tracing the "田" character:

"Reverently invoke the Great Black Deity of Heaven,
with sixfold penetration, swiftly sever and seize!"

Once the incantation is complete and the character formed, have the patient cough once, drawing in qi and blowing it onto the center of the "田" character. Immediately grasp the purified axe in the right hand and split it along the qi—whereupon the ghostly fetus, ghostly mass, and malevolent qi will dissipate at once.

**Talisman of the Three Officials for Searching Out Malevolence**
"Dispersed Form"

**Upper Prime: Heavenly Official of Bestowed Blessings**
**Middle Prime: Earthly Official of Pardoned Transgressions**
**Lower Prime: Water Official of Released Calamities**
Left: Azure Dragon
Right: White Tiger
Above: Vermilion Bird
Below: Dark Warrior
Generals of the Three and Five—
in hand they grasp the coiling serpent, ten thousand *zhang* in length,
from whose mouth fire spews ten thousand *li*, burning and slaying all wayless and malevolent ghosts.

**Concentrated Form**
This talisman, when worn upon the body, serves as the *kao-zhao* method for the ritual master. Recite the incantations over brush and ink before inscribing it.

**Incantation for the Brush**
Three hairs remain and spread,
revered beneath all heaven.
Heaven and Earth settle into place—
what ghost dares linger?
Left, the yang; right, the yin,
the Northern Dipper’s stalwart might.
Slay the deviant, sever the ghost,
annihilate misfortune and woe.
With the divine brush’s first stroke,
ten thousand ghosts cower and hide.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*
Blow *qi* upon the brush.

**Incantation for the Ink**
Divine ink, luminous and bright,
essence true from within the moon.
Inscribed talismans restrain ghosts,
demons and evil spirits lose their form.
Swallowed or worn by the afflicted,
eternal peace and health are secured.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*
Blow *qi* upon the ink.

Once the brush and ink are consecrated, face the five directions and silently recite the incantation while inscribing the talisman. If there is a place haunted by ghosts or malevolence, burn the talisman to ash, mix with water, and apply to the patient’s heart—or have them wear it—to repel all demonic spirits and ghostly beings.

*Dispersed Form*

**Zi Xin, Zi Yin, Zi Hui, Zi Zhen, Zi Lin, Zi Zhen, Zi Wu, Zi Geng** □□□□□□□
From Horn to Winnowing Basket,
From Well to Chariot,

From Dipper to Wall—
The Twelve Monthly Spirit Generals,
Great Yang Lord,
Great Yin Lord.
*Assembled Form*

Inscribe this talisman in the manner prescribed above. If a person is possessed by a ghost, place the talisman upon their head, and they will engage in battle—no ghost will fail to do so.

**Method for Interrogating Ghosts**
Invoke the Divine Official of the Northern Dipper, a revered spirit known as the Great General Without a Face. The Holy Mother of the Nine Heavens commands the interrogation of the ghost—swiftly manifest your numinous power.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

Recite this incantation thrice, face the northeast, and draw true *qi* of the dark hue. Blow it upon the rod and lean it against the afflicted one’s body. Visualize four mighty warriors striking and interrogating the ghostly affliction, compelling it to reveal its name.

**Method for Nailing Ghosts**
Mighty Celestial Deity of the Firmament, join with me to summon the Six Ding Generals—swiftly apply punishment!
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

After reciting this thrice, draw the *qi* of the firmament and blow it upon the crown of the afflicted. Cry aloud: *"Nail, arise!"*

**Method for Seizing and Controlling the Six Jia**
Whenever performing this rite, first offer sacrifice to the Six Jia Spirit Generals and recognize their forms, that they may be summoned to drive away and seize malevolent ghosts, appearing at once when called.

For the sacrifice, prepare twelve bundles of yellow paper, twelve horses, and twelve portions of wine and fruit. Perform the rite on a *gengshen* or *jiazi* day, or on a *ding* or *jia* day.

The First Spirit General, Tongbao Ling, stands before me.
The Second Spirit General, Wenhua Tong, stands behind me.
The Third Spirit General, Lingbao Gui, stands to my left.
The Fourth Spirit General, Ling Tongbian, stands to my right.
The Fifth Spirit General, Song Baoyi, stands above me.
The Sixth Spirit General, Huang Shengyi, stands below me.

When I walk a hundred paces, the Spirit Generals follow.
When I traverse ten thousand *li*, they remain at my left and right, before and behind.
Swiftly seize and control the ghosts and spirits—do not be remiss!
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

**Method for Interrogating with the Rod**
The Five Thunder Envoys of the Black East and Red Emperor descend in numinous power, wielding the Dragon Seal Rod to interrogate the ghost—swiftly reveal your name!
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

Face north, form the Heavenly Ding mudra with your left hand, and grasp the rod with your right. Recite the incantation thrice, draw the *qi* of the firmament, and blow it upon the rod. Visualize the Heavenly Ding warriors wielding the rod to strike and interrogate, compelling the ghost to reveal its name.

**Mountain-Character Method for Illuminating Ghosts**
The heavens are round, fourfold the spray—
drive the vengeful souls upward!
Six Ding and Six Jia,
Heavenly Ding warriors—
by the decree of the Heavenly Cavern and Celestial Perfection,
