**Mountain-Character Seal for Revealing Ghosts**
With the left hand, form the Mountain-Character seal, cover its face with a silk cloth, and face the northeast. Recite the incantation thrice, draw the true *qi* of the profound darkness, and blow it upon the patient’s crown. Instruct the patient to close their eyes and cough, then gather the *qi* with the sound and blow it upon the seal. Have the patient open their eyes to gaze upon it, and they will see the ghost of the afflicting spirit.

Should possession be required, have the patient close their eyes again. With the right hand, form the Sword mudra and drive it into the crown. Then recite the Ghost-Summoning Incantation:
*Azure and numinous, swiftly descend, flying soul—*
*Enter the sickened body, reveal your name!*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

Recite this thrice, draw three breaths of the firmament’s *qi*, and blow them upon the patient’s crown. Command the ghost to be bound beneath the cangue, and it will naturally transmit its confession.

**Solar Needle Method**
The sun of heaven and earth,
the divine radiance of the lunar horn—
wash away corpse-illness,
dispel pernicious *qi* to annihilation.
*Swiftly, swiftly, strike and seize!*

Fashion a needle from jujube wood struck by thunder, three *cun* and six *fen* in length. When treating illness, pass it through incense smoke. Hold the needle in the right hand, press the left hand’s third fingernail with the thumb, raise it before the heart, and gaze upon the sun. Recite the above incantation thrice in a single breath, then draw *qi* and blow it upon the needle. Pierce all painful and afflicted areas—none shall fail to respond.

**Firmament’s Canopy for Quelling Frenzied Malevolence**
If one raves, runs amok, shouts, laughs, or charges at others, swiftly identify the direction pointed by the Living Brilliance of the Firmament. Strike the teeth thrice, press the left thumb upon the second fingernail, hold the breath, and visualize the Great Sage of the Firmament: hair unbound, clad in plain robes, barefoot, wielding a sword, a nine-colored halo blazing from his crown, flames swirling fiercely around the blade. Upon completion of the vision, inscribe a talisman in the air with the right hand and recite the incantation:
*Firmament, numinous and bright,*
*seize and bind ghosts and spirits by decree!*
Recite this thrice in a single breath, draw *qi*, and spray it upon the afflicted. The possessed will submit at once, or bind their own head and beg for mercy. When finished, burn the talisman as described below.

**Jujube Charm for Curing All Illnesses**
Wash jujubes clean with fragrant water, any quantity will suffice. On the third or seventh day of the lunar cycle, within a purified chamber or before an altar of merit, burn incense and bow in reverence. Stand facing north, split the jujube, and recite the incantation:
*Your servant humbly invokes the Jade Emperor of the Vast Heaven,*
*swiftly dispatch the Fire Dragon to seize!*
Upon completion, visualize the Perfected Warrior, draw the true *qi* of azure, and blow it upon the jujube. For all illnesses, chew the jujube while reciting the charm over water—none shall fail to respond.

**Northern Emperor’s Seven-Star Elbow *Qi*-Dispersing Method**
This method is to be received and practiced on the days of *jiazi* or *gengshen*, one’s natal day, or the dawn of the third or seventh day of the lunar cycle. Take a length of pure hemp cord, as thick as three fingers, and comb it smooth with a clean wooden comb. Prepare twenty-five strands of five-colored silk thread (or five strands if fewer are available), and a single ancient coin with four characters. With the left hand, twist the thread and coin together into a cord, threading the coin and tying a knot while reciting the incantation once:
*Star of the Well, Star of the Well,*
*Star of Metal, Star of Metal.*
*Lost soul, lost soul,*
*hun-soul, po-soul, hun-soul, po-soul.*
*I humbly invoke the true fire of the southern quarter,*
*to aid your disciple’s hanging method.*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

The following day at sunrise, receive and practice the method as before.

Upon completing the ritual, when employing the method, thread the cord through the coin’s hole and tap it behind the elbow. For suppressing pain and the like, draw in a breath of *qi*, tightly bind it with the hand, and the effect will manifest immediately.

To restrain ghosts and spirits, dispel malevolent entities, or suppress inauspicious dwellings, hang the cord on the main hall’s beam or along the path where ghosts and spirits manifest—they will depart at once. Do not wear it when entering sacred temples, and avoid contact with women, chickens, dogs, or miscellaneous objects.

**Heavenly Master’s Method for Interrogating the Stove and Binding Ghosts**
Use a piece of wood, one foot and two inches in length, fashioned into a three-tiered altar, representing the Three Terraces stars. Visualize yourself as the Interrogating Summoner, stepping upon the Seven Primes’ Net before the stove. When binding the ghost, first have the head of the household hold the binding cord while the master writes the character for "ghost" on the ground, reciting:
*Open the Gate of Heaven, close the Door of Earth,*
*leave the Human Gate, block the Ghostly Path.*
Circle the "ghost" character three times, then recite:
*Generals Tang, Ge, and Zhou, hasten forth!*
Immediately have the head of the household strike the stove three times with the cord, then take it back. Envision the two messengers striking the Stove Lord, forcing him to bind the ghost beneath the character. Strike seven times, reciting [missing characters], then tie the Prison Seal at the cord’s end, followed by the Secure Head and Ghost-Binding Seals. Visualize the Stove Lord bound in prison, then apply the Ghost-Binding Seal again to secure him. Admonish the Stove Lord thus:
*Ho! Ho! Ho! You are a descendant of Zhang Nuo,*
*sealed by the Celestial Emperor as the Stove Lord,*
*charged with protecting this household.*
*How dare you allow foreign ghosts to enter,*
*bringing misfortune and disturbance to this dwelling?*
*Depart at once! Should you disobey,*
*I shall report you to the Celestial Emperor and the Northern Emperor,*
*file a petition to the Heavenly Bureau.*
*Do not say you were not warned!*
*Swiftly expel the foreign ghosts—*
*go at once, do not linger, or the blame shall be yours!*

After three days, lift the binding cord and burn spirit money for the two messengers, Ābōluó. When using the Ghost-Binding Seal, first recite the Sun and Moon Lords’ incantation, then step upon the Celestial Net.

*Great Sage Sun, Great Sage Moon,*
*descend with your radiant light,*
*your true *qi* of original form,*
*enter my Ghost-Binding Seal.*

**Ghost-Binding Seal**
*Chén*: raise the stroke upward from the second horizontal.
*Gèn*: press the middle joint of the middle finger.
*Yín*: on yin days, use the right hand; on yang days, the left, crossing them in application.

**Method for Imprisoning Ghosts in the Fire Prison**
On the southeastern *dìhù* (Earth Door), first spread a layer of fine ash to form a level circle three feet and six inches in diameter, leaving the southern gate open. Add another layer of ash, leaving the northern gate open. Drive the ghost in through the northern gate, then write the character for "fire" at the southern gate’s entrance with ash. When closing the prison gate, again write "fire" to seal it.

**Diagram of the Fire Prison**
**Incantation for Erecting the Fire Prison**
*Humbly invoke the Fire Bell Generals and Fire Bell Officers of the southern quarter,*
*descend from heaven to close my prison gate,*
*drive and bind malevolent ghosts,*
*subject them to interrogation and punishment.*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

Upon reciting, draw in *qi* and blow it into the prison. When the master establishes the prison, first visualize himself as the Great Emperor of Zhūlíng, pressing the nail of the left hand’s third finger, stepping upon the *Dīng* Net while reciting the incantation. If the ghost is particularly fierce, or if many ghosts are to be interrogated that day, or if unresolved malevolent matters persist, drive them into the Fire Prison to be incinerated.

**Method for Locking the Gate**
*The might of Heaven slays, the power of Earth seizes the true direction.*
*A thousand evils, ten thousand ghosts—who dares remain hidden?*
*With a single step and a breath drawn, all ghosts perish.*
*Left Kuí, right [missing character], the divine powers seize.*
*Lock them so none escape—*
*the divine generals swiftly bind them.*
*I act by the Northern Emperor’s decree.*

If someone petitions claiming harm from malevolent forces, the master first transforms into a deity to receive and restrain them, then proceeds with the dispatch. As the petitioner exits, the master forms the Locking Seal with his hand, takes three steps upon the *Dīng* Net, summons the divine generals, and draws the *qi* of the Celestial Net, reciting three times toward the northwest. Then, drawing the *qi* of the sun’s rays, he blows it onto the seal and directs it toward the afflicted person’s dwelling, silently commanding:
*Divine generals, swiftly lock them—*
*let none escape the slightest gap.*
Envision the Four Upright and Six *Jiǎ* warriors surrounding the place, locking down the malevolent ghosts.

**Northern Dipper’s Method for Entering a House to Protect the Body**
*Northern Dipper’s seven stars, I call you by name.*
*Malevolent spirits and lingering corpses, earthbound ghosts—hide your forms!*
*The Eight Kings’ soldiers, wherever I go,*
*guard my body for a thousand miles.*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

When the master arrives at the afflicted household, after entering and taking several steps, he visualizes himself as True Warrior, hair unbound and sword in hand, with the Four Upright Messengers, the Celestial Pivot, the Earthly Axis, and their retinue following. Forming the Dipper Seal with his left hand, he silently recites the incantation three times. Upon reaching the main hall, he sits and commands the afflicted person to be brought forth for questioning and treatment.

**Four Numinous Powers’ Method for Seizing Ghosts**
*Zhōng the True, Zǐ the Scenic, descend with the wronged and the sagely hosts.*
*Swiftly, Four Numinous Powers, in samādhi descend with truth!*
*Four divine generals, seize the wronged souls at once!*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

Have the afflicted person stand facing the master with eyes closed. The master then faces north, presses the *mǎo* trigram with his left hand, recites the incantation three times, draws a breath of *qi* from each of the four directions, takes a sip of water, and together with the *qi*, sprays it onto the afflicted person’s face, shouting:
*Divine generals, swiftly seize the ghost and deliver it into this body!*
If the body trembles, it is a sign of efficacy.

**Another Seizing Method**
*Humbly invoke the True Lord of the South, present in the bǐng direction,*
*swiftly descend with true fire into my water.*
*Heavenly Strategist, Heavenly Slayer,*
*aid my incantation’s power, aid my Daoist method,*
*seize the ghosts and spirits at once!*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

Face south, press the Dipper Seal with the left hand and the *zǐ* trigram with the right. Hold a bowl of pure water, draw in a breath of true *qi* from the sun, recite the incantation three times, and draw a breath of *qi* from each of the four directions, blowing them into the water. Then, envision the southern fire blazing across the sky, draw in a breath, and blow it into the water. Perform this method three times.

Then have the afflicted person drink the water, and they will tremble immediately. If you do not wish to subject them to interrogation, do not let them consume the ritual water; instead, the ritual master should inhale it, then spray it into a dim place and ask the afflicted what malevolent spirit they see.

**Binding Ghost Method**
*Humbly invoke the Northern Emperor, the gods of Fengdu.*
*Northern Emperor, Divine Lord,*
*aid the enactment of my sacred method,*
*seize and bind the pernicious spirits.*
*Humbly invoke the Great Divine Warden of Heavenly Prison,*
*let the binding method descend upon the heavenly prison,*
*with iron chains, swiftly bind the ghost’s hands.*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

Face north and perform the malevolent gesture. With both hands, form the Binding Ghost Seal, recite the incantation three times, draw in three breaths of *qi*, take a small sip of water, and spray it onto the afflicted person’s face. Command the divine generals to seize their head and bind it. When the binding takes effect, simply say, *"Bind tightly."*

**Pillory Ghost Method**
*Humbly invoke the Year Regulator, Month Regulator, Day Regulator, Hour Regulator,*
*the Six Yin Jiazi, the Six Yang Jiazi,*
*the Three Yang Assembly Chiefs,*
*the Earth Lords of the Nine Provinces,*
*the Four Mighty Ones, the Eight Vajras,*
*the Twelve Hourly Messengers—*
*now command them to place the ghost in the pillory for me.*
*I act by the decree of the Northern Emperor.*

After the malevolent spirit is seized, if it refuses to speak, the ritual master should face north, press the Ghost Eye Seal with the left hand, recite the previous incantation, and inscribe a Pillory Ghost Talisman. When the incantation and brushstroke are complete, recite the incantation again, burn the talisman to ashes, blow them onto the afflicted person’s head, and shout: *"Pillory it!"*

**Pillory Ghost Talisman Form**

**Alternative Method**
*Humbly invoke the Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper, the Heavenly Vajra Great Gods.*
*To the left, drive the Six Jia; to the right, drive the Six Ding.*
*Let the Dingmao swiftly command the ghostly Ding to pursue the soul,*
*let the Four Great Divine Continents seize and pillory it,*
*swiftly affix it to the ghost’s body, the ghost to the person’s body.*
*The iron pillory has arrived, its weight a thousand *jin*.*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

For this method, borrow a pillory from a nearby City God’s sacred temple. First, face north and recite the incantation three times. With the left hand, press the Celestial Stem Seal and blow toward the direction of the pillory’s location. Then, with both hands, form the Pillory Ghost Seal, recite the incantation three times, draw in a breath of *qi*, and blow it onto the afflicted person’s neck. Envision the divine generals pillorying the ghost and shout: *"Swiftly!"*

**Five Dipper Interrogation Method**
*Humbly invoke the true *qi* of the Five Dippers,*
*by the Northern Emperor’s decree, let it be enacted,*
*to distinguish the malevolent spirits.*
*Now impose the penal code,*
*swiftly interrogate the ghost’s body.*
*Beneath my hand: the Four Mighty Ones, the Eight Vajras,*
*the Heavenly Vajra Great Generals, the Heavenly Ding Warriors,*
*the Heavenly Prison Great Divine Warden—*
*swiftly interrogate the ghost to reveal its name.*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

Alternatively, the ritual master should face north, holding three interrogation rods. Recite the incantation three times, draw in a breath of *qi* from each of the five directions, and blow them onto the rods. Place one rod on the afflicted person’s back and the other two beside their legs. Recite the incantation once more, draw in a breath of Heavenly Vajra *qi*, blow it out, and command the divine generals to strike.

**Alternative Method**
*Humbly invoke the true *qi* of the Black Slayer of the North to descend in spirit,*
*wielding an iron rod to interrogate the ghost and reveal its name.*
*Interrogate the ghost to eradicate its root,*
*strike the ghost to sever its form.*
*Heaven turns, earth splits,*
*humans live, ghosts perish.*
*When the method arrives, let it be enacted.*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

For this method, use the rods as before and draw in a breath of Heavenly Vajra *qi* to blow upon them.

**Suppressing Ghost Method**
*Humbly invoke the Great Might of Heavenly Origin, the Great Might General,*
*the Great Might of Heavenly Light, the Great Might General,*
*the Great Might of Heavenly Impulse, the Great Might General,*
*the Great Might of Great Unity, the Great Might General.*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance, seize it!*

The ritual master should face the Heavenly Gate, form the Mountain Character Seal with the left hand, and hold paper and brush in the right. Recite the incantation three times, draw in a breath of *qi*, and blow it onto the seal on the paper. Form the seal again, recite the incantation, and inscribe a single character, completing the incantation and brushstroke. Blow the seal onto the character, place it on the afflicted person’s back, and command the divine generals to press it down.

**Alternative Method**
*Mount Tai’s foundation overturned, crushing the ghost without delay.*
*The Mighty Spirit pierces through the ear,*
*the ghostly fiend turns to mud.*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

The ritual master should face east, form the Mountain Character Seal with both hands, recite the incantation three times, and draw in a breath of *qi*. Envision the Mighty Spirit lifting Mount Tai and fiercely placing it upon the afflicted person’s head.

**Master Li’s Ghost-Subduing Method**
*Humbly invoke the divine spirits of Heaven and Earth,*
*the Five Agents—Metal, Wood, Water, Fire, Earth—*
*the mighty Ghost Kings who communicate with the numinous,*
*the brave warriors who enact the method □□□□,*
*the Golden-Armored Generals, the mighty ritual warriors,*
*seize and hold it on both sides.*
*Master Li, the Perfected Lord, wields the sword in hand,*
*enacting the method to seize the malevolent.*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

Face north and perform the malevolent gesture. With the left hand, form the Dipper Seal, and with the right, press the *zǐ* trigram. Recite the incantation three times, draw in three breaths of *qi*, and blow them onto the afflicted person’s face. Command the divine generals to seize it. If instructed to strike, strike; if instructed to subdue, subdue.

**Burning Ghost Method**
*Humbly invoke the Generals of the Southern *bǐng-dīng*,*
*the Fire Bell Generals, the Heavenly Vajra Fire Gods,*
*the Great Fire Dragon Generals, the Fire Wheel Generals,*
*the Great Burning Ghost Generals—*
*swiftly burn the ghost for me!*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

The ritual master should face south, form the Fire Wheel Seal with both hands, recite the incantation three times, and draw in a breath of *qi* to blow onto the cinnabar ink and brush. Then, take a piece of black paper, form the Small Fire Seal with the left hand, and inscribe the Fire Wheel Talisman on the afflicted person’s back, commanding it to burn. When inscribing and burning the talisman, recite the following incantation:

**Fire Wheel Talisman**
*Within the heart, seven revolutions; the Twenty-Eight Constellations—*
*Humbly invoke the Lord of the Sun of the East,*
*secondly invoke the Lord of Fire Virtue of the South,*
*thirdly invoke the Fire Mountain Spirit of the West,*
*fourthly invoke the Great Fire Wheel of the North,*
*fifthly invoke the True Fire descending from the Center.*
*In my hand, I grasp the Great Fire Wheel,*
*burning the ghost’s body to nothingness.*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

Recite this in a single breath, completing the incantation and talisman.

**Four Rivers Freezing Malevolent Spirits Method**
*Humbly invoke the Source Lords of the Four Rivers,*
*the Great Gods of the Nine Rivers,*
*seize the icy souls of the malevolent,*
*swiftly freeze them!*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!*

The ritual master should face north, press the *zǐ* trigram with the right hand, and hold a bowl of pure water. Recite the incantation three times, draw in a breath of *qi*, and blow it into the water.

Recite the incantation once more, face north, draw in a breath of water-*qi*, and spray it upon the afflicted. Command the divine generals: "Hasten and freeze them for me!" If the afflicted shivers, this is the sign of efficacy.

**Spirit-Illumination Method**
Humbly invoke the Ascending Clarity Spirit,
the Hastening Earth Spirit,
the Great Spirit Who Drives the Hun-Souls,
and the Swiftly Obeying Numinous Pursuit-of-Hun General.
"Without fail, reveal the true form
of those I have subdued,
of those I have manifested!"
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!

For this method, the ritual master first faces north, takes a sheet of paper, and recites the incantation three times. Drawing in *qi*, he blows it onto the paper, then instructs the afflicted to twist two paper legs—one left, one right—and dip them in oil. Recite the incantation once more and blow upon the paper legs. Have a family member light a lamp and support the afflicted in the room to illuminate them. The ritual master conceals the Iron Rod Seal within his sleeve. When illuminated, all present may see the malevolent spirit.

**Summoning the Local Earth God Method**
Humbly invoke the Dark Thearch of the North:
"Hasten and summon the Earth God of this household!
By the decree of the Three Clarities,
upon hearing this command, you shall bear heavy punishment.
All spirits stand in attendance,
daring not leave their posts.
Swiftly come forth to the altar below!"
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!

For this method, the ritual master faces north and recites the incantation once. Drawing in *qi*, he blows it upon the ground, saying: "Summon the Earth God of this household to follow." Next, inscribe one Summoning Earth God Talisman and burn it to ashes. With the left hand, form the Earth-Thunder Seal—the *chǒu* trigram. Recite the incantation once more and blow upon the talisman ashes, saying: "Hasten and come, await my instructions. Divine generals, temporarily restrain the malevolent spirit to one side." Recite the incantation again, take a small mouthful of water, and spray it upon the afflicted’s face. Command the divine generals to drive the Earth God into the afflicted’s body for a clear response. The Earth God shall report the details. Once verified, order the divine generals to escort the Earth God back to his post, where he shall constantly patrol and protect, and drive the malevolent spirit forth for further interrogation. The Gatekeeper and Street Earth Gods shall be summoned in the same manner.

**Summoning Earth God Talisman**
Black Slayer Spirit, Black Slayer Sage,
summon the Earth God, gather and seize within the courtyard.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!

First face north and recite the incantation once, draw qi and blow it upon the brush, then recite the incantation again as you write. When the incantation ends, the talisman is complete.

**Summoning the Hun-Soul Method**
Reverently invoke the Great Deity of the Northern Emperor, the Jade Maidens of the Nine Heavens, the Six Ding and Six Jia, the Heavenly Demon King, the Divine General of the Left Hun-Soul, and the Divine General of the Right Po-Soul. Swiftly summon the true qi, swiftly deliver the true form.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!

The ritual master then faces east, recites the incantation three times, draws three mouthfuls of qi, and blows them upon the afflicted’s body. Next, take two sheets of yellow paper and a cinnabar brush, recite the incantation once, draw qi, and blow it upon the paper and brush. With the left hand, form the Six Ding mudra and write two Summoning the Hun-Soul Talismans. Secure them with a needle, burn them in a paper lantern to ash, and mix with ritual water.

If the afflicted is severely ill, unconscious, with clenched jaw and rigid limbs, yet the heat in the heart has not ceased, swiftly pour the talisman water into the ears. Have one person hold a mirror beside the ear and strike it while loudly calling the afflicted’s name; soon they will revive.

When writing the Summoning the Hun-Soul Talisman, recite the following incantation:

**For Summoning the Hun-Soul**
Reverently invoke the Six Ding and Six Jia gods, the Six Ding and Six Jia generals, bestow the Five Numinous Scripts. Summon the original destiny from the northeast. How swiftly it comes—permitted by Xu Chang’s command.

Recite the incantation and write the talisman; when the incantation ends, the brush is spent.

**Transferring the Method**
Reverently invoke the Seven Descending of Flying Ascent, come to the body and declare your names. Urgently summon the Flying Hun-Soul Messenger to swiftly arrive and transfer the hun-soul.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance!

This method is used when the afflicted is emaciated and weak, unable to endure the driving and interrogation. Summon another person to stand facing the patient. First, have the afflicted blow qi, then have the standing person inhale it. Both close their eyes. The ritual master faces north, recites the incantation three times, draws qi, and blows it upon the afflicted’s head. Recite the incantation once more, draw the afflicted’s qi, and blow it upon the substitute’s body, commanding: "Swiftly enter the body!"

**Another Method**
Reverently invoke the Heavenly Deities of the Black Path to come to my body, as I act by the Northern Emperor’s decree.

This method is used when a child is afflicted and unable to speak. The ritual master first has the mother hold the child, stand facing him, and inhale the child’s qi once with eyes closed. The ritual master forms the Golden Spear mudra with both hands, faces north, recites the incantation three times, draws three mouthfuls of qi, and blows them toward the child’s face. Command the divine generals to swiftly drive the spirit into the body. The child’s spirit, once transferred, will differ from its usual state.

**Erasing the Blockage Method**
Reverently invoke the Great Sage of Six Penetrations, the Mighty Heavenly Ding, assist me in attaining numinous communion, and together search for and seize the malevolent qi. Let it enter the brush without movement.

By the Emperor’s decree!

First, inquire about the size of the patient’s blockage, then have them firmly grasp it with their hand. Place a sheet of thick paper on the table. With the left hand, form the Golden Spear mudra, and with the right hand, hold the brush. Visualize the brush as a golden spear and the paper as the blockage. Facing the Heavenly Gate, recite the incantation three times, inhale qi, and blow it into the brush. Next, with the left hand, press the *mao* trigram, and on the paper, write a single "field" character (田). Recite:

Open the Heavenly Gate,
Seal the Earthly Door.
Preserve the Human Portal,
Block the Demon Path.
Pierce the demon’s heart;
Rend the demon’s belly.

Use this incantation to write the "field" character. Have the patient cough once, then with the sound, inhale qi and blow it onto the *mao* trigram. Press firmly, and with the brush, erase the "field" character, starting from the Heavenly Gate and moving toward the southeast. Ask how much the blockage has diminished, then take black ink and erase it again. Each stroke must be accompanied by reciting the incantation and inhaling qi to erase it.

**Method for Treating Childhood Fright and Convulsions**
Sever the waist, sever the hands,
Split the belly, gouge the heart—
The Six Ding wield the blade.

The ritual master takes a brush dipped in ink, recites the incantation once, draws the Heavenly Rigid Qi, and blows it into the brush. Then, with the left hand, forms the Golden Blade mudra, pressing the thumb against the four fingers, extending the index and middle fingers straight. Recite the first line of the incantation and write the character "moon" (月) on the child’s palm. Recite the second line and write the character "blade" (刀). Then draw the Solar Qi and exhale it onto the crown of the head. If the eyes begin to droop, immediately wash away the characters.

**Character Placement in the Hand:**
For boys, first write on the left hand; for girls, first write on the right hand.

**Method for Treating Childhood Milk-Retention**
By decree! I summon the Earth Spirit of the Central Palace, the obedient *mie* soul, to sever and seize.

First inquire about the size of the retention, then take a thick piece of paper. Have someone firmly grasp the retention mass, ensuring the child cries out once. Inhale qi, recite the incantation three times, and blow onto the paper and brush. According to the size of the retention, draw its shape on the paper. With the left hand, form the Golden Blade mudra, recite the incantation once, inhale qi, and blow onto the paper, then swiftly tear it into two or three pieces. Recite the incantation again, inhale qi, and tear it into finer shreds—immediate efficacy.

**Method for Treating Blown Retention**
Left Green Dragon, swiftly vanish.
Right White Tiger, swiftly vanish.

Have the patient face west and stand before the ritual master, regardless of distance. If the retention is on the left, instruct the patient to grasp it firmly, cough three times, and with each cough, inhale qi, recite the incantation, and blow onto the ritual master’s hand. The master then locates the left retention and performs the seizure thrice. If the retention is on the right, repeat seven times.

**Nine Heavens Mysterious Maiden’s Flying Needle Method**
Divine needle, numinous and bright,
Aligns with the Great Clarity above.
The three paths’ bitter afflictions,
Disease appears, startling the self.
The needle meets the Heavenly Bureau,
The Heavenly Bureau takes heed.
Again, it meets the Earthly Prison,
The Earthly Prison must hear.
By decree of the Most High Lord Lao,
The needle shall not strike again,
The disease shall not recur.
Swiftly, swiftly, as in the statutes and ordinances.

For this method, first select a fire-day to gather the first straight branch from the southeast side of a peach tree, one foot and two inches in length. Immediately face north, recite the incantation seven times, draw the Heavenly Rigid Qi, blow upon it, and store it in a red silk pouch. When treating a patient, have them stand facing the ritual master at a distance of about ten feet. Ask where the pain is, and instruct them to grasp the spot firmly. The ritual master then forms the Golden Spear mudra with the left hand, holds the needle in the right, and presses it against the *mao* trigram. The left hand rests on the waist, the right hand at the chest. Recite the incantation seven times, draw the Heavenly Rigid Qi, and blow onto the needle. Instruct the patient to cough once, inhale qi, recite the incantation once, and blow onto the *mao* trigram on the right hand. Rotate the needle three turns to the left, seven turns to the right, recite the incantation, and visualize the needle entering the afflicted area.

**Four Saints’ Qi-Dispersing Method**
Reverently invoke Heavenly Peng, Heavenly You, Black Killer, and True Martial—restrain the martial, sever and kill: *hūm*.

First, have the patient stand facing southwest. The ritual master then burns incense and transforms into the Envoy of the Demon-Quelling Court. With both hands forming the *zi* trigram, step backward along the Seven Stars’ Net. For a male patient, use the left foot to tread the net and point at him. For a female patient, use the right foot to tread the *ding* trigram and point at her. The ritual master steadies their body, closes their eyes, and silently recites the incantation once, visualizing the Four Saints descending from the sky. Swiftly inhale qi and blow toward the patient, instructing them to inhale the qi through their nose and swallow it, then exhale the pathogenic qi from their mouth. The breathing must not be audible to the ritual master’s own ears. After the treatment, have four people present money and horses in four portions, seal the petition, and detail the circumstances of the treatment and the patient’s condition—expressing gratitude must not be omitted.

**Record of Breaking Malevolent Spirits**
[Text missing]

The sacred talismans and the divine decree of True Warrior are invoked. We respectfully summon the Heavenly General Guangming, Ghost King of the Vast Net. Record the patient’s native place, birth year, month, day, and hour. The ritual master states their partial title.

Reveal the register and issue the command: Marshal Zhao Gongming, coercively summon the demonic form. Step *lin-lin*, step *lin-lin*, *lin* step *lin*, *lin* step *lin*—command and seize. Record the patient’s birth year, month, day, and hour. The ritual master states their partial title.

For these two registers, first have the patient’s family prepare a detailed petition before inscribing them. When writing, first burn incense and present the petition’s contents in prayer. Then, using the Mudra of the Five Peaks and Three Paths, inscribe the talismans. Draw *qi* from the Ghost Gate, combine it with the mudra, and blow it into the *Breaking Malevolent Spirits* register. Have the family take it home and burn one thousand strings of paper money. Reveal the register and place it by the patient’s head, beneath their bedding. After a short while, the malevolent spirit will manifest its form and shadow, or enter the body and declare its name.

**Mudra of the Five Prisons and Three Paths**
With the left hand, press the *mao* trigram and say: *"Grind the needle."*
Next, shake the upper joint of the middle finger and say: *"Vajra."*
Then, press the middle joint of the four fingers and say: *"Red apricot."*
Press the *mao* trigram near the palm and say: *"Ink-black."*
Next, press the middle joint of the middle finger and say: *"Numinous Treasure."*
Press the *mao* trigram and say: *"All merits accomplished, the horn is subdued and the corner is suppressed."*
Press the *chen* trigram and say: *"Rise and live, alone and bound, gather the souls of Han, gather the souls of the public."*
Draw *qi* and flick it into the talisman.

**Methods for Invoking Divine Generals in Sacrificial Offerings**
This is a separate technique among miscellaneous methods, often used with great efficacy. It is appended here.

For all divine generals invoked in sacrificial rites, on the third, seventh, or thirtieth day, or on *jiazi* or *gengshen* nights, prepare money, horses, wine, fruit, incense, and lamps. Offer one steamed bun, a black silk banner, two bamboo knives, three staffs, two *qian* of cinnabar, and half a cup of pure vinegar, arranging them in a purified chamber. After the attendants have settled, present the invocation and prayers. Thrice offer incense and wine. At the third watch, burn all the money, horses, banners, and staffs. The ritual master consumes the steamed bun, cinnabar, and vinegar. Then, at the place of offering, calm the mind, close the eyes, and sit upright—or lie down if necessary. After a short while, a figure wearing a hat, robe, and sash will appear and converse with the ritual master. If anything is forgotten, perform the summoning and subduing method, and memory will naturally return.

When offering money and horses, prepare a petition for each, inscribe the spirit tablets, and present them:
*Seizing General Cui Shuxuan.*
*Binding General Lu Jiquan.*
*Shackling General Dou Yang, Beating General Yang Guang.*
*Yellow-Headed General Chen Zhen.*
*Disheveled General Liu Zhong.*
*Prison-Head General Yang Zheng.*
*Five Directions’ Pursuing Ghost General Zhao Gongming.*
*Left and Right Urgent Seizing Generals Yao Duan.*
*Fire Wheel General Song Wuji.*
*Torturing Ghost General Deng Xingwen.*
*Beheading and Draining Blood General Liu Yan.*
*Yaksha General Chen Shouzhong.*
*Divine Officer Wu Lang Ma Sheng.*

**Method for Suppressing Scorpion Stings**
If a scorpion’s venom stings a person, swiftly press the second joint of the left hand’s second finger, recite the incantation, and blow on the painful area to suppress it—the pain will cease immediately.
Incantation:
*"Eight Mights spew poison—hasten as the law commands!"*

**Alternative Method (Mudra as Above)**
Heavenly Scorpion, beseech the water to extinguish the poison. By day, face the sun; by night, face the Dipper’s net. Draw a breath of *qi*, blow it onto the talisman, then inhale a breath from the talisman and swallow it—the pain will cease immediately.

Recite the above incantation, write the talisman, and affix it—the cure will be immediate.

*Tai Shang’s Secret Essentials for Assisting the State and Saving the People, Volume Seven—Concluded*
*Tai Shang’s Secret Essentials for Assisting the State and Saving the People, Volume Eight*

Master Yuanmiao Zong of the Cavernous Mystery, Compiler of *Tai Shang’s Orthodox Methods: Diagrams and Texts of Yu’s Steps, Dipper-Net Hand Seals, and Gaze Techniques*

The methods of Yu’s steps, Dipper-net hand seals, and gaze techniques constitute the great essentials of the Dao and the primordial discipline of its methods. The step-net rides upon the upright *qi* to govern beings; the seal-gaze operates through the divine mechanism to enact transformation. Whether cultivating immortality and refining the true, or summoning, commanding, and subduing, none can do without these.

Though earlier versions of the method texts recorded their outlines, omissions in practical application were not few. Here, I have compiled what has been transmitted to make them complete. May this modest effort encompass the vast, so that the marvels of the method families may be fully realized in their application.

**Method of Yu’s Steps and Dipper-Net Seals**

Yu’s steps emulate the images of creation and the movements of the sun and moon’s measured cycles. One month has three conjunctions; each conjunction spans three decades. These three decades are the three full numbers. One season has three conjunctions; these three conjunctions make nine decades. Thus, one step is one conjunction; one conjunction has three traces. Three steps yield nine traces, symbolizing one season. Bringing the feet together represents the celestial conjunction.

Raising the left foot first is the step of spring and autumn; raising the right foot first is the step of winter and summer. The first months of spring and autumn are yang phases; the first months of winter and summer are yin phases.

Thus, life and death, control and command employ spring and autumn; storage and accumulation employ winter and summer. It is also said: men should use spring and autumn, while women should use winter and summer.

Moreover, the three steps and nine traces emulate the three origins and nine qi. The twelve traces emulate the twelve pitch-pipes. The fifteen traces emulate the numbers of three and five.

The art of adapting to circumstances lies in the subtleties of the method’s weight and measure. Yet it is called "Yu’s Steps" because Great Yu, in regulating the waters, accomplished a work that covered the heavens. He was truly bestowed this step-method to control spirits and summon numinous beings, hence it was named "Yu’s Steps."

In all step-treading methods, visualize the body as the Envoy of the Demon-Quelling Court, the Orthodox Unity Dharma Master, the Three Origins and Five Virtues General, the Clerk and Merit Officers, the Lion and White Crane, with an array of attendants standing guard.

First recite the Purification Mantra. According to the scriptural method, stepping with the mind focused on the spirit is especially efficacious; one need not rely solely on physical traces.

The scripture states: "Yu’s Steps were received by Yu from the Most High, unfolding the celestial net and earthly principles. Externally, they are Yu’s Steps, seeking the true and restraining the hundred things—humans, spirits, dragons, ghosts, evil beasts, venomous insects—subduing them without killing. Those who resist and do not submit are executed."

Its principles include combining the five dipper-stars into three steps and nine traces, or twelve traces, or thirty-five traces, or fifteen traces. There are also methods for reversing and circling three times, which are listed below.

When stepping the seven stars, proceed from the first to the seventh, called "forward progression." Then reverse from the seventh back. Return again from the first to the seventh, called "reverse progression." The "earthly gate" signifies ascending from the earthly gate to heaven.

**Method of Three Steps and Nine Traces**
The scripture states: "First, as the Flying Celestial Net treading the Earthly Principles, Yu’s Steps transform into nine traces, also corresponding to the Dipper’s numbers, circling forward, backward, and reverse three times. Stepping three times is not as effective as performing the Three Nets three times. If one seeks swift efficacy, simply step the old net three times, once on the left and once on the right—men emphasize the left, women the right. After completing left and right, repeat once more, totaling three presses."

**Method of Twelve-Trace Yu’s Steps**
**Method of Three-Five-Trace Yu’s Steps**
**Method of Treading Earthly Principles and Flying Celestial Net**
For Yu’s Steps of the Flying Celestial Net treading Earthly Principles, all must be performed in reverse three times.

The scripture states: "For those who perform hidden merits to aid the state, protect the body, and save others, first tread the Earthly Principles three times, then fly the Celestial Net three times, then disperse into the three-step, nine-trace Yu’s Steps, turning the Celestial Pivot to strike and halt. If fearing it will not stop, perform the twelve-step Yu’s Steps once, or step fifteen steps. Visualize the upper, middle, and lower Three Generals, their troops, and the Six Jia spirits, turning the Celestial Pivot to point at them. Doing this three times will dissolve all matters without harming the lives of yin spirits or creatures. If performed six times, what is controlled can be destroyed, restraining its reckless actions and diminishing one’s merit and virtue."

The scripture states: "When stepping to control or destroy, simultaneously form the Knife-Finger Seal with the left and right hands, on the third joint of the fifth finger. When dealing with violent people, form the Knife-Finger Seal for evil persons on the right side of the third joint of the right hand’s fifth finger. The right governs killing, the left governs life; do not act recklessly, and carefully examine the principles. To subdue evil ghosts, form the Ghost-Knife Seal on the underside of the third joint of the left hand’s fifth finger."

The scripture states: "For malevolent spirits, poisonous dragons, demonic ghosts causing reckless storms and violent rains that harm people and things, whether on water or land, step the Celestial Net and Earthly Principles each three times, dispersing into nine, twelve, or fifteen traces of Yu’s Steps, or perform three reversals. First nine steps, then reverse to the net’s head, then perform twelve steps, then reverse to fifteen steps. Align left and right with clothing, grasp the Dipper-Star with the left hand and point. Turn the Celestial Pivot, raising the hand to point three, six, or nine times, three rounds, and the poisonous demons will cease. Six rounds will cause harm and illness; nine rounds will result in death. Though this is a method of restraint and killing not of the Dao, one must not fail to be cautious in its principles. Assess the demonic affliction; if it ceases, release it, and do not kill immediately. If people and things are unsettled, or there are droughts, floods, or baleful stars, all can be restrained and governed."

The various diagrams of the Celestial Net, Earthly Principles, and Three-Five Yu’s Steps are of great importance, each with its own scriptural methods. Here, only the essentials are briefly outlined, so that practitioners of the method may know the ladder to its profound mysteries and recognize the threshold of the Original True.

**Purification Mantra for Ascending Steps**
"I purify my body with the sun, refine my true nature with the moon. Immortals assist me; sun and moon aid my form. The twenty-eight constellations unite with me; a thousand evils and ten thousand impurities are swept away by water and made clear. Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands."

**Method of Yu’s Steps for Heaven-Earth Harmony**
Whenever ascending Yu’s Steps, first recite the incantation:
"I am the Great One of the Grotto’s depths, my head bears the Seven Stars, my steps tread the Four Numinous Beasts. Grasping the golden sword, I stand in the Xun position, meandering in procession until I reach Kun. The earthly gate at Xun Palace must be sealed until I reach the Heavenly Gate to pay homage to the Emperor Lord. Three steps and nine traces ascend the Bright Star; the three disasters and nine calamities depart from my body. Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands."

After completing Yu’s Steps, recite the incantation:
"Qian honors the radiant spirit; Kun complies with the inner camp. The Two Modes harmonize; the Six Directions are auspicious and upright. Heaven and earth unite in prosperity; eternal peace and solemn clarity. Responding to the primordial yellow, above is the robe, below the skirt. Zhen ascends, Gen rises; Kan complies, Li shines. Xun flourishes, Dui generates; tiger steps and dragon soars. Heavenly Gate, Earthly Gate, Human Gate, Ghost Gate. Who guards me? The vast azure heavens. Today’s Yu’s Steps correspond to the Celestial Net above. Ghosts and spirits submit as guests; below, misfortune is repelled. What is sought is granted; the response is timely and numinous. Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands."

After reciting the step-incantations, proceed according to the method and follow the heart’s intent.

**Method of Intersecting Qian with Yu’s Steps**

Incantation:
*Kan’s double, Gen’s single step to intersect Qian;
Zhen’s ascent with double strides, Dui does the same.
Kun’s single, Li’s single and double step Xun;
Returning via the Three Terraces, one ascends to face Heaven.*

Upon completing the steps, form the Purple Tenuity Seal. Above Qian, transform the body and mount the white crane, drifting to the Heavenly Gate to pay homage to the Imperial Lord. Present the matters of the heart and petition for a decree to fulfill one’s wishes. Then retrace the steps from the Heavenly Gate back to Xun.

Within the oratory or altar, ascend the platform daily at the hours of *zi* and *wu*. Yu’s Steps may be employed. Dishevel the hair and wield the sword, stepping toward Qian. Enter the altar, sit with upright heart, close the eyes, and intone:

*Qian’s origin, prosperity, advantage, and steadfastness;
Sun and moon conceal my form.
Ten thousand calamities cannot assail me;
My lifespan equals Heaven’s.*

Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands.

Again, intone:
*I am the master of Daoist ritual practice.
Water, fire, blades, and weapons cannot reach me;
Sickness and thieves cannot approach me.
I shine with the same light as sun and moon;
All I undertake prospers.*

Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands.

Upon completing the step-incantation, proceed according to the method.

**Ji Ji Yu’s Steps Method** may be used on yang days.
**Wei Ji Yu’s Steps Method** may be used on yin days.
The incantations for these two step-methods are the same as above.

**Fire Bell Dipper Steps to Slay and Subdue All Malevolent Spirits**

**Fire Bell Spirit Incantation:**
*Supreme Divine Bell, essence of the Flame Emperor.
Radiance like lightning, illuminating the Three Clarities.
Raging fire spans ten thousand *li*; ghosts cannot escape their forms.
With one imprint of the divine seal, perverse spirits are reduced to ashes.
Generals of the Three and Five, officers and soldiers of the Vast Expanse.
Leveling Heaven and striking Earth, they ceaselessly slay ghosts.
Flying talismans and swift seals, crowned with the Five Stars.
Hurl fire to slay ahead; ten thousand ghosts and a thousand spirits.
Ghosts and thieves of the Six Heavens are delivered to the divine soldiers.
The Five Numinous True Elders are my original masters.
Unobstructed divine power; all spirits return in unison.
Evil ghosts are annihilated; misfortune is swiftly pursued.
The Nine Paths of the Central August One spread might to the four directions.
Lurking old *qi* is eradicated, not a trace remains.
The Five Pestilences and Seven Afflictions—I can slay them.
What spirit dares oppose? What ghost dares transgress?
Their forms are executed in Fengdu; their corpses are severed by the Northern Dipper.
With one imprint of the divine seal, ten thousand ghosts dissolve to dust.*

Swiftly, swiftly, as the True Lord of the Great Emperor commands.

Grasp the seal in the left hand and the sword in the right. Recite the Fire Bell Incantation seven times, one star per incantation. Step in the likeness of the Northern Dipper: first, left step to *Tanlang*; next, right step to *Jumen*; then, left point to *Luxing*; next, left step to *Wenqu*; then, right step to *Lianzhen*; next, left step to *Wuqu*; finally, right step to *Pojun*. For the *Luxing* star, do not step directly upon it. With each of the seven steps, visualize a star as golden beneath the feet—all seven steps are identical. Imprint the seal upon any doubtful location, applying cinnabar and realgar to the seal.

**Three Terraces Seven Stars Dipper Method** may be employed for all healing and salvific matters.
**Entering the Dipper Step Method** is used for petitions, summons, and decrees.

For all steps of this Dipper, first recite the incantation:
*I am the Heavenly Eye, following Heaven’s course.
My essence is like thunder and lightning, illuminating the eight extremities.
Bright and penetrating within and without, nothing does not submit.*

Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands.

When stepping the Dipper, enter its bounds. For petitions, summons, or decrees, proceed according to one’s original intent. If purifying defilement, healing illness, or performing rituals, recite the *Purifying Heaven and Earth Incantation*:

*Within the cavern, profound and void; resplendent and vast, the Supreme Origin.
Mighty spirits of the eight directions, render me natural.
Numinous treasure talismanic command, universally proclaimed to the Nine Heavens.
Qianluo Danna, the mighty *gang* of the Supreme Mystery.
Slay demons and bind perversity; slay a thousand ghosts.
Zhongshan spirit incantation, original jade script of the Primordial Beginning.
Reciting it once repels ghosts and extends years.
Marching through the Five Marchmounts, known to the Eight Seas.
Demon kings bow their heads; divine perfected attend and guard.
Malevolence and defilement are cleansed; the Dao’s *qi* endures eternally.*

Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands.

Again, intone:
*Limpid water, blossoming with the essence of sun and moon.
Within lies the Northern Dipper, concealing the Three Terraces.
Divine water sprayed and sprinkled; misfortune departs, fortune arrives.*

Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands.

Again, intone:

My left eye is the sun, my right eye the moon.
The sun serves as general, the moon as marshal.
The Five Agents spray water to purge defilement—nothing remains unremoved.
Sweep away malevolent spirits, dispel the Five Evils.
Ghosts of every defilement swiftly flee ten thousand leagues.

Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands.

When treating illness or resolving impurity is complete, step forth from the Dipper with Yu’s Pace, reciting the Pace of Yu incantation. At the afflicted one’s place, intone the Heavenly Peng demon-slaying and other incantations, then administer the ritual water to cure.

Upon completing the Dipper-stepping rite, exit the Dipper with this incantation:
The Five Phases spur one another; the rigid sword wields might.
The Six Jia assist me; the Three Terraces ward off wrong.
Heaven revolves, earth turns; yin and yang open and part.
Attain long life, transcend the world; sun and moon shine as one.

Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands.

**Stepping the Huoluo Dipper Method**
**Incantation and Formula for Stepping the Huoluo Dipper**

Essential is the Dipper, the twelve celestial hours.
Upholding heaven’s net, martial might arrays.
*Qi* flickers and shifts like floating clouds.
The Seven *Qi* ascend, corresponding to heaven above.
Know transformation—there is a time and season.
Enter the Dipper’s lodging, cross the heavenly pass.
The Six Jia’s rhythm holds, uniting with Yi.
Tread upon Heavenly Ying, mount Heavenly Ren.
Flank Heavenly Pillar, embrace Heavenly Heart.
From here traverse, pass Heavenly Qín.
Beside Heavenly Fǔ, gaze toward Heavenly Chōng.
Enter Heavenly Inner, exit Heavenly Péng.
Essential is the Dipper’s Way—hard and soft harmonize.
Augment fortune and emolument, leave them for posterity.
Emerge from darkness, live for a thousand myriad years.

Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands.

When this Dipper is meticulously traversed, apply it as needed in the moment. Upon completing the steps, recite other incantations and methods at will.

**The Three-Cable Net Method**
The Three-Cable Net of the Northern Spirit subdues all spectral perversities, ghosts, and plague demons.

**Stepping the Thunder-Fire Dipper Method**
One revolution, thrice tapping at *yín*.

Two revolutions, tap at *chén*.
Three revolutions, tap at *wǔ*.
Four revolutions, tap at *zǐ*.
Five revolutions, tap at *shēn*.
Six revolutions, tap at *yǒu*.
Seven revolutions, tap at *xū*.
Eight revolutions, tap at *hài*.

**The Three-Powers Net Method**
For all incantations and consecrated water, summon and visualize the Three Origins and the Five Virtue Generals, clench the fists, and step this net.

**The Three-Step Ding-Character Net Method**
For drawing sword-water, use this net-stepping method.

**The Thunderclap Dissolution Incantation for Slaying Ghosts Net Method**
First tap beneath the nail of the left ring finger, then cross the feet of the Northern Dipper, gather wandering souls with the hand, and slay ghosts to annihilate their forms.

**The Net-Stepping Incantation for Consecrated Water to Slay Ghosts in the Capital Bureau**
Solemnly command: "Hark! Naked and towering, burn through the Heavenly Lord.
Heaven is my father, Earth my mother,
the Sun my elder brother, the Moon my elder sister.
To my left strides the Azure Dragon, to my right the White Tiger.
Before me, the thousand-mile net is deployed; behind me, the White Yang sword.
I summon the Five Dragons of the Five Directions into my water.
I summon the Five Crows of the Five Directions to enter my water.
All malevolent persons, evil ghosts, thieves, tigers, wolves—those who plot harm—
are seized and delivered beneath the Heavenly Rigor, forbidden to move or act.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands."

**The Seven-Step Iron Lid Net Method**
Tap the upper joint of the left middle finger, seal the Four Mountains with three revolutions, and gather mountain spirits and temple demons into the Nine Springs below, then cover them with the iron lid.
Afterward, tap the roots of the four fingers to return to position.

**The Finger-Palm Flying Five Dippers Method**
For treating illness, expelling evil, restraining souls, controlling spirits, concealing the spirit to shield the body, establishing prisons to pursue ghosts, protecting households and safeguarding the people—even for the ritual master to subdue gods, ghosts, evil demons, *wǎngliǎng* spirits, and malevolent specters—one must first fly and twist the Five Dippers to coil around the body, securing one’s form and stabilizing the hun and po. Only then may all methods be applied to restrain and subdue evil demons.
If, when expelling ghosts and evil, the afflicted shows slight improvement and the haunting spirit is clearly distant, then encircle the patient’s body with the Flying Five Dippers. Also, first burn named incense in a full circle, ensuring it is abundant and pure, free from any defiling *qi* that might profane the Dipper stars.
If the patient’s soul has long been claimed by the dead, do not draw it away to inhabit the body.
If, after deploying talismanic methods, the spirit does not return to cause harm that very day, cover and shield them all with the Flying Five Dippers.
When establishing a prison to summon ghosts or securing a household to pacify its inhabitants, apply the Flying Five Dippers’ technique to encircle the area. Carefully follow the illustrated manual, clearly understanding the finger joints. Thrice click the teeth, step the Dipper while holding the breath, silently recite the star names, and fly and twist accordingly.

**Hand-Seal and Gaze-Decision Diagram:**
**Seal of the Lord of the All-Heaven Method:** The four fingers must conceal the five claws. Used in memorials and transformations.

**Jade Clarity Seal:** Middle joint of the middle finger. For submitting memorials and commanding the Celestial Soldiers and Horses, or directing the Plague Envoys. Also called the Supreme Emperor Seal or Jade Emperor Seal, used similarly.

**Upper Clarity Seal:** Upper joint of the middle finger. For summoning Upper Clarity’s soldiers and horses. Also, beneath the middle fingernail: for inquiring about illness.

**Great Clarity Seal:** Lower joint of the middle finger.

**Northern Emperor Seal:** Middle finger and index finger together, tapping the middle joint of the thumb. For transforming into the Northern Emperor, commanding ghosts and spirits of the Three Realms, or entering and destroying temples.

**Heavenly Master Seal:** Thumb taps the first joint of the index finger.

**Original Master Seal:** Thumb taps the root of the index finger. For summoning divine generals, officers, soldiers, and local deities such as Merit Officers and Earth Gods.

**Purple Tenuity Seal:** The little finger crosses over the back of the four fingers to hook the thumb, tapping the third joint of the four fingers. The middle finger taps the horizontal lines of the palm. Also called the Subduing Evil Seal or Prison Seal. For restraining evil at the flank.

**Sun Lord Seal:** Upper joint of the second finger. For reciting the Sun Lord incantation and visualizing the Grand Yang to absorb *qi*.

**Moon Lord Seal

**Gate of Retention:** Tap the root of the middle finger.
**Sealing the Ghost Path:** Press the upper edge of the middle fingernail.
**From the Ghost Gate to the Heavenly Gate:** Trace from the root of the three fingers to the upper edge of the index fingernail.

**Ghost-Shackling Seal:** Thumb taps the root of the little finger.
**Alternative Seal:** Cross the index and middle fingers, then the ring and little fingers, opening a central cavity; thumb taps the *yin* position.

**Ghost-Restraining Seal:** Tap the first joint of the four fingers. Also used for entering plague-afflicted areas.

**Golden Blade Seal:** Thumb presses the index and middle fingers, tapping the *hai* position while extending the little finger straight. Compels ghosts to transmit messages.

**Dispatching Troops Seal:** Thumb presses the middle finger, tapping below the ring fingernail. Used for deploying troops, cavalry, and sending forth emissaries.

**Four Mountains Seal:** Middle finger taps the palm’s lines, thumb presses the middle finger, remaining fingernails straight. For crossing seas to capture ghosts and spirits.

**Celestial Stem Seal:** Tap the *yin* position in the first month, *mao* in the second, and so on for each month and hour. Used for summoning the twelve monthly and hourly *gongcao* (functionaries).

**Ghost-Pursuing Seal:** Curve the index and middle fingers; thumb taps the middle joint of the ring finger. For establishing prisons and pursuing ghosts.

**Gathering Wandering Spirits:** Tap the upper joint of the ring finger, visualizing the Four Mountains’ fire to gather and restrain ghostly bandits.

**Golden Nail Seal:** Middle finger taps the middle joint of the thumb.

**Seal-Opening Seal:** Thumb’s nail flicks the middle finger’s nail.
**Seal-Entering Seal:** Thumb flicks into the palm from beneath the middle fingernail.

**Guiding Ghosts to Prison Seal:** Release the *Golden City Seal*, then shift the middle finger to tap the palm’s center; thumb presses the four fingers, tapping the middle joint of the little finger.

**Golden City Seal:** Middle finger taps the central line of the thumb.

**Driving Away Hundreds of Specters Seal:** Press the underside of the left thumb’s nail with the right thumb’s nail.

**Locust-Driving Seal:** Tap the second joint of the middle finger.

**Cloud-Riding Seal:** Tap the second joint of the ring finger.

**Ghost-Slaying Seal:** From *yin*, tap upward to *chen* and flick outward.

*(The above seals are all performed with the left hand.)*

**Entering Temple Seal:** Index finger taps the root of the thumb.
**Temple-Destroying Seal:** Index finger taps the middle joint of the thumb, then the root of the little finger.

**Disease-Driving Seal:** Thumb directly taps the root of the index finger. Used when entering a sick person’s home.

**Ghost-Binding Seal:** Thumb taps the middle joint of the index finger. For divine generals to restrain ghosts.

**White Tiger Seal:** Thumb taps the index finger. For *jiading* (first and fourth celestial stems) to enter mountains and forests to drive away tigers.

**Azure Dragon Seal:** Thumb taps the middle joint of the middle finger. For crossing rivers.

**Soul-Pursuing Seal:** Thumb taps the root of the middle finger. For pursuing the souls of deceased family members.

**Ghost-Examining Seal:** Thumb taps below the middle fingernail. For interrogating strange phenomena, madness, and demonic possession.

**Sword-Pointing Seal:** Thumb taps the root of the four fingers. For dispatching *gongcao* (functionaries).

**Dragon-Releasing Seal:** Tap the second joint of the index finger, then release after completion.

*(The above seals are all performed with the right hand.)*

**Seven Stars Fundamental Seals**
**First Star Seal:** On the second joint of the left index finger.
**Second Star Seal:** On the first joint of the left index finger.
**Third Star Seal:** On the first joint of the left middle finger.
**Fourth Star Seal:** On the second joint of the left middle finger.
**Fifth Star Seal:** On the second joint of the left ring finger.
**Sixth Star Seal:** On the second joint of the left little finger.
**Seventh Star Seal:** On the third joint of the left little finger.

**Five Phases Governing Five Seals**
**Wood Seal:** Below the second joint of the left index finger.
**Jade Seal:** On the second proper joint.
**Fire Seal:** On the left side of the third joint of the left middle finger, at the center of the *wang* seal’s joint.
**Earth Seal:** On the third joint of the left ring finger.
**Metal Seal:** On the third joint of the *right* ring finger, below the Jade Seal’s lower half-rice (grain).
**Water Seal:** On the first joint of the left middle finger, above the *wang* seal’s upper half-rice (grain).

**Demon-Slaying Knife Branch Seal:** Tap the third joint of the left ring finger; the ghost will die.
**Dragon-Subduing Knife Branch Seal:** On the upper right side of the third joint of the left middle finger; bind tightly with silk thread, and the demon will die or submit.
**Earth Core Knife Branch Seal:** On the left side of the root joint of the left thumb; regularly mark with cinnabar.
**Earth Core Small Knife Branch Gate Seal:** The straight line near the wrist on the left palm is called the *Earth Graduation Seal* or *Grotto Heaven Seal*.

**Ghost-Slaying Knife Branch Seal:** On the right side of the third joint of the left little finger; tap urgently until blood nearly appears—this is auspicious. Tapping the left side releases it.

**Bandit-Destroying Knife Branch Seal:**
- For eastern incursions, use the *Wooden Man Knife Branch*.
- For southern incursions, use *Fire*.
- For western incursions, use *Metal*.
- For northern incursions, use *Water*.
- For incursions during the four seasons, use *Earth*.
*(The knife branches for *chen*, *xu*, *chou*, and *wei* represent the four seasons.)*
Tap this knife branch with the palm, then mark it with the corresponding directional color:
- *Wood Knife Branch* with gold-white.
- *Metal Knife Branch* with fire-red.
- *Water* with earth-yellow.
- *Fire* with water-black.
- *Earth* with wood-green.

**Seven Demons-Subduing, Two Ghosts-Beheading Knife Branch Seal:** On the left thumb, pinch above the index fingernail.

**Five Sufferings, Eight Difficulties, Nine Calamities, Hundred Diseases-Destroying Knife Branch Seal:**
- For those of *Metal* fate, tap the *Fire Knife Branch*.
- For those of *Wood* fate, tap the *Metal Knife Branch*.
- For those of *Water* fate, tap the *Earth Knife Branch*.
- For those of *Fire* fate, tap the *Water Knife Branch*.
- For those of *Earth* fate, tap the *Wood Knife Branch*.

**Three Officials Ghost-Slaying Seal:** Tap the lower middle of the left middle finger.

**Star-Summoning Seal:** On the first joint of the left ring finger. When the star enters its corresponding region, tap this seal to summon it.

**Heavenly Master’s Method for Writing Talismans and Visualizing *Gongcao* Divine Generals**
The left thumb represents the *yang qi* *gongcao*. When writing talismans to memorialize the Heavenly Bureau, visualize it as the presiding entity.

**Left Hand Index Finger as the Earth Gate *Gongcao*:**
For all talismans to suppress earth, slay earth *qi*, or subdue its influences, visualize it as the presiding entity.

**Left Hand Middle Finger as the Central Governor *Gongcao*, Overseer of the Five Peaks:**
For all talismans to restrain mountain and river spirits, banish demons, or inscribe talismans for the Five Peaks and Four Streams, visualize it as the presiding entity.

**Left Hand Ring Finger as the Welcoming and Sending *Gongcao*:**
For all talismans of harmony, amulets of aversion, or sealing talismans, visualize it as the presiding entity.

**Left Hand Little Finger as the Hundred Convergences *Gongcao*:**
For all talismans to suppress scalds, fires, stoves, flood dragons, *shen* serpents, and aquatic creatures, visualize it as the presiding entity.

**Tiger’s Mouth Crease (Below the Left Thumb):**
For talismans to sever all tiger and wolf influences, inscribe while holding the breath and visualizing its authority.

**Middle Crease of the Left Thumb:**
For talismans to repel plagues, sever misfortunes, block poisonous *qi*, and subdue lingering spirits or corpse demons, visualize it as the Great Slayer Spirit.

**Crease Near the Base of the Left Index Finger:**
For talismans to suppress official disputes, litigation, market misfortunes, or myriad strange creatures, visualize it as the Supreme Heavenly Master.

**Middle Joint of the Left Index Finger:**
For talismans to avert death, prevent harm from neighbors, or restrain construction disturbances.

**Upper Joint of the Left Index Finger:**
For talismans to suppress dogs, ease difficult births, expel retained placenta, or address stillborn children.

**Crease Near the Base of the Left Middle Finger as the Dike-Guardian Messenger:**
For talismans to counter curses, to be ingested by the targeted person.

**Middle Joint of the Left Middle Finger as the Crossbeam Messenger:**
For talismans to ascend altars, petition nobles, retrieve debts, or foster harmony.

**Crease Near the Base of the Left Ring Finger as the Perceptive Eye:**
For talismans to suppress nightmares, grinding teeth, restless sleep, or children’s night terrors and spiritual unease.

**Middle Joint of the Left Ring Finger as the Level Eye:**
For talismans to repel wild beasts entering dwellings or all manner of strange phenomena.

**Crease Near the Base of the Left Little Finger:**
For talismans to alleviate all pains, swellings, and boils.

**Middle Joints of the Left Five Fingers as the Subduing Spirit Envoys:**
For talismans to restrain all insects, rodents, flies, and clams.

**Upper Joint of the Left Little Finger as the Mighty Warrior Messenger:**
For talismans to suppress boats, rafts, wine, and vinegar.

**For all actions—walking, inquiring after illness, exorcising demons, entering temples, crossing rivers, or entering mountains—talismans must be inscribed while tapping the corresponding seal.**

**When setting out to inquire after illness or entering a household:**
Visualize the Two Envoys of Left and Right, the Twenty-Eight Constellations encircling the body, the Four Upright and Four Spirits positioned fore and aft. Envision oneself as Tianpeng, tapping the middle crease of the left middle finger.

**When traveling through mountains:**
Visualize the Azure Dragon and White Tiger at the left and right, the Day and Hour Governors fore and aft. Step the Dipper’s Pattern, tapping the *hai* position on the left hand.

**When entering mountains or ruined temples:**
Visualize the rank bestowed by the Register, imagining Tianpeng’s body towering fifty *zhang*, leading an army of ten thousand times ten thousand, with ghost-seizing envoys, Heavenly Soldiers, and the One Hundred Twenty Generals of the Northern Emperor’s Divine Shrine. Upon entering the temple’s rear, tap the first crease of the left thumb for the Ruined Temple Seal, and the second crease for the Temple Entry Seal.

**When crossing rivers:**
Visualize the Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water ahead, the Four Upright behind, and the officers and soldiers of one’s Register to the left and right. Tap the second joint of the right middle finger.

**To subdue a great tiger:**
Draw *qi*, tapping the *chen* position below the left hand as the Great Tiger Seal, and the tiger will cower, unable to meet one’s gaze.

**To subdue evil ghosts:**
Visualize oneself as Tianpeng, eyes closed, pressing the seal. Envision Tianpeng’s incantation with the Thirty-Six Generals arrayed fore and aft, Meng Zhang the Inspector leading troops, Ling Guang wielding the luminous standard, and Gou Chen Qiong Long standing at the center. Step the Seven Stars, perform the Seal-Pressing Rite to expel illness and drive out ghosts, tapping the *mao* position as the Ghost-Subduing Seal.

**To dispatch talismans to slay ghosts:**
Visualize oneself as the Heavenly Official of one’s Register, talisman in hand. Step the Pattern, summon the officers and soldiers, and command the Northern Emperor, Southern Dipper, and Great Primordial Slayer Youth. Decree the Dark Warrior Messenger of the Northern Emperor to receive the talisman and act accordingly. First dispatch the document, following the previously described Document-Dispatching Seal, then tap the crease below the right palm as the Ghost-Slaying Seal.

**When confronting evil adversaries in battle:**
Visualize oneself as General Zhou Wu, body towering ninety-six *zhang*, crowned with a celestial diadem and crimson headband, clad in vermilion robes, wielding the Jade Yang Standard, leading an army of three hundred thousand. Hold the talisman, step the Pattern, tapping the third crease of the left middle finger as the Battle Array Seal. To subdue the malevolent spirits and monstrous beings of the Five Directions, visualize oneself with unbound hair, sword in hand. Step the Pattern, using the Thunder Master and Lightning Master Seals, and the Seal of the Lord of the Universal Law. Then tap the center of the left palm to draw the Celestial Rigid *Qi*, with the Northern Dipper’s canopy overhead and the Four Spirits fore and aft. Next, tap below the lower joint of the thumb as the Five Stars within the *Kui* Constellation.

**When entering a patient’s home:**
Visualize oneself as the Heavenly Physician, commanding attendant youths to prepare medicine, with true youths following one’s movements. Tap the *yin* position on the right hand as the Illness Seal.

**For those harboring evil intentions, uttering curses, or employing suppressive talismans—once illness arises and no cure is sought:**
Follow this method: step the Dipper’s Pattern, face the Celestial Rigid to draw *qi*, inscribe the talisman, and apply it to the patient. Tap the *zi* position on the right hand as the Curse-Reversing Seal, causing the curser to suffer the backlash, rendering all arts ineffective.

*Here ends Scroll Eight of the* Supreme Aid to the State and Salvation of the People: Comprehensive Essentials of the True and Secret.
*Scroll Nine of the* Supreme Aid to the State and Salvation of the People: Comprehensive Essentials of the True and Secret.

Master of Mysteries Dongyou’s Compilation of the Primordial Wondrous School:
*Methods for Transmission, Establishment of Prisons, Ascension to the Celestial Terrace, Divination by the Dipper’s Canopy and Lamp, and the Push-Occultation Formulae*
*The Celestial Heart Orthodox Rites and Talismanic Contracts*

On talismanic tablets: these are made of wood, upon which talismans and incantations are inscribed. On iron contracts: these are fashioned from iron sheets, with orpiment as the ground and cinnabar for the contract’s text. Alternatively, yellow-flowered silk may be used, upon which the talismanic contract is written—iron is not strictly required, serving only to signify firmness and certainty. According to ancient methods, each carries its own significance, but in essence, they all manifest sincerity and eternal solidity.

Below are the traditional forms as transmitted:

**Iron Contract Form**
Forged from an iron sheet, three *cun* in diameter, sealed within the talismanic tablet. The talismans within the scroll are all inscribed in cinnabar.

**Talismanic Tablet and Contract Text Form**
Made of cypress wood, two *fen* thick, seven *cun* high, and nine *cun* wide.

In the year [X], cyclical year [Y], month [Z], the first day of the month being [A], hour [B], of this native place:
The Daoist of [X] Palace-Observatory, [Y] Prefecture, [Z] Commandery, [A] District, [B] Village, of the Great Ming State, [Name], born on the [X] day of the [Y] cyclical sign at [Z] hour, this day reverently presents himself at the gate of the Great Cavern Master of the Supreme Clarity, [Master’s Name], to receive the transmission of the *Supreme Clarity Northern Culmen Celestial Heart Orthodox Rites*, the numinous texts beneath the Dipper, talismanic tablets, and iron contracts, for the aid of the state and salvation of the people, the practice of the Daoist rites, the deliverance of sentient beings from suffering, the severance of demonic influences, the eradication of pestilence, and the salvation of the hidden and obscure.

Incantation: *Oṃ hūṃ hūṃ*.
All spirits bow their heads; evil demons submit to rectitude.
Should any dare to act with malice, they shall be reduced to dust.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the Celestial Emperor’s decree commands.

**Contract Text**

**Volume One:**
The disciple of transmission [Name], having received the great Daoist immortal arts, shall employ them to heal the ailments and sufferings of the people. Ever conduct yourself with uprightness, aligning your actions with the celestial will. Beware of deceit, flattery, or reckless misconduct.

**Volume One:**
The disciple of transmission [Name], in all undertakings, shall compare his own body to others’, honor and support his parents, reverently serve his masters and elders, and succor the impoverished, the aged, the sick, the orphaned, and the young. Upon encountering them, render aid without delay. Beware of greed or exploitation.

**Volume One:**
The disciple of transmission [Name], in practicing the celestial arts and immortal talismans, shall adhere strictly to the orthodox teachings, maintaining a sincere and solemn purity. Beware of careless disclosure or disrespect. Never dare to transmit these arts to others without the master’s decree. Should you violate this, your practice shall lack efficacy when the moment arrives.

**Memorandum:**
The aforementioned disciple [Name], by nature pure and void, reveres the great Dao and aspires to master the immortal arts, desiring to guide the lost multitudes. It is necessary to grant him talismanic tablets and an iron contract to guard his person, protect his life, and prolong his years. Respectfully invoke the Four Heavenly Kings, the Eight Classes of Dragons and Devas, the Nine Celestial Sovereigns, the Eight Great Vajras, the Dharma-protecting Deva Kings of the Ten Directions, the Generals of the Six Ding and Six Jia, the Celestial Ding Warriors, the Enforcers of the Five Thunders, the Lords of Wind and Rain, the Grotto-Palaces of the Five Sacred Peaks and Four Waterways, the renowned mountains, and all luminous deities of the Three Realms to constantly and vigilantly guard and protect him. As this disciple practices the Supreme Daoist arts, healing the people’s afflictions, dispelling pestilence, and severing demonic influences, may all his aspirations be fulfilled. This decree is hereby enacted.

**Imperial Decree from the Three Terraces:**
Whereas [Name], an officer of the Bureau for Expelling Demonic Influences, petitions to recommend [Name of Disciple], whose nature is pure and simple, who upholds goodness and cultivates sincerity, who constantly reveres the exalted immortals and ever takes refuge in the great Dao, and who harbors the aspiration to assist the state and save the people—desiring to transmit to him the *Celestial Heart Orthodox Rites* and talismans to protect his person and life, aid in the celestial transformation, and benefit all beings.

**Proclamation issued.**

**Petition of Gratitude for Appointment and Celestial Response (Template)**

Your servant [Name] humbly states: I have heard that the Great Dao is formless, nurturing and embracing the myriad transformations; the supreme virtue does not dominate, yet it revolves and governs the Three Origins. All things flourish and manifest, with the most numinous at their head. The unitive Dao is not apart from its root; the essence of guarding the One arises from sincerity.

Looking upon my own humble talents, I have been granted participation among the ranks of immortals. With awe and reverence, I bow my head again and again. I reverently consider the **Great Clarity Supreme Emperor**, the **Ancestral Master Supreme Clarity Supreme Emperor**, and the **Jade Clarity Supreme Emperor**, who holds the tally and governs the celestial mandate as the **Dao Lord of Nine Hundred Ninety-Nine Thousand Nine Hundred Million**; who opened the earth in the Red Brightness and Dragon Han eras as the **Scriptural Treasure of Ten Titles, Ten Perfected, and Hundred Spirits’ Source**.

The orthodox arts of the Three Heavens and the true talismans of the Five Emperors spread transformation, bestow auspiciousness, and extend their radiance in response to all things. Though I dwell in lowliness and baseness, I have presumptuously received the profound teachings, escaped the dusty world, and rejoiced in being ranked among the registers of immortals. How dare I not uphold the celestial precepts above and fulfill human sentiments below, taking the relief of suffering as my heart and the repayment of kindness as my duty?

I respectfully present this petition in gratitude, daring to intrude upon Your Celestial Majesty. My humble feelings are overwhelmed with longing for the sagely response, trembling with awe.

Your servant [Name], with awe and reverence, bows his head again and again, respectfully states.

Petition presented on the [Day] day of the [Month] month of the [Year of the Great Era], by your servant [Full Title and Name].
