**Method for Establishing the Celestial Prison**

When establishing the Celestial Prison, first select a location according to the directional guidelines and prepare a pure chamber, ensuring it is secure and tightly sealed. Sweep and purify it thoroughly before constructing the prison.

**Directional Formula**
In the first month, [build] at *zi*; the fifth and ninth months share the same [direction].
In the second month, the sixteenth [day] is in the Rabbit Garden.
The third and seventh [months], the eleventh [day], are within the Horse Pen.
The fourth and eighth [months], the twelfth [day], enter the Chicken Coop.

When establishing the prison, first transform the spirit. Then take three steps in the *ding* register, visualizing two blue-clad youths holding sword seals standing to the left and right. Assume the role of the **Expelling Demonic Influences Bureau Envoy**, wearing the **Interlocking Harmony Crown** and the **Fish-Scale Robe**. Hold the **Samādhi Fire Bell Sword** in the right hand and the **Lord of the Celestial Law Seal** in the left.

Within the prison chamber, step through the **Seven Stars Register**, having an assistant follow each step to insert bamboo stakes. Then take a left-twisted hemp rope and strike each star in sequence.

First, write two **Summoning Ghost Talismans**, one in cinnabar and one in ink. Attach five paper coins to the front of the prison. Burn the talismans while visualizing the **Summoning Ghost Talisman Envoy** in the form of a swift runner. Then form the **Summoning Ghost Mudra** (the mudra is found in the eighth scroll) and recite the incantation:

> *"Celestial Prison, numinous and bright,*
> *By the Emperor’s command, act with might.*
> *The Celestial Law’s decree is stern,*
> *Seize and bind the demonic, show no concern.*
> *Swiftly, swiftly, as the law ordains!"*

Take a strip of paper and write in cinnabar:
*"By order of Mount Tai, the attending divine generals are to apprehend all malevolent ghosts and spirits causing harm and bring them to this prison."*

Above this text, write the title and rank of the ritual master in one line, followed by a decorative flourish. Above the flourish, write *"By the Emperor’s Decree."*

Recite the previous **Celestial Prison Incantation**, then form the **Supreme Emperor Mudra** and the **Celestial Soldier Mudra**, and affix the paper to the bamboo stake of the Celestial Prison.

Visualize black silk transforming into dark clouds, and the **Northern Dipper** manifesting as the **Dark Celestial Prison**. On yang days, use lime; on yin days, use charcoal ash, each seven inches wide.

Establish the prison beneath the **Military Brilliance Star**, making it round and twelve inches in diameter. Use nine green bamboo stalks, each four feet and nine inches long. The stars and prison are delineated with fine ash, and bamboo stakes mark each position. The bamboo serves as the upright prison officers.

Use nine strips of black silk, each nine inches long and one inch two-tenths wide, tied seven inches below the top of the bamboo stakes. Write the names of the Eight Stars in cinnabar on the black silk.

The prison is closed by day and opened by night. Take care to avoid disturbance, and do not use lamps or candles.

When treating illness, point the register toward the patient’s bedchamber. For other matters, point the register toward the monthly branch.

If after two nights no traces appear in the Celestial Prison, repeat the previous written instructions to urge the attending divine generals. Affix a large inscription of *"Celestial Prison"* to the door of the prison chamber.

Whether there is a response or not, proceed according to the circumstances, following the **Yang Dao Public Law** without yielding to human sentiment.

The establishment of the prison must not be witnessed by others; only the ritual master should enter and exit regularly.

The **Five Prison Masters of the Expelling Demonic Influences Bureau** and the **Direct Altar Earth Deity** must first be offered paper money and horses.

---

**Summoning Ghost Talisman Formula**

When writing the talisman, face the monthly branch. When burning it, recite the prayer:
*"All malevolent spirits causing harm, swiftly return to your origin and be seized!"*

---

**Method for Verifying Ghost Traces in the Prison**

If the ghost is fierce and violent, it will manifest in its true form. If it is a yin and subtle ghost, only traces will appear.

If the patient’s life is fated to end, a double trace will appear beneath their natal star in the prison, indicating the arrival of the **Soul-Summoning Envoy**. Examine this carefully and promptly dissolve the prison.

- **Chicken traces** indicate a visiting death.
- **Human traces**, large or small, indicate the **Five Penetrations**.
- **Cat, rat, or fox traces** indicate mountain spirits.
- **Human hands or feet** indicate fierce and violent mountain deities.
- **Snake or earthworm traces** indicate kitchen gods, Buddhist statues, earth deities, altar mats, or ancestral ghosts.
- **Goose or duck traces** with bloodstains indicate ghosts of violent death.
- **Raised mounds** indicate temple or monastic spirits causing harm.
- **Small traces like knife cuts** indicate disturbances from construction in the household.
- **Mule, donkey, ox, or horse traces**, large, indicate household **gu** poison; small, indicate neighboring **gu** poison.
- **Rope-drag marks** indicate hanging ghosts.
- **Chaotic ant-like traces** indicate **consumptive corpse ghosts**.
- **Traces like a small finger, uniform at both ends**, indicate **tomb-curse ghosts**; smaller ones indicate disturbances from mountains, forests, slopes, or ponds.
- **Traces resembling a small finger with one end larger** indicate **water ghosts**.

---

**Method for Dissolving the Celestial Prison**

**Method for Dissolving the Celestial Prison**

Transform the deity into the **Director of the Demon-Quelling Court**, commanding the ghosts and spirits to first appear at the **Star Altar**, then submit their case in accordance with the law, petitioning **Mount Tai** for resolution. Issue a writ to the divine generals to take them into custody and escort them beneath the mountain, where each shall be sealed with an official document. Once completed, offer **paper money and spirit horses**, then instruct the two divine generals to order the generals dispatched from **Mount Tai** and those under the **City God** to swiftly take charge of the malevolent ghosts and spirits afflicting the household, bringing them before the court to await further command. Upon their arrival, issue the following instructions:

First, bestow upon them **wine, food, paper money, and spirit horses** according to their rank. Then, hand over the writs for their custody and escort, and have an attendant dismantle the prison and burn it, scattering the ashes into the river. The format for the petition is detailed in **Scroll Ten**.

**Method for Erecting the Terrace of Ascension to Heaven**

Examine the petition carefully, ensuring the grievances are clearly stated, and proceed accordingly. If the cause is not precisely identified, send an official document to **Mount Tai**, requesting that divine generals, along with the local **City God**, the **Household Deities**, the **Five Paths**, the village and community temple spirits, and all other relevant deities—both within and beyond the household—thoroughly investigate: What manner of person is this? Which sorcerer or shaman aided them? At which ghostly shrine did they make their vows? What offerings did they pledge? Who was wrongfully killed, and why has their grievance not been resolved?

The court shall then construct a **Terrace of Ascension to Heaven** at the afflicted person’s home. The divine generals are to escort the responsible spirits to the terrace. Upon arrival, proceed with the rite, addressing the aggrieved soul thus:

*"Disciple [Name]—you and I once shared enmity. Why do you persist in clinging to the netherworld, bringing harm to this extent? Now, [Name] lies stricken with illness. For your sake, I have prepared grand offerings—**vegetarian feasts, rituals, scriptures, paper money, and spirit horses**—to aid your ascent to heaven from this terrace. Henceforth, you must reform your heart and amend your ways. Cease your former obstinacy. Should you defy this command, your grievances shall persist through kalpas, and you will be unable to attain rebirth. If you refuse my words, I shall bind you in the **Dipper Prison**, shatter your form and shadow, and reduce you to dust. Swiftly obey this decree!"*

Once the ritual transformation is complete, issue a writ to the divine generals, entrusting them to escort the spirits to **Mount Tai**. Enlist the **local earth deities** along the route to ensure their safe passage, delivering them before the **Prefect of the Underworld**. There, petition the Prefect to swiftly report the case, annul the grievance, retrieve the written complaint, and permit the soul’s ascent to heaven.

The **Terrace of Ascension to Heaven** shall be constructed in the **direction of vital qi**, using **sweet flag, sandalwood, and aloeswood** mixed with wine and water to form three layers of sand:
- The base: **two feet wide, three inches high**.
- The middle: **one foot five inches wide, two inches high**.
- The top: **one foot wide, seven inches high**.

Atop the upper layer, place a mirror centered over the heart. At the four corners of the middle layer, set four lamps. Before the terrace, light the Seven Star Lamps, their stems pointing toward the sick person’s chamber. On the terrace, inscribe a placard with the words: *Terrace of Ascension to Heaven*. Additionally, arrange a small table bearing seasonal fruits, incense, lamps, tea, and wine as offerings. Behind the table, place a plaque three fingers wide and six inches tall, inscribed: *Reverent bows to the Supreme Emperor of Highest Clarity, Ancestral Master*. The plaque shall be crafted from *fuyan* wood. Then, recite the petition three times, stating the matter’s intent. Humbly implore the Supreme Emperor of Highest Clarity, Ancestral Master, to issue a special decree and act in accordance with this petition.

**Design of the Terrace of Ascension to Heaven**
**Method for the Protective Canopy (Huagai)**
First, submit a memorial to the Celestial Emperor, petitioning the Seven Kings of the Northern Dipper and Mount Tai to dispatch orders to the local City God, who shall assign divine generals alongside the household’s Controller of Destiny and local earth deities to vigilantly guard the persons under the protective canopy, ensuring no misfortunes befall them within the year. Once the ritual dispatch is complete, the memorial’s format is provided in the subsequent scroll.

Next, take an iron pillar as thick as a thumb, twelve inches long, symbolizing the twelve months. Engrave seven segments upon it, representing the seven palaces of the Northern Dipper’s Seven Kings, visualized as a jeweled hall of golden steps and jade chambers. Prepare a small, purified vase to hold a talisman, and an iron plate seven inches long and two inches wide, inscribed with the *Three Luminaries Talisman* to consecrate it.

**Design of the Iron Pillar**
**Design of the Iron Plate Talisman**
The talisman shall be inscribed on a piece of yellow silk twelve inches long. At the top, inscribe the Three Terraces; at the bottom, the Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper, symbolizing the Seven Kings’ palaces. Beneath each corresponding star, write the disciple’s name, along with the year, month, day, and hour.

**Design of the Silk Talisman**
Place the silk talisman into the vase, along with the protective canopy fee corresponding to the number of persons covered. Bury a large vase beneath the canopy’s location, and position the small vase in the *Hua Gai* direction for the current month, digging a hole twelve inches deep to inter it. The *Hua Gai* directions are provided in the subsequent scroll.

Thereafter, perform the divine transformation, pacing the Seven Star Net, employing the *Heavenly Ding* mudra. Begin at *Greedy Wolf* and conclude at *Breaking Army* to enact the prohibition. While pacing the net, recite the incantation:

*Mighty Northern Dipper, radiant Dipper’s handle star.
Greedy Wolf wields malice, devouring ghosts and consuming essence.
Majestic Gate shines resplendent, illuminating with brilliance.
Wealth Star races through mist, commanding talismanic soldiers.
Rosy clouds surge through Literary Star, light piercing Integrity Star.
Mighty Martial Star, true person’s auxiliary star.
Great Sage of the Celestial Net, swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

Deposit the fee and talisman into the vase. When placing the protective canopy, recite the incantation:

*Heaven is my canopy, Earth my support.
The Northern Dipper’s suspended stars are my raiment.
I shelter my disciple, [Name], and [number] persons,
within the Seven Primes of the Northern Dipper,
in the courtyard of flowing fire.
Neither stems nor branches shall harm them.
Those who aid me are the Great Yang.
Those who oppose me shall perish.*

Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!
Bury the vase with the prohibition charm, plant the iron talisman at the front, and set the iron pillar at the rear.
Then visualize the Four Heavenly Gate Kings stationed at the four corners, and imagine the person sheltered by the canopy residing in the Palace of the Seven Kings.
Next, envision the City God dispatching soldiers to encircle and patrol in protection.
When done, click the teeth and withdraw. At year’s end, open the canopy and prepare wine, food, paper money, and horses to offer to the sacred assembly within the talisman, the Three Terraces of the Northern Dipper, and the stars of one’s natal destiny. According to one’s means, hold a thanksgiving jiao ritual to repay their grace and protection.
Also reward the patrolling divine generals and their troops, as well as the local earth god. Submit a formal document to each, dispatching them back to their respective peaks to report completion.
Once the generals have received and acknowledged the troops, request a confirming response.

**Decree-Character Longevity Lamp Formula**
Forty-nine lamps for the *Decree* character, thirty-six for the *Extend* character, and twenty-four for the *Life* character.
For treating pestilence, madness, and demonic afflictions, or for thanksgiving rituals, light these lamps. They may also be lit regularly to repel plague and extend life.
Use lime to mark the positions, then place and light the lamps.
First, pace the Seven Stars’ Net and recite the incantation:

*Northern Dipper’s seven stars, jade perfected immortals divine.
Greedy Wolf and Majestic Gate, guard me with eternal glory.
Wealth Star and Literary Star, grant me wisdom and clarity.
Integrity Star and Martial Star, preserve my peace and tranquility.
Breaking Army and Auxiliary Stars, shield my body and form.
Ever dwell in fortune’s embrace, forever secure in blessed years.
Inscribe me in the register of life, erase my name from death’s scroll.
Spirit pure, qi pristine, penetrating the hidden and obscure.
Command demons, seize ghosts, all malevolent spirits crushed and overthrown.
Cultivating Dao, refining truth, may my wish be fulfilled.
The Seven Primes lend their protection, ascending to the Purple Court on high.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

Employ the Five Thunder Hand Seal, flash the eyes three times to fill the room with lightning, then form the Triggering Seal and recite the Lamp-Lighting Incantation:

*By the Emperor’s decree, the Dipper’s lamps are lit.
The Seven Kings descend to illuminate and guard all beings.
Left and right, the Auxiliary Stars manifest their mighty power.
Heavenly Marshal Tianpeng commands the celestial troops.
Envoys of the Five Thunders, the Six Jia and Six Ding spirits,
Great Sage of the Dark Warrior, the Three Stars of the Terrace.
Banish illness, dispel misfortune, execute and slay demonic spirits.
The three hun souls fortify the body, the seven po souls rest in peace.
Those who defy this decree shall perish; those who uphold it shall prosper.
A single point of Longevity’s light illumines body and home.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

Then light the lamps. If a person’s illness lingers and resists medical treatment, these lamps should be lit.
First, use sixty-four ounces of pure oil, one ounce of wood, one ounce of licorice, one fen of borneol, one ounce of peach twigs (each nine inches long), half an ounce of realgar, and half an ounce of cinnabar. Except for the cinnabar, steep all ingredients in the oil for seven days, facing the direction of Longevity. Guard it with the Great Black Destruction Talisman, and seal the bottle’s mouth with the Three Lights Talisman. When the days are complete, remove the herbs, pour the oil into a clean lamp, and coat the lamp’s green rim thickly with cinnabar.
From the patient’s natal star, hold the breath, pace the Net, and light the lamp as before, directing the Dipper’s handle toward the patient’s bedroom.
Do not use paper wicks; ignite the lamp with pine resin. Do not leak qi.
If, on that night, the lamp corresponding to the patient’s natal star extinguishes first, inform the household: the case is beyond saving.
If the lamp burns brightly and moths fly into it, the person will recover and the ghost will be subdued.
If moths live but the lamp dies, the ghost thrives and the person weakens.
Carefully observe these signs at the time. If the lamp dims but does not extinguish, the person’s life is not in danger—only the illness remains unresolved.

**Lamp Divination for Household Fortune and Misfortune**
On the six assembly nights, arrange the ritual as before to divine outcomes. Bright lamps signify good fortune; dim lamps, misfortune.
- **Blue light**: Hidden corpse qi.
- **Red light**: Bloodshed or calamity.
- **White light**: Mourning or external bereavement.
- **Black light**: Illness or legal troubles.
- **Yellow light**: Pestilential qi.
- **Long, steady flame**: Auspicious.
- **Flame forming a wheel**: Inauspicious.
- **Dims then brightens**: Impending misfortune.

**Canopy of Flowers Method**
- **First month**: Zi direction.
- **Second month**: Chou direction.
- **Third month**: Yin direction.
- **Fourth month**: Mao direction.
- **Fifth month**: Chen direction.
- **Sixth month**: Si direction.
- **Seventh month**: Wu direction.
- **Eighth month**: Wei direction.
- **Ninth month**: Shen direction.
- **Tenth month**: You direction.
- **Eleventh month**: Xu direction.
- **Twelfth month**: Hai direction.

Each month, in its designated direction, erect the canopy and the Platform of Heavenly Birth, and light the Longevity Lamp—this is called the *Canopy of Flowers*.

**Purple Tenuity’s Seven Governors: Method of the Living Celestial Luminaries and Heavenly Rigidity**
Where Heavenly Rigidity descends, all malevolent spirits and baleful stars flee in terror, daring not to confront it.
The Seven Stars revolve day and night across the azure sky,
With the Dipper’s bowl at the head and Rigidity at the tail’s edge.
One day contains twelve hours; within twelve hours, Rigidity begins at Xu.
*Formula*:
Every night at the Xu hour, place Rigidity at Xu.
Align it with the month’s branch, shifting one position per hour.
Repeat this cycle without end; the method remains unchanged for ten thousand years.

**Ancient Heavenly Rigidity Method**
Each month, Rigidity is always added to Xu; each hour, it begins at Breaking Army.
Before the Sun passes its palace, start at Hai.
After the Sun passes its palace, start at Xu.
Always begin with the month’s branch, starting from Hai or Xu, and at the correct hour, Heavenly Rigidity’s movement becomes apparent.

**Determining the Sun’s Direction**
In the first and ninth months, exit Yi and enter Geng.
In the second and eighth months, seek the Rabbit and enter You’s rigidity.
In the third and seventh months, ascend Jia and enter Xin’s position.
In the fourth and sixth months, emerge from Yin and arrive at Xu’s land.
In the fifth month, enter Qian from Gen.
In the tenth month, the body enters Kun from Xun.
In the eleventh and twelfth months, reside at Chen—
This is the Celestial Heart harmonizing with the Sun.

**Determining the Moon’s Direction**
In the first and ninth months, begin at Chou’s position.
In the second and eighth months, return to the Water Palace of Zi.
In the third and seventh months, Hai’s direction; in the fourth and sixth, Xu.
In the fifth month, the Western Heaven’s true return to the East.
In the eleventh and twelfth months, reside at Chen.
Count forward by hours, retreat one palace.

When the Moon’s radiance descends to illuminate,
This is where moonlight and qi converge in union.

**Method for Entering the Divination Stance**
The art of entering the divination stance is wondrous and profound:
Align the Moon’s General with the hour at the position’s apex.
Observe which spirit shares the same place,
Then invoke the person’s origin from the day’s stem.
The subduer becomes the origin, judged by its vigor;
Examine closely within the Five Phases.
Discern the spirits and generals to detail fortune or misfortune,
Then scrutinize the visitor to perceive the truth.
The moving is the guest, the unmoving the host;
The generals represent wealth—observe their clashes.
If the host subdues wealth, wealth remains inert;
If wealth subdues the host, they contend for office.
If the guest subdues the host, they come to demand goods;
If the host subdues the guest, the guest departs displeased.
When aligned with one’s native place, wealth remains inert;
If they harmonize, listen for joy and reunion.
Two Woods as lines make wealth hard to obtain;
Two Earths together bring delay.
Two Metals clashing bring no harmony;
Two Fires bring disaster, all affairs ruined.
Two Waters are most auspicious;
Water entering Fire unsettles the wife.
Metal entering Wood’s domain stirs quarrels;
Fire entering Metal’s domain brings hardship.
Wood entering Earth leads to imprisonment;
Earth entering Water sparks disputes over fields.
When the above subdues the below, it comes from without;
When the below subdues the above, it turns outward.
Commonly take *yin* and *shen* as noble guests;
*zi*, *wu*, *mao*, and *you* for feasts of wine and food.
*si* and *hai* must come to demand goods;
*chen* and *xu* bring lawsuits and lingering strife.
*chou* pertains to copper, iron, gold, and silver;
*xiaoji* concerns women and wasted wine and food.
When the four positions harmonize, all affairs are auspicious—
No need to speak of clashes within.
This is Sun Bin’s true *jiazi* method,
Brought from heaven and earth into the palm’s transmission.

**Method for Determining Illness**
To inquire about a person’s age and the root of their illness,
Align the Moon’s General with the hour and transmit to their fate.
Encountering Wood indicates wind and qi disorders;
*you* Metal’s fullness connects to the lungs.
Meeting Fire generates heat both inside and out;
Seeing Water brings cold illness to the waist.
Encountering Earth with clashes causes sores and swelling;
Harmony eases the body’s afflictions.
To see an eagle’s circling, seek the auspicious *chou*;
Observe alongside the noble spirit’s position.

**Alternative Method**
The method for divining illness requires discussion:
Align the Moon’s General with the hour at the position’s apex.
The four cardinal points (*zi*, *wu*, *mao*, *you*) speak of severe suffering;
The four seasonal beginnings (*yin*, *shen*, *si*, *hai*) are celestial afflictions.
The four transitions (*chen*, *xu*, *chou*, *wei*) define chronic illness;
Only by observing clashes can one judge its depth.
Subduing Metal causes wheezing; subduing Earth brings bloating;
Subduing Water brings many hardships.
Subduing Wood harms the liver;
Subduing Fire affects the heart.
This is the immortals’ true esoteric formula—
Sun Bin’s ten methods, not to be transmitted lightly.

**Method for Determining Life and Death in Illness**
Discern life and death from the visitor’s direction;
The noble spirit and Moon’s General are used together.
If the noble spirit and general clash,
Know the illness is grave and difficult to halt.
If the person’s origin and position are further harmed,
Stupor and sinking indicate it is hard to cure.
Fate and wealth injured by Wood or Metal qi—
This text’s secrets align with the immortals’ intent.

**Method for Determining Life and Death by Ghostly Limits**
*Jiazi* and *jiawu* transmit through the Nine Palaces;
*Yigeng* and *bingen* follow the Eight Paths of the year.
*Bingsin* and *gengxin* occupy the Seven Positions of *yin* and *shen*;
*Dingren* and *renren* speak of the Six Paths of *mao* and *you*.
*Wugui* and *guikui* hold the Five Positions of *chen* and *xu*;
*Jihai*’s Four Killers trace to the root.
The year and fate align with the day’s branch and stem—
See which palace and constellation they connect to.
One is *kan*, two is Earth, three resides in Thunder;
Four is Wind, five is unspeakable.
Six seeks *ding*’s companionship, passing through seven dwellings;
Nine Fire Immortals traverse eight mountains.
At *Lichun*, *gen* flourishes on the mountain’s peak;
The eight nodes follow the hexagrams’ flowing sequence.
Flourishing, resting, conceived, or waning—no other matters;
Imprisoned or dead in *fei*—midnight brings sorrow.
If within this there is decline or encountering ghosts,
Prepare the coffin and head to the barren hills.

**Removal Method**
Water one, Fire two, Wood three,
Metal four, Earth five, six seven eight nine ten—
Black, red, green, white, yellow.
Heaven removes one, Earth removes two,
Humans remove three and four, hours remove four and five,
Movement removes five and six, *jia* removes six and seven,
Stars remove seven and eight, hexagrams remove eight and nine,
Luminaries remove nine—what remains is the lifespan.
Combine with the ghost’s number, discerning by position
The color of their garments and eyes.

**Method for Locating Hidden Corpses**
Finding hidden corpses is not difficult—
This method originally holds wondrous subtlety.
Align the Moon’s General with the hour to know the place;
Beneath *Ludu*, the hidden corpse lies.
*Yigeng* and *bingsin* seek the direction;
*Dingren* and *renren* lie beside *qian* at *hai*.
On *jiaji* days, beneath *xiaoji*,
Beneath *Ludu* is the dry spring.
*Ludu*’s *wuji* hides the corpse;
Where it subdues *Lu*, the response is hard to obtain.

**Method for Divining the Spirit Behind Afflictions**
When someone comes to divine the spirit’s intent,
Align the Moon’s General with the hour and seek the direction.
*hai* is for parents, the Northern *Tai* Mountain spirit;
*si* is the hearth’s household spirit causing affliction.
*zi* is the ditch dragon, the Dark Warrior spirit;
*wu* is scalding harm, vexation in the heart.
*chou* is the hidden corpse, the River Earl’s spirit;
*wei* is the inner palace or self-hanging.
*yin* is for blades and weapons, the Tree Dragon spirit;
*shen* is for vows and merits causing affliction.
*mao* is for those who died away from home;
*you* is for Buddhist statues and birth-death ghosts.
*chen* is the Celestial Heart, the household spirit;
*xu* is for offending the household earth deity.

**Diagram for Divining the Spirit in Illness**
Whenever examining illness, simply ask the visitor:
In which direction does the afflicted person lie?
For example, if in *dui*, know it is the household spirit of the youngest girl.
The rest follow this pattern—
At the time, write talismans, draft petitions,
Or use charms to expel and drive away.

**Method for Auspicious and Inauspicious Hours for Talismans**
On *jiayi* days, in *yin* and *mao*.
On *bingding* days, in *chen* and *si*.
On *wuji* days, in *wu* and *wei*.
On *gengxin* days, in *shen* and *you*.
On *renkui* days, in *xu* and *hai*.
On the above days, performing talismans to treat illness is forbidden—greatly inauspicious.

**Method for Using Talismans to Treat Illness**
When someone requests a talisman, set the hour,
Align the Moon’s General with the hour and inquire of the ill person.
Transmit to their fate, observe clashes and flourishing,
Carefully examine the qi’s movement at the established time.
Take *hai* as the first month,
Clearly distinguish the twelve spirits in reverse order.

If no clashes appear in the patient’s fate,
Talismanic water at the proper hour brings peace and tranquility.

**Miscellaneous Taboos for Talisman Use Across the Twelve Months**

| Month: | 1st | 2nd | 3rd | 4th | 5th | 6th | 7th | 8th | 9th | 10th | 11th | 12th |
|--------|-----|-----|-----|-----|-----|-----|-----|-----|-----|------|------|------|
| Great Destructor | *xu* | *si* | *wu* | *wei* | *yin* | *mao* | *chen* | *hai* | *zi* | *chou* | *shen* | *you* |
| Lesser Destructor | *chou* | *xu* | *wei* | *chen* | *chou* | *xu* | *wei* | *chen* | *chou* | *xu* | *wei* | *chen* |
| Celestial Prison | *mao* | *yin* | *chou* | *zi* | *hai* | *xu* | *you* | *shen* | *wei* | *wu* | *si* | *chen* |
| Earthly Prison | *xu* | *you* | *shen* | *wei* | *wu* | *si* | *chen* | *mao* | *yin* | *chou* | *zi* | *hai* |
| Celestial Soul | *ding* | *bing* | *yi* | *jia* | *gui* | *ren* | *xin* | *geng* | *ding* | *bing* | *yi* | *jia* |
| Earthly Corpse | *gui* | *ren* | *xin* | *geng* | *ding* | *bing* | *yi* | *jia* | *gui* | *ren* | *xin* | *geng* |
| Celestial Thief | *you* | *yin* | *wei* | *zi* | *yi* | *yi* | *xu* | *mao* | *jia* | *chou* | *wu* | *hai* |
| Monthly Virtue | *ding* (☷) | *kun* (☷) | *ren* (☰) | *xin* (☰) | *qian* (☰) | *jia* (☰) | *gui* (☶) | *gen* (☶) | *bing* (☶) | *jia* (☴) | *xun* (☴) | *geng* (☴) |
| Monthly Destructor | *chou* | *xu* | *wei* | *chen* | *chou* | *xu* | *wei* | *chen* | *chou* | *xu* | *wei* | *chen* |

Whenever a month’s Great Destructor, Lesser Destructor, or Monthly Destructor is in effect, writing or deploying talismans is inauspicious—best to suppress malevolent forces, foxes, and owls for good fortune.

When visiting a patient’s home, avoid entering from the direction of the Earthly Prison. Neither should the patient face the direction of the Prison when the master treats them.

If a person’s fate aligns with the Celestial Soul or Earthly Corpse, talismans must not be written nor sent on that day—violation brings death.

During the month when the Celestial Soul or Earthly Corpse direction is active, do not drive talismans into the earth—transgression causes crop and silkworm failure, and all affairs turn inauspicious.

For example, those born under *ding*, *gui*, *jia*, or *geng* must not write talismans for others in the first or fourth month, nor provide talismans to those born under *ding* or *gui*—this is the principle.

When the Monthly Virtue direction is active, move the patient to that position for treatment—auspicious.

**Seasonal Position of the Celestial Unity**
Spring: *mao*

Summer: *wu*.
Autumn: *you*.
Winter: *zi*.

Whenever writing talismans, if the downward illumination falls upon the Noble One’s direction, it is most auspicious. Alternatively, arrange a Celestial Unity seat, placing talismans upon it according to the direction’s color and qi number, and perform rites. Spring: nine; summer: three; autumn: seven; winter: five. Once measured, entrust them to the spirits for verification.

**The Supreme Pervasive Aid to the State and Salvation of the People: Comprehensive Essentials of the True and Secret, Scroll Nine—End**

**The Supreme Pervasive Aid to the State and Salvation of the People: Comprehensive Essentials of the True and Secret, Scroll Ten**
*Compiled by Master Dongyou of the Profound Dao, Yuan Miaozong*
*Standard Documents for Dispatch from the Northern Culmen Bureau of Expelling Evil*

According to the ritual statutes, whenever matters arise, one must submit documents to the numinous deities and memorialize the divine perfected—this is the essential framework. The forms and standards of documents must be prepared without omission. Here, the requisite dispatch formats are revised and presented to ensure no deficiencies.

For all matters requiring dispatch documents, these are not exhaustively listed. If any are missing, compare them to analogous formats, adapt them to the circumstances, and issue them accordingly.

**Format for Petition by the Transmitter of the Dao**
[From] Disciple [Name], of [such-and-such] village, ward, or market in [such-and-such] prefecture or county.

Respectfully presents the ritual offering, specifying its type and quantity. With utmost sincerity, [the disciple] humbly submits this petition.

**Petition from a Disciple Under the Venerable Master of Supreme Clarity**

To the Venerable Master of Supreme Clarity, [Name], [this disciple] humbly vows to seek the transmission of the *Northern Dipper Heavenly Heart Orthodox Daoist Method*. With steadfast resolve, [I] aspire to assist in the transformative work of Heaven, aid the state and save the people, heal the sick and succor the perilous, and sever all demonic and heterodox influences. After receiving and practicing this method, [I] shall follow the master’s guidance without fail, never daring to transmit it to unworthy persons or employ it in defiance of the Great Dao. Should [I] ever transgress, [I] beseech that [my] own life be extinguished first, and thereafter the sins of seven generations be visited upon [me].

[I] humbly petition the Seven Primal Lofty Perfected and the Sacred Emperor of the Eastern Marchmount to bestow compassionate regard and grant permission for this transmission.

Respectfully submitted.
[Date] by [Name], [Rank/Title].

---

**Format for Petition of Recommendation by Disciples Seeking a Master**

[From] [Name], of [such-and-such] village, ward, or hamlet in [such-and-such] prefecture or county.

Previously, on [date], [I] submitted a petition and personally presented myself at the abode of the Venerable Master of Supreme Clarity, [Name], to seek the transmission of the *Heavenly Heart Orthodox Daoist Method*. With steadfast resolve, [I] aspired to assist in the transformative work of Heaven, aid the state and save the people, heal the sick and succor the perilous, and sever all demonic and malevolent influences. Having received the master’s gracious permission and set a date for the submission of [my] name, [I] was commanded to seek out a renowned master of the Dao in accordance with the method and secure a recommendation for transmission.

Reflecting humbly, [I] was born fortunate to dwell in the Central Kingdom, yet [my] heart has long abided beyond the realm of forms. [I] have repeatedly sought masters among those known to [me], and only now, pouring forth sincerity, have [I] encountered a luminous guide. Recently, with reverence...

To the esteemed master,

Having entered your discipleship, [I] have witnessed the utmost refinement of the transmitted method, the flourishing of the Great Dao, the salvation of the people and all beings, and profound deliverance. With reverence, [I] now submit myself to your tutelage, humbly seeking your recommendation. Should [I] be so fortunate as to be accepted, [I] dare not fail to steel [my] resolve, carving [your teachings] into bone and inscribing them upon flesh, devoting [myself] wholeheartedly to cultivation. Above all, [I] shall strive to repay the grace of your guidance—how boundless would be [my] fortune!

With utmost sincerity, [I] present this petition for your consideration and await your sacred decree.

Dated the ___ day of the ___ month, ___ year of the reign of ___.

Submitted by your disciple, [Name], of [State, County, Township, Village, Ward].

---

**Petition Formula for Disciples Seeking Transmission of the Daoist Method**

[State, County, Township, Village, Ward, Name of Guarantor, Disciple’s Name]

The undersigned, [Name], born on the ___ day of the ___ month, ___ year, at ___ hour, under the governance of the Northern Dipper’s Star Lord ___. With reverence, [I] present nine taels of gold, a pair of gold rings, and one bolt of plain silk as tokens of sincerity. Four taels of black silk thread are offered in lieu of shorn hair; seven taels of cinnabar, in lieu of blood sacrifice. [I] now prostrate myself before the esteemed Master [Name], seeking transmission of the *Heavenly Heart Orthodox Daoist Method*, with the intent to assist in the transformative work of Heaven and serve the state by saving the people.

Reflecting upon the fleeting nature of this mortal realm, [I] have long lamented the fragility of this body. Ashamed of [my] inability to dispel harm and lacking the means to promote benefit, [I] have grown lax in cultivation, and my dread deepens. Who could have foreseen that after countless kalpas, [I] would encounter this auspicious meeting today?

[I] have heard that you, Master, do not obstruct the path to the Mysterious Capital but instead propagate the winds of the Most High. Holding fast to the mind of unwavering practice, you illuminate the Daoist teachings; extending your hand to deliver all beings, you shatter the cages of the mundane. Even those withered and decayed at the root rely upon your nurturing power. In conduct, how dare [I] transgress? Should [I] forget the grace of your instruction, [I] would willingly endure the suffering of eternal submersion. Once liberated from the cycle of rebirth, [I] shall devote [myself] to cultivation with unwavering resolve, and when the primal destiny aligns, [I] shall repay [your kindness] with all [my] heart.

[I] humbly beseech you, Master, to open wide the gate of compassion and deign to perceive [my] sincerity. Though these words may seem but dust before you, [I] implore your merciful consideration. [My] heart is overwhelmed with longing for your grace.

Respectfully submitted.

Dated the ___ day of the ___ month, ___ year of the reign of ___.

---

**Petition Formula for Masters Presenting Disciples’ Requests**

[Full Title and Name of the Master]

The humble servant [Name] hereby reports: The disciple [Name] of [State, County, Township] has submitted a petition and presented the ritual tokens of transmission, prostrating before this servant to seek instruction in the *Northern Dipper Heavenly Heart Cessation Method*. [His] aspiration is to assist in the transformative work of Heaven, aid the state and pacify the people, heal the sick and relieve suffering, and sever all demonic influences.

Hereafter, [he] shall abide by this master’s guidance, daring not to transmit [the method] recklessly to unworthy persons nor wield it in defiance of the Great Dao. Should [he] ever violate this vow, [he] willingly accepts the annihilation of [his] own body and the punishment of [his] seven generations of ancestors.

[I] humbly request that this petition be submitted for approval, that [the method] may be transmitted in accordance with the established protocols.

Having carefully examined this disciple, [I] find [him] to be of pure and simple nature, steadfast in goodness and sincerity. [He] has ever revered the Lofty Perfected and constantly taken refuge in...

The disciple has expressed a resolve to aid in the salvation of the people, desiring to receive the transmission of the Orthodox Method, along with the Celestial Talismans of the Three Luminaries, the Northern Dipper, the Heavenly Valiant Great Sage True Warrior, and the Black-Killing Celestial Talisman. [I] humbly request to appoint this disciple, so-and-so, to the office of such-and-such, and to present for approval the seal pattern of the Northern Culmen Demon-Quelling Institute, along with the talismanic texts and oral instructions, that [he] may be duly ordained in accordance with the established protocols.

As [I] dare not presume to act unilaterally, [I] now respectfully submit this transcribed memorial for Your august perusal. Prostrate, [I] beseech the Great Emperor of Supreme Clarity, the Supreme Emperor of Highest Clarity, the Jade Emperor of Jade Clarity, to deign to issue a divine mandate, commanding the subordinate deities of Mount Tai to dispatch spirit talismans, soldiers, and officials to the disciple’s institute, that they may assist in the Daoist rites. [I] implore Your sagely compassion to permit the transmission of the method and the ordination in accordance with the Dharma, that karmic retribution may be fulfilled.

Presumptuously intruding upon Your celestial attention, [I] am truly awestruck and trembling. Bowing my head to the ground, [I] respectfully submit this memorial.

On the __ day of the __ month, in the __ year.

Memorial submitted by the Dharma Master [full title and name].

**Memorial Enclosure and Delivery Instructions**

**Seal of the Northern Culmen Demon-Quelling Institute**
To the Messenger of the Day, the Merit-Officer Attendant, on duty this __ day.

On the __ day of this month, at the __ hour, dispatch one memorial, sealed at the paper corners and doubly enclosed in a leather tube, to be delivered in full to the Celestial Pivot Institute for transmission.

Hereby instruct the Messenger of the Day, the Merit-Officer Attendant, on duty this __ day, to act in accordance with this directive, transmitting it swiftly and without delay. En route, no negligence, damage, smudging, or tampering with the seal shall be tolerated. Any failure to comply, or any carelessness, shall incur severe punishment without pardon.

Thus the directive is issued.

On the __ day of the __ month, at the __ hour.

**Judgment of the Supreme Heavenly Great Law Master, Director of the Northern Culmen Demon-Quelling Institute**

**Memorial to Mount Tai: Formula**

The Supreme Heavenly Controller of Demons, Rectifier of the Deviant, bearing full title and name, submits this memorial.

On the __ day of this month, according to the petition of disciple so-and-so of such-and-such ward in such-and-such prefecture and county, who has come to this Institute with sincere devotion, seeking transmission of the **Northern Culmen Heavenly Heart Orthodox Dao**, to assist in rectifying the deviant, expelling demons, aiding the transformative work of Heaven, relieving the suffering of the people, and severing all ghostly afflictions—with the vow to uphold and practice it:

The aforementioned disciple has already submitted a record of the matter, memorializing the **Supreme Emperor**, and has been enrolled and appointed to such-and-such office. He has been issued the talismanic texts, oral instructions, and the seal formula of the Demon-Quelling Institute, to be transmitted in accordance with the established protocol.

The transmission having been completed, this memorial is respectfully submitted to the **August and Benevolent Sagely Emperor of the Eastern Peak**, humbly beseeching His Sagely Perception to deign to issue directives, widely proclaiming to the **City God Kings** within the Three Realms, and to all subordinate orthodox Dao officials, past and present, as well as to the **Five Peaks and Four Waterways**, famous mountains and great rivers, palaces and temples, village altars, and all numinous spirits of mountains, rivers, and marshes, that they be forewarned and instructed.

Should the aforementioned disciple, having received the Dao and assumed office, hereafter treat illnesses or expel demons for others, they must assist the Daoist methods, apprehend ghostly afflictions, and not indulge in negligence or disrespect.

Furthermore, it is humbly requested that, in accordance with precedent, two mighty and awe-inspiring divine generals of vast spiritual power, along with one thousand divine soldiers, be dispatched to the newly ordained disciple’s institute to assist and oversee the Dao.

The **Seal of the Supreme Heavenly Great Law Master** and the personal signature-seal of the disciple have been issued for his use. The seal’s impression is appended herewith; may it be duly noted.

This seal’s script differs from all other talismanic seals, its characters refined to accord with the True Dao. Henceforth, should any memorials, petitions, or documents be submitted by this person, it is hoped that they will be verified by this seal to prevent forgery.

Respectfully submitted.

On the __ day of the __ month, [Name and Title] submits this memorial.

**Catalogue of Documents for Divine Bureaus**
For petitions to the Five Sacred Peaks’ Divine Masters, submit a *die* to this bureau.
For transmitting documents along the way, use an *yin tie* for local earth deities.
For the Underworld and Water Realms, as well as this bureau, use a *guan die*.
For transmitting texts via the Year-Star Merit Officers, use a *guan yin tie*.
For the Six Ding, City Gods, and Tai Sui, use *die* and *guan*.
For the local earth deity and household Controller of Fate, use an *yin tie* or *zhi zi* for directives.
For texts concerning sacred mountains and blessed lands, submit through the Six Jia and Six Ding.
For supervising spirits and ghosts, dispatch the Divine Generals of the Eastern Culmen.
For liberating the deceased, submit to the Hell Realm.
For chronic illnesses, submit to the Celestial Bureau’s records.
For merit-based rituals, submit to the Merit Assessment Bureau.
For matters concerning spirits and gods, submit to the Five Paths Central Bureau.
For major calamities, submit to the Life Verification Bureau.
For merit-based promotions, submit to the Controller of Fate’s Longevity and Prosperity Bureau.
For summoning the recently deceased, submit to Director Zhang’s Bureau.
For febrile illnesses resistant to sweating, submit to the Sweating Induction Bureau.
For sins borne in the yang realm, submit to the Transmission Clerk.
For febrile illnesses resistant to resolution, submit to the Sweating Induction Bureau.
For matters of lifespan, submit to the Life Registration Bureau.
For life liberation rituals, submit to the Life Bureau.
For the dead who remain uncooled after three days, submit to the Soul Return Bureau.
For pardons and amnesty, submit to the Underworld Bureau’s Judges.
For matters of Daoist scriptures, submit to the Ghost Immortal Bureau.
For lost property and textiles, submit to the Extortion Bureau.
For requesting additional years, submit to the Short Lifespan Bureau.
For posthumous merit offerings, submit to the Underworld’s Body Preservation Bureau.
For current merit calculations, submit to the Heavenly Path Bureau.
For annual illnesses, submit to the Epidemic Bureau.
For matters of life and death, submit to the Gaoli Central Bureau.
For mass casualties, submit to Director Li’s Bureau.
For matters concerning the deceased, submit to the Six Paths Internal Bureau.

When inscribing blessings or longevity, the Heavenly Bureau bestows fortune, and the Controller of Fate records prosperity. For matters such as longevity, wealth, and textiles, the gravity of the matter must be weighed, and the feasibility of the request assessed before proceeding.

For punishments in the Knife Mountain, Boiling Cauldron, Ash River, Sword Tree, Tongue Extraction, and Stone Mill Hells, the deceased’s conduct in life must first be examined before any action is taken. Additionally, the rank and status of the individual must be carefully considered to ensure the document is appropriate. Generally, civil officials of the seventh rank and above fall under the jurisdiction of Director Huo of the Celestial Bureau, while military officials of the seventh rank and above fall under Director Li of the Celestial Bureau.

**The Four Water Deities and Nine River Lords**
The Nine River Lords of the Yangtze, the Broad Source King of the Jiang River.
The Nine River Lords of the Yellow River, the Numinous Source King of the He River.
The Upper Minister of the Huai River, the Long Source King of the Huai River.
The Upper Minister of the Ji River, the Clear Source King of the Ji River.
